const CACHE = {
  set(k,v,ns='esv07'){try{localStorage.setItem(ns+'_'+k,JSON.stringify({v,t:Date.now()}));}catch(e){}},
  get(k,maxAge=3600000,ns='esv07'){
    try{const d=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(ns+'_'+k)||'null');
    if(!d)return null;if(Date.now()-d.t>maxAge)return null;return d.v;}catch{return null;}
  },
  getStale(k,ns='esv07'){try{const d=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(ns+'_'+k)||'null');return d?d.v:null;}catch{return null;}},
  del(k,ns='esv07'){localStorage.removeItem(ns+'_'+k);},
};

let caRes=null;
function showAlert(icCls,icType,title,msg,btns,hasInput,ph){
  return new Promise(res=>{
    caRes=res;
    $('caIcWrap').className='ca-ic '+icType;
    $('caIc').className=icCls;
    $('caTitle').textContent=title;
    $('caMsg').textContent=msg;
    const inp=$('caInp');
    if(hasInput){inp.style.display='block';inp.placeholder=ph||'';inp.value='';}
    else inp.style.display='none';
    const bb=$('caBtns');bb.innerHTML='';
    (btns||[{l:'OK',c:'ca-primary',v:'ok'}]).forEach(b=>{
      const btn=document.createElement('button');
      btn.className='ca-btn '+(b.c||'ca-primary');btn.textContent=b.l;
      btn.onclick=()=>{$('caBg').classList.remove('open');caRes({btn:b.v,input:hasInput?inp.value.trim():null});};
      bb.appendChild(btn);
    });
    $('caBg').classList.add('open');
  });
}
const caAlert=(t,m)=>showAlert('fas fa-info-circle','info',t,m,[{l:'OK',c:'ca-primary',v:'ok'}]);
const caConfirm=(t,m,d)=>showAlert('fas fa-question-circle','warn',t,m,[{l:d||'Haan',c:'ca-danger',v:'yes'},{l:'Nahi',c:'ca-ghost',v:'no'}]);
const caInput=(t,m,p)=>showAlert('fas fa-pen','info',t,m,[{l:'Save',c:'ca-primary',v:'save'},{l:'Cancel',c:'ca-ghost',v:'cancel'}],true,p);

function initApp(){
  loadTheme();
  // Nav lock karo
  document.querySelector('.nav')?.classList.add('auth-loading');
  // Login button hide karo jab tak auth resolve na ho
  if($('miLogin'))$('miLogin').style.display='none';
  // Hamesha content hide karo — cache se bhi direct na dikhe
  authResolved=false;
  ['contentHome','contentBooks','contentStore','contentChat','contentProfile'].forEach(id=>{
    const el=$(id);
    if(el)el.classList.remove('show');
  });
  ['skelHome','skelBooks','skelStore','skelChat','skelProfile'].forEach(id=>{
    const el=$(id);
    if(el)el.classList.remove('hide');
  });
  // Auth loading state — Premium button disable karo
  setAuthLoading(true);
  checkAuth();
  loadFromCache();
  loadStoreCats();
  loadStoreItems();
  setupLazyLoader();
  loadSubjects('science');
  
  renderPlans('science');
  renderHomeFeed();
  loadHomePYQ('science');
loadHomeBooks('science');
  renderStories();
  watchMembershipChanges(); 
  loadPYQs('science');
  loadBooks('science');
  loadAmazonItems();
  // Hamesha Home se shuru karo — saved tab restore nahi
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_activeTab','home');
  // Hide splash
  setTimeout(()=>$('splash').classList.add('hide'),2500);
  initWatermark();
  setTimeout(()=> checkProfileDeepLink(), 3000);
  
}

function setAuthLoading(loading){
  const memBtn=document.querySelector('.hdr-r .btn.bp');
  if(!memBtn)return;
  if(loading){
    memBtn.disabled=true;
    memBtn.style.opacity='0.5';
    memBtn.style.cursor='not-allowed';
  } else {
    memBtn.disabled=false;
    memBtn.style.opacity='1';
    memBtn.style.cursor='pointer';
  }
}
if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',initApp);}
else{initApp();}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   CACHE LOAD (instant display)
══════════════════════════════════════ */
function loadFromCache(){
  const cf=CACHE.getStale('feed');if(cf&&cf.length)renderPostCards(cf,$('homeFeed'));
  const cs=CACHE.getStale('store');if(cs&&cs.length){storeItems=cs;renderStore(storeItems);renderHomeFree();}
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   AUTH — FIXED (mobile redirect + desktop popup)
══════════════════════════════════════ */

function checkAuth(){
  auth.onAuthStateChanged(user=>{
    // Auth resolve — sab skeletons hide karo
    setAuthLoading(false);
    hideAllSkeletons();
    if(user){CU=user;onLogin(user);}
    else{CU=null;onLogout();}
  });
}

function hideAllSkeletons(){
  authResolved=true;
  // Nav unlock karo
  document.querySelector('.nav')?.classList.remove('auth-loading');
  // Login button ab show karo
  if(!CU) $('miLogin').style.display='flex';
  // Skeletons hide karo
  ['skelHome','skelBooks','skelStore','skelChat','skelProfile'].forEach(id=>{
    const el=$(id);
    if(el)el.classList.add('hide');
  });
  // Content fade in karo
  setTimeout(()=>{
    ['contentHome','contentBooks','contentStore','contentChat','contentProfile'].forEach(id=>{
      const el=$(id);
      if(el)el.classList.add('show');
    });
  },100);
  // Active page ka data load karo
  loadSubjects('science');
  loadStoreItems();
}

function onLogin(user){
  // Nav profile icon update
  const navProfile=document.querySelector('#nav-profile .ni-ic');
  if(navProfile){
    const av=user.photoURL||genAv(user.displayName||'U');
    navProfile.innerHTML=`<img src="${av}" style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:50%;object-fit:cover;border:2px solid var(--p);" onerror="this.src='${DAV}'">`;
  }
  // Update UI elements
  const av=user.photoURL||genAv(user.displayName||'U');
  $('profAv').src=av;
  $('editAv').src=av;
  $('refOvAv').src=av;
  $('profName').textContent=user.displayName||'User';
  $('profEmail').textContent=user.email||'';
  $('editName').value=user.displayName||'';
  $('editEmail').value=user.email||'';
  $('refOvName').textContent=user.displayName||'User';
  // Show/hide elements
  $('guestView').style.display='none';
  $('loggedView').style.display='block';
  $('editGuest').style.display='none';
  $('editForm').style.display='block';
  $('miEdit').style.opacity='1';
  $('miEdit').style.pointerEvents='auto';
  $('miLogout').style.display='flex';
  $('miLogin').style.display='none';
  $('chatLoginRequired').style.display='none';
  $('chatLoggedIn').style.display='block';
  updateThemeBtns();
  // Load GUN user data
  loadGunUser(user.uid, user);
  setOnlineStatus(user.uid, true);
  checkPayTimer(user.uid);
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_loggedIn','1');
}

function onLogout(){
  // Nav profile icon reset
  const navProfile=document.querySelector('#nav-profile .ni-ic');
  if(navProfile){
    navProfile.innerHTML=`<i class="fas fa-user"></i>`;
  }
  $('guestView').style.display='block';
  $('loggedView').style.display='none';
  $('editGuest').style.display='block';
  $('editForm').style.display='none';
  $('miEdit').style.opacity='0.4';
  $('miEdit').style.pointerEvents='none';
  $('miLogout').style.display='none';
  $('miLogin').style.display='none'; // Auth resolve hone tak hide
  $('miAdmin').style.display='none';
  $('miAiKey').style.display='none';
  $('chatLoginRequired').style.display='block';
  $('chatLoggedIn').style.display='none';
  GU={};
}

function loadGunUser(uid, fbUser) {
  const userRef = DB.users().get(uid);

  // 1. Pehle Cache se load karo (Instant UI)
  const cached = CACHE.getStale('user_' + uid);
  if (cached) { GU = { ...cached }; applyGU(); }

  // 2. LIVE LISTENER: Admin kuch bhi change karega, ye turant chalega
  userRef.on((data) => {
    if (!data || !data.uid) {
      // Agar user DB mein nahi hai, toh initialize karo
      const newUser = {
        uid: uid,
        name: fbUser.displayName || 'User',
        email: fbUser.email || '',
        photo: fbUser.photoURL || genAv(fbUser.displayName || 'U'),
        referralCode: makeRef(uid),
        membership: null,
        isAdmin: false,
        courses: 0,
        referrals: 0,
        earnings: 0,
        createdAt: Date.now()
      };
      userRef.put(newUser);
      return;
    }

    // --- REAL-TIME UPDATES ---
    const oldBanned = GU.isBanned;
    const oldMem = GU.membership;

    // Update global user object
    GU = { ...GU, ...data };
    CACHE.set('user_' + uid, GU);

    // A. BAN CHECK: Agar admin ne ban kiya toh turant overlay dikhao
    // A. BAN CHECK — Realtime (ban + unban dono)
    const nowBanned = (data.isBanned === true || data.isBanned === 'true');
    const wasBanned = (oldBanned === true || oldBanned === 'true');

    if (nowBanned) {
      // Ban hua — overlay dikhao, sab kuch lock karo
      $('banReason').textContent = data.banReason || 'Admin ne aapka account suspend kar diya hai.';
      $('banOv').classList.add('open');
      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    } else if (wasBanned && !nowBanned) {
      // UNBAN hua — overlay hatao, access wapas do
      $('banOv').classList.remove('open');
      document.body.style.overflow = '';
      toast('✅ Tumhara account restore ho gaya!');
    }

    // B. MEMBERSHIP CHECK: Agar membership status badla toh UI update karo
    if (data.membership !== oldMem) {
      console.log("Membership Updated:", data.membership);
      // Membership circle update
      if (data.membership) {
        DB.members().get(uid).put({ name: data.name, photo: data.photo, uid: uid, ts: Date.now() });
      } else {
        DB.members().get(uid).put(null);
      }
    }
    // UI Refresh
    applyGU();
    
    // Extra: Agar Membership mili hai toh content reload karo
    if(data.membership && (oldMem === null || oldMem === 'pending')) {
        loadSubjects(activeStream);
        renderStories();
    }
  });
}

function applyGU(){
  if(!GU||!GU.uid)return;
  // Header button update
  const memBtn=document.querySelector('.hdr-r .btn.bp');
  if(memBtn){
    if(GU.membership){
      memBtn.innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-crown"></i> You Are Member';
      memBtn.style.background='var(--g3)';
    } else {
      memBtn.innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-crown"></i> Premium';
      memBtn.style.background='';
    }
  }
  // Ban check
  // Ban check — unban bhi handle karo
  const isBannedNow = (GU.isBanned === true || GU.isBanned === 'true');
  if(isBannedNow){
    $('banReason').textContent = GU.banReason || 'Admin ne ban kar diya.';
    $('banOv').classList.add('open');
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
  } else {
    $('banOv').classList.remove('open');
    document.body.style.overflow = '';
  }
  // Admin check
  if(GU.isAdmin){
    $('miAdmin').style.display='flex';
    $('miAiKey').style.display='flex';
  }
  // Referral code
  const rc=GU.referralCode||makeRef(GU.uid);
  $('refDisp').textContent=rc;
  $('refOvCode').textContent=rc;
  // Stats
  $('psCourses').textContent=GU.courses||0;
  $('psRefs').textContent=GU.referrals||0;
  $('psEarnings').textContent='₹'+(GU.earnings||0);
  renderMemCard();
  checkWithdrawBtn();
  // Profile page mein bhi videos load karo
  loadProfileVideos();
  
  // Membership expiry check karo
if(GU.membership) checkMembershipExpiry(GU.uid);
// Stream profile render karo
renderStreamProfile();
// Watermark update karo
applyWatermark();
// Watermark update karo

// Privacy state apply karo
applyPrivacyState();
// My likes watch
watchMyLikes();

}

function renderMemCard(){
  const c = $('memCard');
  if(!c) return;

  if(!GU || !GU.membership){
    c.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mem-card none" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="openMem()">
        <i class="fas fa-lock" style="font-size:22px;"></i>
        <div style="flex:1;">
          <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;">Koi Membership Nahi</div>
          <div style="font-size:11px;opacity:.9;">Premium features unlock karein</div>
        </div>
        <button class="btn bsm" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.25);color:#fff;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.3);">Join Now</button>
      </div>`;
    return;
  }

  const planNames = {
    batch: 'Batch',
    pro: 'Pro',
    infinity: 'Infinity Pro'
  };
  const streamNames = {
    science: 'Science',
    arts: 'Arts',
    commerce: 'Commerce',
    '10th': '10th Class'
  };

  const plan = planNames[GU.membershipPlan || GU.membership] || (GU.membership || '').toUpperCase();
  const stream = streamNames[GU.membershipStream] || GU.membershipStream || '';
  const expTs = GU.membershipExpiry || 0;
  const days = expTs ? Math.ceil((expTs - Date.now()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) : null;
  const isExpiring = days !== null && days <= 7 && days > 0;
  const isExpired = days !== null && days <= 0;

  c.innerHTML = `
    <div class="mem-card active" style="background:${isExpired ? 'var(--g4)' : isExpiring ? 'linear-gradient(135deg,#f59e0b,#ef4444)' : 'var(--g3)'};">
      <div style="flex-shrink:0;">
        <i class="fas fa-crown" style="font-size:24px;"></i>
      </div>
      <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
        <div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:800;">${stream} — ${plan}</div>
        <div style="font-size:11px;opacity:.9;margin-top:2px;">
          ${isExpired
            ? '⚠️ Membership expire ho gayi — Renew karo'
            : isExpiring
              ? `⏰ Sirf ${days} din bacha hai!`
              : days !== null
                ? `Valid till: ${new Date(expTs).toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {day:'numeric', month:'short', year:'numeric'})}`
                : 'Active Membership ✓'
          }
        </div>
      </div>
      <i class="fas fa-${isExpired ? 'exclamation-circle' : 'check-circle'}" style="font-size:20px;flex-shrink:0;"></i>
    </div>

    <div style="display:flex;gap:9px;margin-top:10px;">
      <button onclick="navTo('books',$('nav-books'))" style="flex:1;padding:10px;border:none;border-radius:12px;background:var(--plight);color:var(--p);font-size:12px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--font);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:6px;">
        <i class="fas fa-book-open"></i> My Courses
      </button>
      <button onclick="openMem()" style="flex:1;padding:10px;border:1.5px solid var(--bd);border-radius:12px;background:var(--sur2);color:var(--txm);font-size:12px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--font);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:6px;">
        <i class="fas fa-sync-alt"></i> ${isExpired ? 'Renew' : 'Upgrade'}
      </button>
    </div>`;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════
// AB NEECHE doLogin function AAYEGA (jo pehle se hai)
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════
 
 
     
/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   LOGIN / LOGOUT — FIXED
══════════════════════════════════════ */
function doLogin(){
  closeMenu();
  const provider=new firebase.auth.GoogleAuthProvider();
  provider.addScope('email');
  provider.addScope('profile');
  auth.signInWithPopup(provider).catch(err=>{
    if(err.code==='auth/popup-blocked'){
      toast('Popup block hai — Browser mein allow karo');
    } else if(err.code==='auth/popup-closed-by-user'){
      toast('Login cancel ho gaya');
    } else {
      toast('Login fail: '+(err.message||'Try again'));
    }
  });
}

function doLogout(){
  closeMenu();
  caConfirm('Logout','Kya aap logout karna chahte hain?','Logout').then(r=>{
    if(r.btn==='yes'){
      if(CU)setOnlineStatus(CU.uid,false);
      auth.signOut().then(()=>{
        localStorage.removeItem('esv07_loggedIn');
        localStorage.setItem('esv07_activeTab','home');
        window.location.reload();
      });
    }
  });
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   NAVIGATION
══════════════════════════════════════ */
function navTo(page,el){
  // Saare overlays band karo
  ['memOv','payOv','refOv','smOv'].forEach(id=>closeOv(id));
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_activeTab',page);
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.ni').forEach(n=>n.classList.remove('active'));
  if(el)el.classList.add('active');
  $(page+'Page').classList.add('active');
  closeMenu();
  if(!authResolved)return;
  if(page==='books')loadSubjects();
  if(page==='store')loadStoreItems();
  if(page==='profile')renderMemCard();
  
}
function openSP(id){closeMenu();$(id).classList.add('open');}
function closeSP(id){$(id).classList.remove('open');}


function openAdminChat(){
  if(!CU){
    showLoginPrompt('Chat karne ke liye pehle Google se login karo. 💬', openAdminChat);
    return;
  }
  
  const msgs=$('chatMsgs');
  msgs.innerHTML='';
  
  // Cache se TURANT render karo
  const cached=CACHE.getStale('msgs_'+CU.uid);
  if(cached&&cached.length){
    chatAllLoaded=new Set();
    chatMsgsList=[];
    cached.sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts).forEach(m=>{
      if(!deletedMsgs.has(m.id)){
        chatAllLoaded.add(m.id);
        chatMsgsList.push(m);
        renderBubble(m);
      }
    });
    msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;
  }
  
  // GUN se naye messages sync karo
  if(chatGunOff){chatGunOff();chatGunOff=null;}
  const chatId=getChatId(CU.uid,ADMIN_UID);
  chatGunOff=DB.chats().get(chatId).map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.ts||deletedMsgs.has(key))return;
    if(chatAllLoaded.has(key)){
      if(data.seen){
        const si=document.getElementById('seen_'+key);
        if(si)si.innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-check-double" style="color:#7dd3fc;"></i>';
      }
      return;
    }
    chatAllLoaded.add(key);
    chatMsgsList.push({id:key,...data});
    chatMsgsList.sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts);
    CACHE.set('msgs_'+CU.uid,chatMsgsList.slice(-100));
    renderBubble({id:key,...data});
    if(data.senderId!==CU.uid&&!data.seen){
      DB.chats().get(chatId).get(key).get('seen').put(true);
    }
  });
  
  // Pehli baar koi message nahi toh welcome
  if(!cached||!cached.length){
    setTimeout(()=>{
      if(chatMsgsList.length===0)showWelcomeMsg();
    },1500);
  }
}
function openAdmin(){
  closeMenu();
  window.open('admin.html','_blank');
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   OVERLAYS
══════════════════════════════════════ */
let _scrollY=0;
function openOv(id){
  const el=$(id);
  if(!el)return;
  el.style.display='flex';   // ← YEH LINE ADD KARO
  el.classList.add('open');
  _scrollY=window.scrollY;
  document.body.style.overflow='hidden';
  document.body.style.top='-'+_scrollY+'px';
  document.body.style.position='fixed';
  document.body.style.width='100%';
}
function closeOv(id){
  const el=$(id);
  if(!el) return;
  el.classList.remove('open');
  el.style.display='none'; 

  // ✅ YEH ADD KARO — mem overlay band hone par watch band karo
  if(id==='memOv' && _promoWatchOff){
    try{_promoWatchOff();}catch(e){}
    _promoWatchOff=null;
  }

  const anyOpen=['memOv','payOv','refOv','smOv'].some(x=>$(x)?.classList.contains('open'));
  if(!anyOpen){
    document.body.style.overflow='';
    document.body.style.position='';
    document.body.style.width='';
    document.body.style.top='';
    window.scrollTo(0,_scrollY);
  }
}


// Promo data apply karna — UI update
function _applyPromoFromData(saved, timeLeftMs){
  promoApplied = true;
  promoDiscount = saved.discount;
  promoCode = saved.code;
  promoData = saved;

  const hoursLeft = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(timeLeftMs/(1000*60*60)));

  if($('promoInputWrap')) $('promoInputWrap').style.display = 'none';
  if($('promoSuccess')){
    $('promoSuccess').style.display = 'flex';
    $('promoSuccessMsg').textContent = `${saved.discount}% OFF Active Hai! 🎉`;
    $('promoSuccessDesc').textContent = `Code: ${saved.code} — ${hoursLeft}h baad expire hoga ⏰`;
  }

  renderPlans(activePlanStream);
  _watchActivePromo(saved.code);
}

// Background mein GUN se verify karo — admin ne delete kiya?
function _verifyPromoInBackground(code, timeLeftMs){
  DB_PROMO().get(code).once(codeData=>{
    if(!$('memOv').classList.contains('open')) return;

    // Admin ne delete kiya
    if(!codeData || codeData._deleted === true || !codeData.code){
      localStorage.removeItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid);
      DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').put(null);
      _clearPromoState();
      _showPromoMsg('❌ Admin ne yeh code remove kar diya — Dusra code try karo','err');
      renderPlans(activePlanStream);
      return;
    }

    // Limit full ho gaya check
    const usedCount = parseInt(codeData.usedCount)||0;
    const maxUse = parseInt(codeData.maxUse)||0;

    // Current user already used check
    const usedBy = codeData.usedBy || {};
    if(usedBy[CU.uid]){
      // User already used — but 24hr active period mein hai
      // UI mein warning nahi — allow karo purchase tak
      // (purchase ke time dobara block hoga)
    }

    if(maxUse > 0 && usedCount >= maxUse){
      localStorage.removeItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid);
      DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').put(null);
      _clearPromoState();
      _showPromoMsg('❌ Is code ki limit khatam ho gayi','err');
      renderPlans(activePlanStream);
    }
  });
}

// 24hr auto expiry timer — background mein chale
function _startPromoExpiryTimer(timeLeftMs){
  clearTimeout(window._promoExpTO);
  window._promoExpTO = setTimeout(()=>{
    if(!CU) return;
    localStorage.removeItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid);
    DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').put(null);
    _clearPromoState();
    renderPlans(activePlanStream);
    if($('memOv').classList.contains('open')){
      _showPromoMsg('⏰ Promo code expire ho gaya — 24 ghante ho gaye','warn');
    }
  }, timeLeftMs);
}


function closeOvClick(id,e){if(e.target===e.currentTarget)closeOv(id);}
// ══════════════════════════════════════
// MEMBERSHIP REQUEST SYSTEM
// ══════════════════════════════════════
function sendMemRequest(planKey, stream){
  if(!CU){ toast('Pehle login karo'); return; }
  
  // Check karo ki already request pending hai
  if(GU && GU.membership === 'pending'){
    toast('⏳ Tumhari request already pending hai — Admin approve karega'); 
    return;
  }

  const planNames = { batch:'Batch', pro:'Pro', infinity:'Infinity' };
  
  showAlert(
  'fas fa-paper-plane', 'warn',
  '📨 Request Bhejo',
  `${stream} — ${planNames[planKey]||planKey} membership ke liye request bhej rahe ho?`,
  [{l:'Haan, Bhejo', c:'ca-primary', v:'yes'}, {l:'Cancel', c:'ca-ghost', v:'no'}]
).then(r => {
  if(r.btn !== 'yes') return;
  const reqData = {
    uid: CU.uid,
    name: GU.name || GU.email || CU.email,
    email: CU.email,
    stream: stream,
    plan: planKey,
    status: 'pending',
    requestedAt: Date.now()
  };
  gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('memRequests').get(CU.uid).put(reqData);
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('membership').put('pending');
GU.membership = 'pending';
GU.membershipStream = stream;    // ← selPlan ki jagah direct 'stream' parameter use karo
GU.membershipPlan = planKey;
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('membershipStream').put(stream);
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('membershipPlan').put(planKey);
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('membershipRequestedAt').put(Date.now());
  GU.membership = 'pending';
  GU.membershipStream = stream;
  GU.membershipPlan = planKey;
  closeOv('memOv');
  toast('✅ Request bhej di! Admin jald approve karega 🎉');
});
}
function openMem(){
  closeMenu();

  _clearPromoState();
  renderPlans(activePlanStream);

  if(CU){
    const TWENTY_FOUR = 24*60*60*1000;
    let lsSaved = null;
    try{
      const raw = localStorage.getItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid);
      if(raw) lsSaved = JSON.parse(raw);
    }catch(e){}

    if(lsSaved && lsSaved.code && lsSaved.discount){
      const elapsed = Date.now() - (lsSaved.appliedAt||0);
      if(elapsed < TWENTY_FOUR){
        _applyPromoFromData(lsSaved, TWENTY_FOUR - elapsed);
        _verifyPromoInBackground(lsSaved.code, TWENTY_FOUR - elapsed);
      } else {
        localStorage.removeItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid);
        DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').put(null);
        _clearPromoState();
        renderPlans(activePlanStream);
        _showPromoMsg('⏰ Promo code 24 ghante baad expire ho gaya','warn');
      }
    } else {
      DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').once(saved=>{
        if(!saved || !saved.code || !saved.discount){
          _clearPromoState();
          renderPlans(activePlanStream);
          return;
        }
        const elapsed = Date.now() - (saved.appliedAt||0);
        if(elapsed > TWENTY_FOUR){
          DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').put(null);
          localStorage.removeItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid);
          _clearPromoState();
          _showPromoMsg('⏰ Promo code expire ho gaya — Naya code lagao','warn');
          renderPlans(activePlanStream);
        } else {
          localStorage.setItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid, JSON.stringify(saved));
          _applyPromoFromData(saved, TWENTY_FOUR - elapsed);
          _verifyPromoInBackground(saved.code, TWENTY_FOUR - elapsed);
        }
      });
    }
  }

  openOv('memOv');
}

/* ══ Realtime Admin Delete Watch ══ */
let _promoWatchOff = null;
function _watchActivePromo(code){
  if(_promoWatchOff){ try{_promoWatchOff();}catch(e){} _promoWatchOff=null; }
  _promoWatchOff = DB_PROMO().get(code).on(codeData=>{
    // Agar overlay open nahi toh kuch mat karo
    if(!$('memOv').classList.contains('open')) return;
    if(!codeData || codeData._deleted || !codeData.code){
      // Admin ne realtime delete kiya — turant invalidate karo
      DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').put(null);
      _clearPromoState();
      _showPromoMsg('❌ Admin ne yeh code remove kar diya — Dusra code try karo','err');
      renderPlans(activePlanStream);
    }
  });
}

/* ══ Helper: Promo state clear ══ */
function _clearPromoState(){
  promoApplied=false; promoDiscount=0; promoCode=''; promoData=null;
  if($('promoInp'))$('promoInp').value='';
  if($('promoInputWrap'))$('promoInputWrap').style.display='block';
  if($('promoSuccess'))$('promoSuccess').style.display='none';
}

/* ══ Helper: Promo message show ══ */
function _showPromoMsg(msg, type){
  const el = $('promoMsg');
  if(!el) return;
  if(type === 'hide' || !msg){
    el.style.display = 'none';
    return;
  }
  el.style.display = 'block';
  const colors = {
    info: 'var(--p)',
    warn: 'var(--warn)',
    err: 'var(--err)',
    ok: 'var(--ok)'
  };
  el.style.color = colors[type] || 'var(--txm)';
  const icons = {
    err: 'times-circle',
    ok: 'check-circle',
    warn: 'clock',
    info: 'spinner fa-spin'
  };
  el.innerHTML = `<i class="fas fa-${icons[type]||'info-circle'}"></i> ${msg}`;
  // Auto hide sirf success/error ke liye
  if(type === 'ok' || type === 'err'){
    setTimeout(() => { if(el) el.style.display = 'none'; }, 5000);
  }
}

function openRefOv(){closeMenu();if(!CU){toast('Pehle login karo!');return;}openOv('refOv');}
function closeSMOv(e){if(e.target===e.currentTarget)closeOv('smOv');}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   DARK MODE
══════════════════════════════════════ */
function toggleDark(){
  document.body.classList.toggle('dark');
  const d=document.body.classList.contains('dark');
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_theme',d?'dark':'light');
  $('darkTgl').classList.toggle('on',d);
  closeMenu();
}
function setTheme(t){
  if(t==='dark'){document.body.classList.add('dark');localStorage.setItem('esv07_theme','dark');}
  else if(t==='light'){document.body.classList.remove('dark');localStorage.setItem('esv07_theme','light');}
  else{document.body.classList.toggle('dark',window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme:dark)').matches);localStorage.removeItem('esv07_theme');}
  $('darkTgl').classList.toggle('on',document.body.classList.contains('dark'));
  updateThemeBtns();
  toast('Theme update hua! ✨');
}
function loadTheme(){
  const t=localStorage.getItem('esv07_theme');
  if(!t){
    // Pehli baar — hamesha light mode, device preference ignore karo
    document.body.classList.remove('dark');
    $('darkTgl').classList.remove('on');
    localStorage.setItem('esv07_theme','light');
  }
  else if(t==='dark'){document.body.classList.add('dark');$('darkTgl').classList.add('on');}
  updateThemeBtns();
}
function updateThemeBtns(){
  const t=localStorage.getItem('esv07_theme');
  ['tbL','tbD','tbDv'].forEach(id=>{if($(id))$(id).classList.remove('at');});
  if(t==='light'&&$('tbL'))$('tbL').classList.add('at');
  else if(t==='dark'&&$('tbD'))$('tbD').classList.add('at');
  else if(!t&&$('tbDv'))$('tbDv').classList.add('at');
}

}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   HOME FEED
══════════════════════════════════════ */
// Live user count — post likes mein realtime add hoga
window._liveUserCount = 0;
const _countedUsers = new Set();
DB.users().map().on((data, key) => {
  if(data && key && !_countedUsers.has(key)){
    _countedUsers.add(key);
    window._liveUserCount = _countedUsers.size;
    // Sab like buttons update karo
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-likeid]').forEach(el => {
      const base = parseInt(el.dataset.likebase || 0);
      const liked = parseInt(el.dataset.likedbonus || 0);
      el.textContent = fmtL(Math.max(16000, base) + window._liveUserCount + liked);
    });
  }
});


let _feedOff = null;
function renderHomeFeed(){
  const feed=$('homeFeed');
  // Cache se turant dikhao
  const cached=CACHE.getStale('feed');
  if(cached&&cached.length){
    renderPostCards(cached,feed);
  } else {
    feed.innerHTML='<div class="skel skel-card"></div><div class="skel skel-card"></div>';
  }
  // Live listener — pehla band karo
  if(_feedOff){try{_feedOff();}catch(e){} _feedOff=null;}
  const posts={};
  _feedOff = DB.posts().map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.title){
      // Delete hua — remove karo
      if(posts[key]){delete posts[key];_updateFeed();}
      return;
    }
    posts[key]={id:key,...data};
    _updateFeed();
  });
  function _updateFeed(){
    const list=Object.values(posts).sort((a,b)=>(b.ts||0)-(a.ts||0));
    if(!list.length)return;
    CACHE.set('feed',list);
    renderPostCards(list,feed);
  }
  // Fallback agar koi post nahi
  setTimeout(()=>{
    if(!Object.keys(posts).length){
      const c=CACHE.getStale('feed');
      if(c&&c.length)renderPostCards(c,feed);
      else renderDefaultFeed(feed);
    }
  },3000);
}

function renderDefaultFeed(feed){
  const posts=[
    {id:'p1',isAdmin:true,aName:'EduSagar Admin',aAv:genAv('Admin'),
     imgUrl:'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1503676260728-1c00da094a0b?w=800',
     title:'EduSagar mein Swagat! 🎉',body:'India ka best learning platform. Science, Arts, Commerce, 10th — sab ke liye premium content.',likes:12500,ts:Date.now()-7200000},
    {id:'p2',isAdmin:true,aName:'EduSagar Admin',aAv:genAv('Admin'),
     imgUrl:'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1588072432836-e10032774350?w=800',
     title:'New PYQ & Books Available! 📚',body:'Board exam ke liye Previous Year Questions aur new study books. Books tab mein dekho!',likes:5800,ts:Date.now()-18000000},
  ];
  CACHE.set('feed',posts);
  renderPostCards(posts,feed);
}
function renderPostCards(posts,feed){
  if(!posts||!posts.length){feed.innerHTML='';return;}

  // ── Carousel wrapper inject (sirf ek baar) ──
  feed.innerHTML=`
    <div id="postCarousel" style="position:relative;overflow:hidden;margin-bottom:13px;border-radius:var(--r);">
      <div id="postTrack" style="display:flex;transition:transform .5s cubic-bezier(.4,0,.2,1);will-change:transform;"></div>
      <div id="carDots" style="display:flex;justify-content:center;gap:6px;padding:10px 0 4px;"></div>
     
    </div>
  `;

  const track=$('postTrack');
  const dots=$('carDots');

  posts.forEach((p,idx)=>{
    const isYT=p.videoUrl&&(p.videoUrl.includes('youtube.com')||p.videoUrl.includes('youtu.be'));
    const isMp4=p.videoUrl&&!isYT;
    let ytId='';
    if(isYT){const m=p.videoUrl.match(/(?:v=|youtu\.be\/)([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{11})/);ytId=m?m[1]:'';}
    let mediaHtml='';
    if(isYT&&ytId){
      const startSec=p.ytStart||6;
      mediaHtml=`<div style="position:relative;width:100%;padding-top:56.25%;overflow:hidden;">
        <iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/${ytId}?start=${startSec}&autoplay=0&mute=1&loop=1&playlist=${ytId}&controls=1&rel=0"
          style="position:absolute;inset:0;width:100%;height:100%;border:none;"
          allow="autoplay;encrypted-media" allowfullscreen loading="lazy"></iframe></div>`;
    } else if(isMp4){
      mediaHtml=`<video src="${p.videoUrl}#t=${p.vidStart||6}" style="width:100%;max-height:200px;object-fit:cover;display:block;" muted playsinline loop preload="metadata" onclick="openPostVideo('${p.id}','${p.videoUrl||''}')"></video>`;
    } else if(p.imgUrl){
      mediaHtml=`<img src="${p.imgUrl}" style="width:100%;max-height:200px;object-fit:cover;display:block;border-radius:var(--r) var(--r) 0 0;" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.style.display='none'">`;
    }

    // Slide
    const slide=document.createElement('div');
    slide.style.cssText='min-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;';
    slide.innerHTML=`<div class="card" style="margin-bottom:0;border-radius:var(--r);">
      ${mediaHtml}
      <div class="pmeta">
        <img class="pav" src="${p.aAv||p.uAv||genAv('U')}" alt="" onerror="this.src='${DAV}'" loading="lazy">
        <div>
          <div class="pname">${esc(p.aName||p.uName||'User')}${(p.isAdmin||p.admin)?'<span class="abadge"><i class="fas fa-shield-alt"></i> Admin</span>':''}</div>
          <div class="ptime"><i class="fas fa-clock" style="margin-right:3px;font-size:9px;"></i>${relTime(p.ts||Date.now())}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="cbody"><h3>${esc(p.title)}</h3><p>${esc(p.body||'')}</p></div>
      <div class="cftr">
        <button class="lbtn ${likedSet.has(p.id)?'liked':''}" onclick="doLike(this,'${p.id}',${p.likes||0})">
  <i class="${likedSet.has(p.id)?'fas':'far'} fa-heart"></i>
  <span 
    data-likeid="${p.id}"
    data-likebase="${p.likes||0}"
    data-likedbonus="${likedSet.has(p.id)?1:0}">
    ${fmtL(Math.max(16000, p.likes||0) + (window._liveUserCount||0) + (likedSet.has(p.id)?1:0))}
  </span>
</button>
        ${(p.isAdmin||p.admin)?`<button class="btn bp bsm" onclick="openMem()"><i class="fas fa-lock"></i> Unlock Content</button>`:''}
      </div>
    </div>`;
    track.appendChild(slide);

    // Dot
    const dot=document.createElement('div');
    dot.id='dot_car_'+idx;
    dot.style.cssText=`width:${idx===0?'20px':'8px'};height:8px;border-radius:4px;background:${idx===0?'var(--p)':'var(--bd)'};transition:all .35s;cursor:pointer;`;
    dot.onclick=()=>carGoTo(idx);
    dots.appendChild(dot);
  });

  // State
  window._carIdx=0;
  window._carTotal=posts.length;

  // Touch/swipe
  let _tx=0,_dragging=false;
  const carousel=$('postCarousel');
  carousel.addEventListener('touchstart',e=>{_tx=e.touches[0].clientX;_dragging=true;},{ passive:true });
  carousel.addEventListener('touchend',e=>{
    if(!_dragging)return;_dragging=false;
    const dx=e.changedTouches[0].clientX-_tx;
    if(Math.abs(dx)>40)carMove(dx<0?1:-1);
  });

  // Auto-slide every 4s
  clearInterval(window._carTimer);
window._carTimer=setInterval(()=>{
  if(!document.hidden)carMove(1);
},12000);

  carGoTo(0);
}

window.carGoTo=function(idx){
  const total=window._carTotal||0;
  if(!total)return;
  idx=(idx+total)%total;
  window._carIdx=idx;
  const track=$('postTrack');
  if(track)track.style.transform=`translateX(-${idx*100}%)`;
  // Dots update
  for(let i=0;i<total;i++){
    const d=$('dot_car_'+i);
    if(d){
      d.style.width=i===idx?'20px':'8px';
      d.style.background=i===idx?'var(--p)':'var(--bd)';
    }
  }
};

window.carMove=function(dir){
  carGoTo((window._carIdx||0)+dir);
};

// MP4 post video fullscreen mein kholne ke liye
function openPostVideo(postId, url){
  if(!url) return;
  $('vidTitle').textContent = 'Video';
  $('vidFull').textContent = '';
  $('vidDesc').textContent = '';
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  ve.src = url;
  ve.currentTime = 0;
  openSP('vidSP');
  showVidLoader(true);
  ve.oncanplay = ()=>{ showVidLoader(false); ve.play(); adjustVideoSize(ve); };
  ve.onerror = ()=>{ showVidLoader(false); showVidError(); };
  loadRecommendedVideos('', {});
}
      

function doLike(btn,id,base){
  if(!CU){toast('Like karne ke liye login karo');return;}
  const ic=btn.querySelector('i'),sp=btn.querySelector('span');
  if(likedSet.has(id)){likedSet.delete(id);btn.classList.remove('liked');ic.className='far fa-heart';sp.textContent=fmtL(base);}
  else{likedSet.add(id);btn.classList.add('liked');ic.className='fas fa-heart';sp.textContent=fmtL(base+1);}
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_likes',JSON.stringify([...likedSet]));
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   STORIES
══════════════════════════════════════ */
let _storiesOff = null;
function renderStories(){
  const row=$('storiesRow');
  if(_storiesOff){try{_storiesOff();}catch(e){}_storiesOff=null;}
  const members={};
  const DEMO=[
    
  ];

  function getMergedList(){
    let list = Object.values(members);

    // ✅ KHUD KO HAMESHA ADD KARO — membership ho ya na ho
    if(CU){
      const selfExists = list.find(x=>x.uid===CU.uid);
      if(!selfExists){
        list.unshift({
          uid: CU.uid,
          name: GU.name || CU.displayName || 'You',
          photo: GU.photo || CU.photoURL || DAV
        });
      } else {
        // Self ko hamesha pehle rakho
        list = list.filter(x=>x.uid!==CU.uid);
        list.unshift(selfExists);
      }
    }

    // Agar sirf khud hai aur koi nahi — DEMO bhi add karo
    const realUsers = list.filter(x=>!x.uid?.startsWith('demo'));
    if(realUsers.length < 4){
      const demoFiltered = DEMO.filter(d=>!list.find(x=>x.uid===d.uid));
      list = [...list, ...demoFiltered];
    }

    return list.slice(0,24);
  }

  // Pehle turant render karo
  _renderStoriesRow(getMergedList(), row);

  // GUN se live updates
  _storiesOff = DB.members().map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.photo){delete members[key];}
    else members[key]={...data,uid:key};
    _renderStoriesRow(getMergedList(), row);
  });

  // ✅ Khud ka membership add karo GUN mein bhi
  if(CU && GU.membership){
    DB.members().get(CU.uid).put({
      name: GU.name||CU.displayName||'User',
      photo: GU.photo||CU.photoURL||DAV,
      uid: CU.uid,
      ts: Date.now()
    });
  }
}

function _renderStoriesRow(list, row){
  list=list.slice(-24);
  row.innerHTML=list.map(u=>`
    <div class="sit">
      <div class="sring"><img src="${u.photo||DAV}" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.src='${DAV}'"></div>
      <p>${esc((u.name||'User').substring(0,7))}</p>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function loadSubjects(str){
  if(str) activeStream = str;
  filterStreamTabs();
  const hasMem = GU.membership === 'active' && (GU.membershipStream === activeStream || GU.membership === 'infinity');

  const defaultList = SUBJECTS[activeStream] || SUBJECTS.science;
  const defaultItems = defaultList.map((s,i) => ({
    id: 'def_'+activeStream+'_'+i,
    name: s.n, icon: s.ic||s.icon,
    locked: s.l, isDefault: true,
    hasVideos: true
  }));
  renderSubjectGrid(defaultItems, hasMem);

  const gunSubjs = [];
  const gs = new Set();
  DB.subjects(activeStream).map().on((data,key) => {
    if(data && data.name && !gs.has(key)){
      gs.add(key);
      gunSubjs.push({id:key,...data});
    }
  });

  setTimeout(() => {
    const DB_SV = () => gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('subjectVideos').get(activeStream);
    const vidMap = {};
    DB_SV().map().once((data, key) => {
      if(data && key) vidMap[key] = data;
    });
    setTimeout(() => {
      const gunNames = new Set(gunSubjs.map(s => s.name));
      const mergedDefaults = defaultItems.filter(s => !gunNames.has(s.name));
      const allSubjs = [...gunSubjs, ...mergedDefaults];
      allSubjs.forEach(s => { s.hasVideos = true; });
      const hasMem2 = GU.membership === 'active' && (GU.membershipStream === activeStream || GU.membership === 'infinity');
      renderSubjectGrid(allSubjs, hasMem2);
    }, 400);
  }, 1200);

  loadPYQs(activeStream);
  loadBooks(activeStream);
  loadVideos(activeStream);
}
function filterStreamTabs(){
  const tabs = $('streamTabs');
  if(!tabs) return;

  // Infinity plan — sab streams dikhao
  if(GU.membership === 'infinity'){
    tabs.querySelectorAll('.tbtn').forEach(btn => {
      btn.style.display = 'flex';
    });
    return;
  }

  const mem = GU.membershipStream || GU.membership;

  if(!mem || mem === 'all'){
    tabs.querySelectorAll('.tbtn').forEach(btn => {
      btn.style.display = 'flex';
    });
    return;
  }

  const userStream = GU.membershipStream || mem;
  const streamMap = {
    'science':  'science',
    'arts':     'arts',
    'commerce': 'commerce',
    '10th':     '10th'
  };

  tabs.querySelectorAll('.tbtn').forEach(btn => {
    const btnText = btn.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();
    const matches = btnText === (streamMap[userStream] || userStream);
    if(matches){
      btn.style.display = 'flex';
      btn.classList.add('active');
    } else {
      btn.style.display = 'none';
      btn.classList.remove('active');
    }
  });

  if(userStream && userStream !== activeStream){
    activeStream = userStream;
  }
}

function renderSubjectGrid(subjects, hasMem){
  $('subjGrid').innerHTML = subjects.map(s => {
    const locked = (s.locked||s.l) && !hasMem;
    const hasPage = s.customPage && s.customPage.length > 10;
    const hasVideos = s.hasVideos || false;

    return `<div class="scard${locked?' locked':''}" style="position:relative;" onclick="openSubject('${s.id}', ${locked})">
      ${locked ? '<div class="lkbdg"><i class="fas fa-lock"></i></div>' : ''}
      ${hasPage ? '<div style="position:absolute;top:9px;left:9px;width:8px;height:8px;background:var(--ok);border-radius:50%;"></div>' : ''}
      ${hasVideos && !locked ? `
        <div onclick="event.stopPropagation();openSubjectVideos('${s.id}','${esc(s.name||s.n||'')}','${activeStream}')"
          style="position:absolute;top:8px;right:8px;width:28px;height:28px;background:var(--g1);color:#fff;border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer;box-shadow:0 2px 8px rgba(79,70,229,.35);z-index:2;"
          title="Videos dekho">
          <i class="fas fa-play-circle"></i>
        </div>
      ` : ''}
      <div class="sicon"><i class="${s.icon||s.ic||'fas fa-book'}"></i></div>
      <h4>${esc(s.name||s.n||'Subject')}</h4>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');

  window._subjectsData = subjects;
}
// Store listeners for cleanup
const subjectListeners = {};

function cleanupSubjectListeners(subjectId, stream) {
  const key = stream + '_' + subjectId;
  if(subjectListeners[key]) {
    const listeners = subjectListeners[key];
    if(listeners.chapters) {
      listeners.chapters.off();
    }
    if(listeners.sets) {
      listeners.sets.off();
    }
    delete subjectListeners[key];
  }
}
function openSubject(id,locked){
  if(locked){openMem();return;}
  const s=window._subjectsData?.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(!s)return;
  openSubjectMILPage(s.id, s.name, s.icon||s.ic);
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   SUBJECT PAGE SYSTEM — MIL ODIA Style
══════════════════════════════════════ */
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════
// STEP 1: YEH POORA FUNCTION DHUNDO AUR DELETE KARO:
// function openSubjectMILPage(subjectId, subjectName, icon){ ... }
// PHIR NEECHE WALA PASTE KARO
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════

function openSubjectMILPage(subjectId, subjectName, icon){
  window._currentOpenSubjectId = subjectId;
$('customPageTitle').textContent = subjectName;
openSP('customPageSP');
const body = $('customPageBody');
body.style.cssText = 'padding:0;background:var(--bg);overflow-y:auto;';
body.innerHTML = _subjChapterLoader();
const currentStream = activeStream;
const cacheKey = 'milpage2_' + currentStream + '_' + subjectId;
const listenerKey = currentStream + '_' + subjectId;
// ✅ FIX 1: पुरानी listeners को साफ करो
cleanupSubjectListeners(subjectId, currentStream);
try {
  const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(cacheKey) || 'null');
  // ✅ Cache सिर्फ तभी दिखाओ अगर current subject वही है
  if(cached && window._currentOpenSubjectId === subjectId) {
    _renderChapterListPage(body, cached, subjectId, subjectName, icon, currentStream);
  }
} catch(e){}
const pageData = { chapters:{}, sets:{} };
const DB_MIL = () => gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('milPages').get(currentStream).get(subjectId);
// ✅ FIX 2: Listeners को store करो
const chaptersListener = DB_MIL().get('chapters').map().on((data, key) => {
  // ✅ अगर दूसरा subject खुल गया तो इस data को ignore करो
  if(window._currentOpenSubjectId !== subjectId) return;
  
  if(!data || data._del) delete pageData.chapters[key];
  else pageData.chapters[key] = { id: key, ...data };
  
  clearTimeout(window['_milTO2_'+subjectId+'_'+currentStream]);
  window['_milTO2_'+subjectId+'_'+currentStream] = setTimeout(() => {
    // ✅ Render करने से पहले फिर से check करो
    if(window._currentOpenSubjectId === subjectId) {
      try { localStorage.setItem(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(pageData)); } catch(e){}
      _renderChapterListPage(body, pageData, subjectId, subjectName, icon, currentStream);
    }
  }, 400);
});
const setsListener = DB_MIL().get('sets').map().on((data, key) => {
  // ✅ अगर दूसरा subject खुल गया तो इस data को ignore करो
  if(window._currentOpenSubjectId !== subjectId) return;
  
  if(!data || data._del) delete pageData.sets[key];
  else pageData.sets[key] = { id: key, ...data };
  
  clearTimeout(window['_milTO2_'+subjectId+'_'+currentStream]);
  window['_milTO2_'+subjectId+'_'+currentStream] = setTimeout(() => {
    // ✅ Render करने से पहले फिर से check करो
    if(window._currentOpenSubjectId === subjectId) {
      try { localStorage.setItem(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(pageData)); } catch(e){}
      _renderChapterListPage(body, pageData, subjectId, subjectName, icon, currentStream);
    }
  }, 400);
});
// ✅ FIX 3: Listeners को globally store करो
subjectListeners[listenerKey] = {
chapters: chaptersListener,
sets: setsListener
};
setTimeout(() => {
const hasCh = Object.keys(pageData.chapters).length;
const hasSt = Object.keys(pageData.sets).length;
if(!hasCh && !hasSt) _renderChapterListPage(body, pageData, subjectId, subjectName, icon, currentStream);
}, 3500);
}


/* ── Loader HTML ── */
function _subjChapterLoader(){
  return `<div style="padding:13px;">
    <div style="height:80px;border-radius:var(--r);margin-bottom:16px;background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;"></div>
    <div style="height:22px;width:40%;border-radius:20px;margin-bottom:14px;background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;"></div>
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px;margin-bottom:14px;">
      ${[1,2,3,4].map(()=>`<div style="height:110px;border-radius:var(--r2);background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;"></div>`).join('')}
    </div>
    <div style="height:130px;border-radius:var(--r);background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;"></div>
  </div>`;
}

/* ── Chapter List Page — FIX 4: stream parameter add kiya ── */
function _renderChapterListPage(body, pageData, subjectId, subjectName, icon, streamOverride){
  GU && GU.membership === 'active';
  const chapters = Object.values(pageData.chapters || {})
    .filter(c => c && c.name)
    .sort((a,b) => (a.order||0)-(b.order||0));
  const sets = Object.values(pageData.sets || {})
    .filter(s => s && s.name)
    .sort((a,b) => (a.order||0)-(b.order||0));
  const useStream = streamOverride || activeStream;

  let html = `
  <div style="padding:13px 13px 60px;">
    <!-- HERO -->
    <div style="background:var(--g1);border-radius:var(--r);padding:20px 18px;margin-bottom:16px;color:#fff;position:relative;overflow:hidden;">
      <div style="position:absolute;top:-25px;right:-25px;width:100px;height:100px;border-radius:50%;background:rgba(255,255,255,.07);"></div>
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:13px;position:relative;z-index:1;">
        <div style="width:50px;height:50px;border-radius:14px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:22px;flex-shrink:0;">
          <i class="${icon||'fas fa-book'}"></i>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;opacity:.8;letter-spacing:1px;text-transform:uppercase;font-weight:600;">+2 Second Year · ${useStream.toUpperCase()}</div>
          <div style="font-family:'Baloo 2',cursive;font-size:19px;font-weight:800;">${esc(subjectName)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- CHAPTERS -->
    ${chapters.length ? `
      <div style="margin-bottom:18px;">
        <div style="font-family:'Baloo 2',cursive;font-size:16px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:12px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;">
          <i class="fas fa-book-open" style="color:var(--p);font-size:14px;"></i> Chapters
        </div>
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px;">
          ${chapters.map((ch, idx) => {
            const locked = ch.isPaid && !hasMem;
            const isOdd = chapters.length % 2 !== 0 && idx === chapters.length - 1;
            return `
            <div style="background:var(--sur);border:1.5px solid ${locked?'var(--bd)':'var(--bds)'};border-radius:var(--r2);padding:14px 12px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .22s;position:relative;${isOdd?'grid-column:1/-1;':''}"
            onclick="${locked ? 'openMem()' : `_openChapterContent('${subjectId}','${ch.id}','${esc(ch.name)}','${useStream}')`}"
            onmouseover="this.style.transform='translateY(-2px)';this.style.boxShadow='0 6px 20px rgba(79,70,229,.15)'"
            onmouseout="this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow=''">
              <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:8px;">
                <span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:700;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;background:${locked?'rgba(239,68,68,.1)':'rgba(16,185,129,.12)'};color:${locked?'var(--err)':'var(--ok)'};display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">
                  <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'unlock'}"></i>${locked?'Premium':'Free'}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;line-height:1.45;margin-bottom:10px;color:var(--tx);">${esc(ch.name)}</div>
              <div style="display:flex;gap:4px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
                <span style="font-size:9px;background:var(--plight);color:var(--p);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">MCQ</span>
                ${ch.has2mark?'<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(249,115,22,.1);color:#f97316;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">2 Mark</span>':''}
                ${ch.has3mark?'<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(245,158,11,.1);color:var(--warn);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">3 Mark</span>':''}
                ${ch.hasLong?'<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(239,68,68,.1);color:var(--err);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">Long Q</span>':''}
              </div>
            </div>`;
          }).join('')}
        </div>
      </div>
    ` : ''}

    <!-- SETS -->
    ${sets.length ? `
      <div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);padding:16px;margin-bottom:14px;">
        <div style="font-family:'Baloo 2',cursive;font-size:15px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:14px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;">
          <i class="fas fa-tasks" style="color:var(--ok);font-size:13px;"></i> Practice Sets
        </div>
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:9px;">
          ${sets.map((s, idx) => {
            const locked = s.isPaid && !hasMem;
            const isOdd = sets.length % 2 !== 0 && idx === sets.length - 1;
            return `
            <div style="background:${locked?'var(--sur2)':'var(--plight)'};border:1.5px solid ${locked?'var(--bd)':'var(--bds)'};border-radius:10px;padding:13px 10px;text-align:center;cursor:pointer;transition:all .22s;${isOdd?'grid-column:1/-1;':''}"
            onclick="${locked ? 'openMem()' : `_openSetContent('${subjectId}','${s.id}','${esc(s.name)}','${useStream}')`}"
            onmouseover="if(!${locked}){this.style.background='var(--p)';this.style.color='#fff';this.style.borderColor='var(--p)';}"
            onmouseout="this.style.background='${locked?'var(--sur2)':'var(--plight)'}';this.style.color='';this.style.borderColor='${locked?'var(--bd)':'var(--bds)'}';this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow='';">
              ${locked ? '<i class="fas fa-lock" style="display:block;margin-bottom:5px;font-size:14px;color:var(--err);opacity:.7;"></i>' : ''}
              <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:${locked?'var(--txm)':'var(--p)'};">${esc(s.name)}</div>
              ${!locked ? '<div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--txm);margin-top:4px;">MCQ Practice</div>' : ''}
            </div>`;
          }).join('')}
        </div>
      </div>
    ` : ''}

    ${!chapters.length && !sets.length ? `
      <div style="text-align:center;padding:50px 20px;color:var(--txm);">
        <i class="fas fa-inbox" style="font-size:36px;display:block;margin-bottom:12px;opacity:.3;"></i>
        <p style="font-size:13px;">Admin ne abhi content add nahi kiya</p>
      </div>
    ` : ''}

    <div style="text-align:center;padding:22px 0 8px;color:var(--txl);font-size:10px;border-top:1px solid var(--bd);margin-top:10px;">
      <i class="fas fa-copyright" style="font-size:9px;"></i> 2026 EduSagar
    </div>
  </div>`;

  body.innerHTML = html;
}

function _openChapterContent(subjectId, chapterId, chapterName, streamOverride){
  const useStream = streamOverride || activeStream;
  $('customSubPageTitle').textContent = chapterName;
  const body = $('customSubPageBody');
  body.style.cssText = 'padding:0;background:var(--bg);overflow-y:auto;display:flex;flex-direction:column;';
  
  // ✅ FIX 1: पुराने listener को बंद करो
  if(currentChapterListener) {
    currentChapterListener.off();
    currentChapterListener = null;
  }
  
  // Loader dikhao
  body.innerHTML = `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;height:200px;"><div style="width:40px;height:40px;border:3px solid var(--bd);border-top-color:var(--p);border-radius:50%;animation:sp .9s linear infinite;"></div></div>`;
  openSP('customSubPageSP');

  let isDataLoaded = false; // Flag to prevent overwriting

  const DB_CH = () => gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('milPages').get(useStream).get(subjectId).get('chapters').get(chapterId);

  // ✅ FIX 2: .once() use करो बजाय .on() के
  currentChapterListener = DB_CH().once(data => {
    if(data && (data.mcqHtml || data.mark2Url || data.mark3Url || data.longqUrl || data.name)) {
      isDataLoaded = true;
      _renderChapterContentPage(body, data, subjectId, chapterId, chapterName, false, useStream);
    }
  });

  // Fallback: Agar 5 second tak kuch nahi mila tabhi empty dikhao
  setTimeout(() => {
    if(!isDataLoaded) {
      _renderChapterContentPage(body, {}, subjectId, chapterId, chapterName, false, useStream);
      // ✅ FIX 3: Timeout के बाद listener को बंद करो
      if(currentChapterListener) {
        currentChapterListener.off();
        currentChapterListener = null;
      }
    }
  }, 5000);
}

/* ── FIX 4: stream parameter added ── */
function _openSetContent(subjectId, setId, setName, streamOverride){
  const useStream = streamOverride || activeStream;
  $('customSubPageTitle').textContent = setName;
  const body = $('customSubPageBody');
  body.style.cssText = 'padding:0;background:var(--bg);overflow-y:auto;display:flex;flex-direction:column;';
  
  // ✅ FIX 1: पुराने listener को बंद करो
  if(currentSetListener) {
    currentSetListener.off();
    currentSetListener = null;
  }
  
  body.innerHTML = `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;height:200px;"><div style="width:40px;height:40px;border:3px solid var(--bd);border-top-color:var(--p);border-radius:50%;animation:sp .9s linear infinite;"></div></div>`;
  openSP('customSubPageSP');

  let isSetLoaded = false;

  const DB_SET = () => gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('milPages').get(useStream).get(subjectId).get('sets').get(setId);

  // ✅ FIX 2: .once() use करो बजाय .on() के
  currentSetListener = DB_SET().once(data => {
    if(data && (data.mcqHtml || data.name)) {
      isSetLoaded = true;
      _renderChapterContentPage(body, data, subjectId, setId, setName, true, useStream);
    }
  });
  
  setTimeout(() => {
    if(!isSetLoaded) {
      _renderChapterContentPage(body, {}, subjectId, setId, setName, true, useStream);
      // ✅ FIX 3: Timeout के बाद listener को बंद करो
      if(currentSetListener) {
        currentSetListener.off();
        currentSetListener = null;
      }
    }
  }, 5000);
}

/* ── FIX 2+3: Main Chapter Content Renderer ── */
function _renderChapterContentPage(body, data, subjectId, chId, chName, isSet, streamOverride){
  const useStream = streamOverride || activeStream;
  const mcqHtml = data.mcqHtml || '';

  // ══ FIX 5 (user side): Multiple PDFs support ══
  // Old single URL + new array format dono support
  const mark2List = _parsePDFList(data, 'mark2');
  const mark3List = _parsePDFList(data, 'mark3');
  const longQList = _parsePDFList(data, 'longq');

  const hasMCQ = !!mcqHtml;
  const has2Mark = mark2List.length > 0;
  const has3Mark = mark3List.length > 0;
  const hasLong = longQList.length > 0;

  // Sections
  const sections = isSet
    ? [{ id:'mcq', label:'MCQ', icon:'fas fa-pen', color:'var(--p)', hasCon: hasMCQ, isMCQ: true }]
    : [
        { id:'mcq',   label:'MCQ',           icon:'fas fa-pen',   color:'var(--p)',    hasCon: hasMCQ,  isMCQ: true },
        { id:'mark2', label:'2 Mark',         icon:'fas fa-star',  color:'#f97316',     hasCon: has2Mark, isPDF:true, pdfList: mark2List },
        { id:'mark3', label:'3 Mark',         icon:'fas fa-star',  color:'var(--warn)', hasCon: has3Mark, isPDF:true, pdfList: mark3List },
        { id:'longq', label:'Long Question',  icon:'fas fa-fire',  color:'var(--err)',  hasCon: hasLong,  isPDF:true, pdfList: longQList },
      ];

  let html = `
  <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;height:100%;min-height:100%;">
    <!-- SECTION TABS -->
    <div id="chSecTabs" style="display:flex;overflow-x:auto;scrollbar-width:none;background:var(--sur);border-bottom:1.5px solid var(--bd);flex-shrink:0;position:sticky;top:0;z-index:20;box-shadow:0 2px 8px rgba(79,70,229,.06);">
      ${sections.map((s,i) => `
        <div onclick="_switchChSec('${s.id}')" id="chtab_${s.id}"
          style="flex-shrink:0;padding:12px 16px;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;white-space:nowrap;border-bottom:3px solid ${i===0?s.color:'transparent'};color:${i===0?s.color:'var(--txm)'};transition:all .2s;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;">
          <i class="${s.icon}"></i>${s.label}
        </div>
      `).join('')}
    </div>

    <!-- SECTION CONTENT -->
    <div id="chSecContent" style="flex:1;overflow-y:auto;min-height:0;">
      ${sections.map((s,i) => `
        <div id="chsec_${s.id}" style="display:${i===0?'flex':'none'};flex-direction:column;min-height:100%;">
          ${_renderSectionContent(s, chName)}
        </div>
      `).join('')}
    </div>
  </div>`;

  body.innerHTML = html;
  window._chSecCurrent = sections[0]?.id || 'mcq';
  window._chSecSections = sections;

  // ══ FIX 2: MCQ HTML inject AFTER DOM ready ══
  if(hasMCQ){
    setTimeout(() => _injectMCQHtml(mcqHtml, 'mcq'), 200);
  }
}

/* ── Helper: Multiple PDFs parse karo ── */
function _parsePDFList(data, type){
  const list = [];
  // New format: mark2_0, mark2_1, mark2_2 ... (unlimited)
  for(let i = 0; i < 50; i++){
    const url = data[type+'_'+i+'_url'] || data[type+'Url_'+i];
    const title = data[type+'_'+i+'_title'] || data[type+'Title_'+i] || (type==='mark2'?'2 Mark':type==='mark3'?'3 Mark':'Long Q')+' '+(i+1);
    if(url) list.push({url, title});
  }
  // Old single URL format bhi support karo
  if(list.length === 0){
    const singleUrl = data[type+'Url'] || data[type==='mark2'?'mark2Url':type==='mark3'?'mark3Url':'longQUrl'];
    const singleTitle = data[type+'Title'] || data[type==='mark2'?'mark2Title':type==='mark3'?'mark3Title':'longQTitle'] || (type==='mark2'?'2 Mark Questions':type==='mark3'?'3 Mark Questions':'Long Questions');
    if(singleUrl) list.push({url: singleUrl, title: singleTitle});
  }
  return list;
}

/* ── FIX 3: Section Content Renderer — z-index fix ── */
function _renderSectionContent(sec, chName){
  if(sec.isMCQ){
    if(!sec.hasCon){
      return `
        <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex:1;padding:40px 20px;text-align:center;color:var(--txm);">
          <i class="fas fa-pen" style="font-size:36px;display:block;margin-bottom:12px;opacity:.25;"></i>
          <div style="font-family:'Baloo 2',cursive;font-size:17px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:5px;">Coming Soon</div>
          <p style="font-size:12px;">Admin jald hi MCQ add karega</p>
        </div>`;
    }
    return `
      <!-- MCQ HEADER BAR -->
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;padding:10px 13px;background:var(--sur);border-bottom:1px solid var(--bd);flex-shrink:0;">
        <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:var(--p);display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;">
          <i class="fas fa-pen"></i> MCQ Questions
        </div>
        <button onclick="_toggleMCQFullscreen()" id="mcqFsBtn"
          style="background:var(--plight);color:var(--p);border:none;border-radius:8px;padding:6px 12px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;">
          <i class="fas fa-expand"></i> Full Screen
        </button>
      </div>
      <!-- MCQ IFRAME — FIX 2: srcdoc blank, inject baad mein ── -->
      <div id="mcqIframeWrap" style="flex:1;overflow:hidden;display:flex;flex-direction:column;position:relative;">
        <iframe id="mcqFrame_mcq"
          style="flex:1;border:none;width:100%;height:100%;min-height:calc(100vh - 130px);"
          sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-forms allow-popups">
        </iframe>
      </div>`;
  }

  if(sec.isPDF){
    if(!sec.hasCon){
      return `
        <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex:1;padding:40px 20px;text-align:center;color:var(--txm);">
          <i class="fas fa-file-pdf" style="font-size:36px;display:block;margin-bottom:12px;opacity:.25;"></i>
          <div style="font-family:'Baloo 2',cursive;font-size:17px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:5px;">Coming Soon</div>
          <p style="font-size:12px;">Admin jald hi add karega</p>
        </div>`;
    }

    // ══ FIX 3: Multiple PDFs + Z-index fix ══
    // Side by side 2 columns grid
    return `
      <div style="padding:13px;">
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px;">
          ${sec.pdfList.map((pdf, idx) => _pdfCard(pdf.title, pdf.url, sec.color)).join('')}
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }
  return '';
}

/* ── FIX 2: MCQ HTML inject — proper srcdoc ── */
function _injectMCQHtml(mcqHtml, secId){
  const frame = document.getElementById('mcqFrame_'+secId);
  if(!frame) return;

  const isDark = document.body.classList.contains('dark');

  // Complete CSS variables inject karo
  const css = `<style>
    *{box-sizing:border-box;margin:0;padding:0;}
    :root{
      --p:#4f46e5;--ps:#6366f1;--plight:rgba(79,70,229,.12);
      --s:#f43f5e;--ok:#10b981;--warn:#f59e0b;--err:#ef4444;
      --bg:${isDark?'#0b0a1e':'#f1f2ff'};
      --sur:${isDark?'#141330':'#ffffff'};
      --sur2:${isDark?'#1a1836':'#f8f8ff'};
      --sur3:${isDark?'#201e40':'#eef0ff'};
      --tx:${isDark?'#eeeeff':'#0f0d2e'};
      --txm:${isDark?'#8885b0':'#6b7194'};
      --bd:${isDark?'#2a2850':'#e4e6f8'};
      --r:18px;--r2:12px;--r3:8px;
    }
    html,body{height:100%;overflow-y:auto;background:var(--bg);color:var(--tx);}
    body{font-family:'DM Sans',sans-serif;padding:12px;}
    /* Common MCQ styles */
    .mcq-question{background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r2);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);padding:14px;margin-bottom:12px;}
    .mcq-option{padding:9px 13px;border:1.5px solid var(--bd);border-radius:9px;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer;margin-bottom:6px;transition:all .2s;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:9px;}
    .mcq-option:hover{border-color:var(--p);background:var(--plight);}
    .mcq-option.correct{border-color:var(--ok)!important;background:rgba(16,185,129,.12)!important;color:var(--ok)!important;}
    .mcq-option.wrong{border-color:var(--err)!important;background:rgba(239,68,68,.08)!important;color:var(--err)!important;}
    button{font-family:'DM Sans',sans-serif;cursor:pointer;}
  </style>
  <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Baloo+2:wght@400;600;700;800&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.5.0/css/all.min.css">`;

  // Poora srcdoc set karo
  frame.srcdoc = `<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1">${css}</head><body>${mcqHtml}</body></html>`;
}

/* ── FIX 3: PDF Card — Z-index fix ── */
function _pdfCard(title, url, accentColor){
  if(!url) return `
    <div style="text-align:center;padding:24px;color:var(--txm);background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r2);border:1.5px dashed var(--bd);">
      <i class="fas fa-file-pdf" style="font-size:24px;display:block;margin-bottom:8px;opacity:.3;"></i>
      <div style="font-size:11px;">Coming Soon</div>
    </div>`;

  const color = accentColor || '#ef4444';

  // ══ FIX 3: openPDFViewer directly — no z-index issue ══
  // String escaping handle karo
  const safeTitle = (title||'PDF').replace(/'/g, "\\'").replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
  const safeUrl = (url||'').replace(/'/g, "\\'");

  return `
    <div onclick="openPDFViewer('${safeTitle}','','${safeUrl}','${safeUrl}')"
      style="
        background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r2);
        border:1.5px solid var(--bd);
        padding:14px;text-align:center;
        cursor:pointer;transition:all .22s;
        display:flex;flex-direction:column;
        align-items:center;gap:8px;
      "
      onmouseover="this.style.transform='translateY(-2px)';this.style.boxShadow='0 6px 20px rgba(79,70,229,.13)'"
      onmouseout="this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow=''">
      <div style="width:46px;height:46px;border-radius:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#ef4444,#f97316);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px;color:#fff;">
        <i class="fas fa-file-pdf"></i>
      </div>
      <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx);line-height:1.4;word-break:break-word;">${esc(title||'PDF')}</div>
      <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--p);font-weight:600;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">
        <i class="fas fa-eye"></i> Open PDF
      </div>
    </div>`;
}

/* ── Section Tab Switch ── */
function _switchChSec(secId){
  if(!window._chSecSections) return;
  const sec = window._chSecSections.find(s => s.id === secId);
  if(!sec) return;
  window._chSecCurrent = secId;

  window._chSecSections.forEach(s => {
    const el = document.getElementById('chsec_'+s.id);
    if(el) el.style.display = 'none';
    const tab = document.getElementById('chtab_'+s.id);
    if(tab){ tab.style.borderBottomColor='transparent'; tab.style.color='var(--txm)'; }
  });

  const active = document.getElementById('chsec_'+secId);
  if(active) active.style.display = 'flex';
  const activeTab = document.getElementById('chtab_'+secId);
  if(activeTab){ activeTab.style.borderBottomColor=sec.color; activeTab.style.color=sec.color; }
}

/* ── MCQ Fullscreen Toggle ── */
let _mcqIsFS = false;
function _toggleMCQFullscreen(){
  const wrap = document.getElementById('mcqIframeWrap');
  const btn = document.getElementById('mcqFsBtn');
  const tabsEl = document.getElementById('chSecTabs');
  const spHdr = document.querySelector('#customSubPageSP .sp-hdr');

  if(!_mcqIsFS){
    _mcqIsFS = true;
    if(wrap){
      wrap.style.cssText = `
        position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:9999999;
        background:var(--bg);display:flex;flex-direction:column;
      `;
    }
    if(spHdr) spHdr.style.display = 'none';
    if(tabsEl) tabsEl.style.display = 'none';

    let closeBtn = document.getElementById('mcqFsClose');
    if(!closeBtn){
      closeBtn = document.createElement('button');
      closeBtn.id = 'mcqFsClose';
      closeBtn.onclick = _toggleMCQFullscreen;
      closeBtn.style.cssText = `
        position:absolute;top:10px;right:10px;z-index:10;
        background:rgba(79,70,229,.9);color:#fff;border:none;
        border-radius:10px;padding:8px 14px;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;
        cursor:pointer;font-family:'DM Sans',sans-serif;
        display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;
        box-shadow:0 4px 14px rgba(79,70,229,.3);
      `;
      closeBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-compress"></i> Exit';
      if(wrap) wrap.appendChild(closeBtn);
    }
    closeBtn.style.display = 'flex';
    if(btn) btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-compress"></i> Exit';

    try{ screen.orientation.lock('portrait-primary').catch(()=>{}); }catch(e){}

  } else {
    _mcqIsFS = false;
    if(wrap){
      wrap.style.cssText = 'flex:1;overflow:hidden;display:flex;flex-direction:column;position:relative;';
      const closeBtn = document.getElementById('mcqFsClose');
      if(closeBtn) closeBtn.style.display = 'none';
    }
    if(spHdr) spHdr.style.display = '';
    if(tabsEl) tabsEl.style.display = 'flex';
    if(btn) btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-expand"></i> Full Screen';

    try{ screen.orientation.unlock(); }catch(e){}
  }
}

/* ── These stubs keep backward compatibility ── */
function _renderMILPageV2(body, pageData, subjectId, subjectName, icon){
  _renderChapterListPage(body, pageData, subjectId, subjectName, icon, activeStream);
}
function _openMCQChapter(subjectId, chapterId, chapterName){
  _openChapterContent(subjectId, chapterId, chapterName, activeStream);
}



/* ── PDF Card (side by side) ── */
function _pdfCard(title, url){
  if(!url) return `
    <div style="grid-column:1/-1;text-align:center;padding:30px;color:var(--txm);">
      <i class="fas fa-file-pdf" style="font-size:28px;display:block;margin-bottom:8px;opacity:.3;"></i>
      <div style="font-size:12px;">Coming Soon</div>
    </div>`;

  return `
    <div onclick="openPDFViewer('${esc(title)}','','${url}','${url}')"
      style="
        background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r2);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);
        padding:14px;text-align:center;cursor:pointer;transition:all .22s;
        display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:8px;
      "
      onmouseover="this.style.transform='translateY(-2px)';this.style.boxShadow='0 6px 20px rgba(79,70,229,.13)'"
      onmouseout="this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow=''">
      <div style="width:46px;height:46px;border-radius:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#ef4444,#f97316);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px;color:#fff;">
        <i class="fas fa-file-pdf"></i>
      </div>
      <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx);line-height:1.4;">${esc(title)}</div>
      <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--p);font-weight:600;"><i class="fas fa-eye"></i> Open PDF</div>
    </div>`;
}

// ══ PDF Button Render ══
function _renderPDFBtn(pdf, hasMem, colorType) {
  const locked = pdf.isPaid && !hasMem;
  const colors = {
    orange: { bg: 'linear-gradient(135deg,#f97316,#ea580c)', light: 'rgba(249,115,22,.1)', text: '#f97316' },
    warn:   { bg: 'linear-gradient(135deg,#f59e0b,#d97706)', light: 'rgba(245,158,11,.1)', text: 'var(--warn)' },
    red:    { bg: 'linear-gradient(135deg,#ef4444,#dc2626)', light: 'rgba(239,68,68,.1)', text: 'var(--err)' }
  };
  const c = colors[colorType] || colors.orange;

  return `
  <div style="
    background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r2);
    border:1.5px solid var(--bd);
    display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;
    padding:12px 13px;margin-bottom:8px;
    cursor:pointer;transition:all .22s;
  "
  onclick="${locked ? 'openMem()' : `openPDFViewer('${esc(pdf.title || 'PDF')}','${esc(pdf.desc || '')}','${pdf.url}','${pdf.dlUrl || pdf.url}')`}"
  onmouseover="this.style.transform='translateY(-2px)';this.style.boxShadow='0 6px 20px rgba(0,0,0,.08)'"
  onmouseout="this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow=''">

    <!-- Icon -->
    <div style="width:46px;height:46px;border-radius:12px;
      background:${locked ? 'var(--sur2)' : c.bg};
      display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;
      font-size:20px;color:#fff;flex-shrink:0;border:${locked ? '1.5px solid var(--bd)' : 'none'};">
      <i class="fas fa-${locked ? 'lock' : 'file-pdf'}" style="color:${locked ? 'var(--txm)' : '#fff'};"></i>
    </div>

    <!-- Info -->
    <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
      <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;color:var(--tx);">
        ${esc(pdf.title || 'PDF')}
      </div>
      <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txm);margin-top:2px;">
        ${pdf.desc ? esc(pdf.desc) : (locked ? 'Premium Members Only' : 'Tap to Open PDF')}
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:4px;display:flex;gap:5px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
        <span style="font-size:9px;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;
          background:${locked ? 'rgba(239,68,68,.1)' : c.light};
          color:${locked ? 'var(--err)' : c.text};">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked ? 'lock' : 'file-pdf'}"></i>
          ${locked ? 'Premium' : 'PDF'}
        </span>
        ${pdf.pages ? `<span style="font-size:9px;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:6px;background:var(--sur2);color:var(--txm);font-weight:600;">${pdf.pages} pages</span>` : ''}
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Arrow -->
    <i class="fas fa-${locked ? 'crown' : 'chevron-right'}" style="color:${locked ? 'var(--warn)' : 'var(--txm)'};font-size:13px;flex-shrink:0;"></i>
  </div>`;
}

function openSubject(id, locked){
  if(locked){ openMem(); return; }
  const s = window._subjectsData?.find(x => x.id === id);
  if(!s) return;
  openSubjectMILPage(s.id, s.name||s.n, s.icon||s.ic);
}
