function _milLoader(){
  return `<div style="padding:12px 13px;">
    <div style="height:140px;border-radius:var(--r);margin-bottom:16px;background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;"></div>
    <div style="height:20px;width:40%;border-radius:20px;margin-bottom:14px;background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;"></div>
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px;margin-bottom:14px;">
      ${[1,2,3,4].map(()=>`<div style="height:120px;border-radius:var(--r);background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;"></div>`).join('')}
    </div>
    <div style="height:120px;border-radius:var(--r);background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;"></div>
  </div>`;
}

const STREAM_ORDER=['science','arts','commerce','10th'];
function switchStream(s,btn){
  const oldIdx=STREAM_ORDER.indexOf(activeStream);
  const newIdx=STREAM_ORDER.indexOf(s);
  const dir=newIdx>oldIdx?'left':'right';
  document.querySelectorAll('#streamTabs .tbtn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');
  activeStream=s;
  // Animate containers
  const targets=[
    $('subjGrid'),
    $('pyqList'),
    $('booksList'),
    $('vidList'),
    $('amazonList')
  ];
  targets.forEach(el=>{
    if(!el)return;
    el.classList.remove('stream-slide-left','stream-slide-right');
    void el.offsetWidth; // reflow
    el.classList.add(dir==='left'?'stream-slide-left':'stream-slide-right');
  });
  loadSubjects(s);
}

function toggleTermsBanner(){
  const banner = document.getElementById('termsBanner');
  const ic = document.getElementById('termsArrowIc');
  const isHidden = banner.style.display === 'none' || banner.style.display === '';
  if(isHidden){
    banner.style.display = 'block';
    ic.className = 'fas fa-chevron-down';
  } else {
    banner.style.display = 'none';
    ic.className = 'fas fa-chevron-up';
  }
}
/* ══ SUBJECT VIDEOS PAGE ══ */
function openSubjectVideos(subjectId, subjectName, stream){
  // SP open karo
  const sp = $('customPageSP');
  $('customPageTitle').textContent = subjectName + ' — Videos';
  const body = $('customPageBody');
  body.innerHTML = `
    <div style="padding:14px;">
      <div style="background:var(--g1);border-radius:var(--r);padding:16px 18px;margin-bottom:16px;color:#fff;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:13px;">
        <div style="width:46px;height:46px;border-radius:13px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:22px;flex-shrink:0;">
          <i class="fas fa-play-circle"></i>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:16px;font-weight:800;">${esc(subjectName)}</div>
          <div style="font-size:11px;opacity:.85;">Video Lectures</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="subjVidList">
        <div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading videos...</p></div>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
  openSP('customPageSP');
  // vidSP ke liye higher z-index ensure karo
  const vidSPEl = document.getElementById('vidSP');
  if(vidSPEl) vidSPEl.style.zIndex = '99999999';

  // GUN se assigned videos load karo
  const DB_SV = () => gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('subjectVideos').get(stream).get(subjectId);
  const assignedVideos = {};

  DB_SV().map().once((data, key) => {
    if(data && data.videoId) assignedVideos[key] = data;
  });

  setTimeout(() => {
    const list = Object.values(assignedVideos);
    if(!list.length){
      $('subjVidList').innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-video-slash"></i><p>Koi video assign nahi hai abhi</p></div>';
      return;
    }

    // Har video ka full data load karo
    GU && GU.membership === 'active';
    let rendered = 0;
    const vidCards = [];

    list.forEach(av => {
      DB.videos(stream).get(av.videoId).once(vData => {
        if(vData && vData.title){
          vidCards.push({id:av.videoId, ...vData});
        }
        rendered++;
        if(rendered === list.length){
          renderSubjVidList(vidCards, hasMem, stream);
        }
      });
    });

  }, 800);
}

function renderSubjVidList(vids, hasMem, stream){
  const el = $('subjVidList');
  if(!el) return;
  if(!vids.length){
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-video-slash"></i><p>Koi video nahi</p></div>';
    return;
  }
  el.innerHTML = vids.map(v => {
    const locked = v.paid && !hasMem;
    return `<div class="vcard" style="margin-bottom:10px;cursor:pointer;" onclick="${locked ? 'openMem()' : `playVideo('${v.id}','${stream}')`}">
      <div class="vthumb">
        ${v.thumb ? `<img src="${v.thumb}" alt="" loading="lazy">` : '<i class="fas fa-play-circle" style="font-size:28px;color:var(--p);"></i>'}
        <div class="vplay"><i class="fas fa-play"></i></div>
        ${locked ? '<div class="vlock"><i class="fas fa-lock" style="color:#fff;font-size:18px;"></i></div>' : ''}
      </div>
      <div class="vinfo">
        <h4>${esc(v.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc(v.desc||'')}</p>
        <div class="vtag ${locked?'paid':'free'}">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'play-circle'}"></i>
          ${locked ? 'Members Only' : 'Free Watch'}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   PYQ — with Download
══════════════════════════════════════ */
const DEMO_PYQS={science:[],arts:[],commerce:[],'10th':[]};

let _pyqOff = null;
function loadPYQs(stream){
  const el=$('pyqList');if(!el)return;
  el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading PYQs...</p></div>';
  if(_pyqOff){try{_pyqOff();}catch(e){}_pyqOff=null;}
  const pyqs={};let hasData=false;
  _pyqOff = DB.pyqs(stream||activeStream).map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.title){delete pyqs[key];}
    else{pyqs[key]={id:key,...data};hasData=true;}
    const list=Object.values(pyqs);
    renderPYQList(list.length?list:(DEMO_PYQS[stream||activeStream]||DEMO_PYQS.science),el);
  });
  setTimeout(()=>{
    if(!hasData)renderPYQList(DEMO_PYQS[stream||activeStream]||DEMO_PYQS.science,el);
  },2500);
}
let _allPYQs=[];
function renderPYQList(pyqs,el){
  _allPYQs=pyqs;
  if(!pyqs.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-file-alt"></i><p>Koi PYQ nahi hai abhi</p></div>';return;}
  const hasMem=GU&&GU.membership==='active';
  const show=pyqs.slice(0,3);
  el.innerHTML=show.map(p=>{
    const locked=p.locked&&!hasMem;
    return`<div class="res-card" data-id="${p.id}" data-locked="${locked}">
      <div class="res-ic pyq"><i class="fas fa-file-alt"></i></div>
      <div class="res-info">
        <h4>${esc(p.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc(p.subject||'')} • ${esc(p.desc||'')}</p>
        <div class="res-tags">
          <span class="rtag ${locked?'paid':'free'}">${locked?'<i class="fas fa-lock"></i> Premium':'<i class="fas fa-unlock"></i> Free'}</span>
          <span class="rtag blue"><i class="fas fa-download"></i> ${fmtL(p.dlCount||0)}</span>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="res-actions">
        <button class="dl-btn ${locked?'locked':''}" title="${locked?'Unlock required':'Download PDF'}" onclick="event.stopPropagation();handleResDownload('${p.id}','pyq',${locked})">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'download'}"></i>
        </button>
        <div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--txm);">PDF</div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
  // Click to view
  el.querySelectorAll('.res-card').forEach((card,i)=>{
    const p=pyqs[i];const locked=p.locked&&!hasMem;
    card.onclick=()=>{
      if(locked){openMem();return;}
      openPDFViewer(p.title,p.subject+' — '+p.desc,p.pdfUrl,p.dlUrl||p.pdfUrl);
    };
  });
}

function handleResDownload(id, type, locked){
  if(locked){ openMem(); return; }

  let data = type === 'pyq'
    ? [...Object.values(DEMO_PYQS).flat(), ..._allPYQs].find(x => x.id === id)
    : [...Object.values(DEMO_BOOKS).flat(), ..._allBooks].find(x => x.id === id);

  const url = data?.dlUrl || data?.pdfUrl || '';
  if(!url){ toast('PDF abhi admin ne upload nahi ki'); return; }

  // Normal device download
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  a.download = (data?.title || 'document') + '.pdf';
  a.target = '_blank';
  document.body.appendChild(a);
  a.click();
  document.body.removeChild(a);
  toast('Download shuru ho rahi hai... 📥');
}
  // Download Manager se download karo
  

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   BOOKS — with Download
══════════════════════════════════════ */
const DEMO_BOOKS={science:[],arts:[],commerce:[],'10th':[]};

let _booksOff = null;
function loadBooks(stream){
  const el=$('booksList');if(!el)return;
  el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading Books...</p></div>';
  if(_booksOff){try{_booksOff();}catch(e){}_booksOff=null;}
  const books={};let hasData=false;
  _booksOff = DB.books(stream||activeStream).map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.title){delete books[key];}
    else{books[key]={id:key,...data};hasData=true;}
    const list=Object.values(books);
    renderBookList(list.length?list:(DEMO_BOOKS[stream||activeStream]||DEMO_BOOKS.science),el);
  });
  setTimeout(()=>{
    if(!hasData)renderBookList(DEMO_BOOKS[stream||activeStream]||DEMO_BOOKS.science,el);
  },2500);
}
let _allBooks=[];
function renderBookList(books,el){
  _allBooks=books;
  if(!books.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-book"></i><p>Koi book nahi hai</p></div>';return;}
  const hasMem=GU&&GU.membership==='active';
  const show=books.slice(0,3);
  el.innerHTML=show.map(b=>{
    const locked=b.locked&&!hasMem;
    return`<div class="res-card" data-id="${b.id}">
      <div class="res-ic book"><i class="fas fa-book"></i></div>
      <div class="res-info">
        <h4>${esc(b.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc(b.subject||'')} • ${esc(b.desc||'')}</p>
        <div class="res-tags">
          <span class="rtag ${locked?'paid':'blue'}">${locked?'<i class="fas fa-lock"></i> Premium':'<i class="fas fa-book-open"></i> Read'}</span>
          <span class="rtag free"><i class="fas fa-download"></i> ${fmtL(b.dlCount||0)}</span>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="res-actions">
        <button class="dl-btn ${locked?'locked':''}" onclick="event.stopPropagation();handleResDownload('${b.id}','book',${locked})">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'download'}"></i>
        </button>
        <div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--txm);">PDF</div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
  el.querySelectorAll('.res-card').forEach((card,i)=>{
    const b=books[i];const locked=b.locked&&!hasMem;
    card.onclick=()=>{
      if(locked){openMem();return;}
      openPDFViewer(b.title,b.subject||'Book',b.pdfUrl,b.dlUrl||b.pdfUrl);
    };
  });
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   PDF VIEWER
══════════════════════════════════════ */
function openPDFViewer(title, subtitle, pdfUrl, dlUrl){
  if(!pdfUrl){ toast('PDF abhi available nahi hai'); return; }

  $('pdfViewTitle').textContent = title || 'PDF';
  $('pdfViewSubtitle').textContent = subtitle || '';
  const dl = $('pdfDownloadBtn');
  if(dlUrl){ dl.href = dlUrl; dl.style.display = 'flex'; }
  else if(pdfUrl){ dl.href = pdfUrl; dl.style.display = 'flex'; }
  else { dl.style.display = 'none'; }

  const frame = $('pdfFrame');
  
  // Pehle blank karo — flicker nahi aayega
  frame.src = 'about:blank';
  
  // Loader dikhao
  let loader = $('pdfLoader');
  if(!loader){
    loader = document.createElement('div');
    loader.id = 'pdfLoader';
    loader.style.cssText = 'position:absolute;inset:0;background:#525659;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;z-index:10;';
    loader.innerHTML = `
      <div style="width:44px;height:44px;border:4px solid rgba(255,255,255,.15);border-top-color:#fff;border-radius:50%;animation:sp .9s linear infinite;margin-bottom:14px;"></div>
      <div style="color:rgba(255,255,255,.6);font-size:12px;font-weight:600;">PDF Load Ho Raha Hai...</div>
    `;
    $('pdfViewSP').querySelector('.pdf-view-wrap').style.position = 'relative';
    $('pdfViewSP').querySelector('.pdf-view-wrap').appendChild(loader);
  }
  loader.style.display = 'flex';

  frame.style.cssText = 'flex:1;border:none;width:100%;height:100%;';
  
  // SP pehle open karo
  openSP('pdfViewSP');
  
  // Thoda delay — blank load ho jaye pehle
  // Thoda delay — blank load ho jaye pehle
  setTimeout(()=>{
    frame.onload = ()=>{
      if(loader) loader.style.display = 'none';
    };
    
    // URL convert karo — Drive / Archive bhi preview ho
    let finalUrl = pdfUrl;
    
    // Google Drive fix
    // https://drive.google.com/file/d/FILE_ID/view
    // https://drive.google.com/open?id=FILE_ID
    if(pdfUrl.includes('drive.google.com')){
      let fileId = '';
      // Format 1: /file/d/ID/
      const m1 = pdfUrl.match(/\/file\/d\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
      if(m1) fileId = m1[1];
      // Format 2: ?id=ID
      const m2 = pdfUrl.match(/[?&]id=([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
      if(m2) fileId = m2[1];
      if(fileId){
        finalUrl = `https://drive.google.com/file/d/${fileId}/preview`;
      }
    }
    
    // Archive.org fix
    // https://archive.org/details/XXXX
    // https://archive.org/download/XXXX/file.pdf
    else if(pdfUrl.includes('archive.org')){
      if(pdfUrl.includes('/details/')){
        // Details page — embed karo
        finalUrl = pdfUrl.replace('/details/', '/embed/') + '?ui=embed';
      } else if(pdfUrl.includes('/download/')){
        // Direct PDF link — Google Docs viewer se
        finalUrl = `https://docs.google.com/viewer?url=${encodeURIComponent(pdfUrl)}&embedded=true`;
      } else {
        finalUrl = `https://docs.google.com/viewer?url=${encodeURIComponent(pdfUrl)}&embedded=true`;
      }
    }
    
    // Direct PDF link jo preview nahi hota — Google Docs viewer
    else if(pdfUrl.endsWith('.pdf') && !pdfUrl.includes('docs.google.com')){
      // Pehle direct try karo
      finalUrl = pdfUrl;
    }
    
    frame.src = finalUrl;
    
    // Download button bhi sahi URL se
    const dl = $('pdfDownloadBtn');
    if(dl) dl.href = pdfUrl; // Original URL se download
    
  }, 150);
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   AMAZON — Commission Tracking
══════════════════════════════════════ */
const DEMO_AMZ=[];

let _amzOff = null;
function loadAmazonItems(){
  const el=$('amazonList');if(!el)return;
  if(_amzOff){try{_amzOff();}catch(e){}_amzOff=null;}
  const items={};let hasData=false;
  _amzOff = DB.amazon().map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.title){delete items[key];}
    else{items[key]={id:key,...data};hasData=true;}
    const list=Object.values(items);
    _amzItems=list.length?list:DEMO_AMZ;
    renderAmazonList(_amzItems,el);
  });
  setTimeout(()=>{
    if(!hasData){_amzItems=DEMO_AMZ;renderAmazonList(DEMO_AMZ,el);}
  },2500);
}

function renderAmazonList(items,el){
  if(!items.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fab fa-amazon"></i><p>Koi item nahi</p></div>';return;}
  const show=items.slice(0,3);
  el.innerHTML=show.map(it=>`
    <div class="amz-card" onclick="openAmazonItem('${it.id}')">
      ${it.imgUrl
        ?`<img src="${it.imgUrl}" class="amz-thumb" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.style.display='none'">`
        :`<div class="amz-thumb-ic"><i class="fab fa-amazon"></i></div>`}
      <div class="amz-info">
        <h4>${esc(it.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc((it.desc||'').substring(0,55))}...</p>
        <div class="amz-price">${esc(it.price||'Check Price')}</div>
        ${it.commission?`<div class="amz-comm"><i class="fas fa-hand-holding-usd"></i> EduSagar ko ${esc(it.commission)} commission</div>`:''}
      </div>
      <div class="amz-arrow"><i class="fas fa-chevron-right"></i></div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function openAmazonItem(id){
  const it=_amzItems.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(!it)return;
  currentAffiliateUrl=it.affiliateUrl||'';
  $('amzViewTitle').textContent=it.title||'Product';
  $('amzViewImg').src=it.imgUrl||'';
  $('amzViewName').textContent=it.title||'';
  $('amzViewDesc').textContent=it.desc||'';
  $('amzViewPrice').textContent=it.price||'Amazon par check karein';
  // Track click
  if(CU)DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('amzClicks').put((Date.now())+'_'+id);
  openSP('amazonViewSP');
}

function openAffiliateLink(){
  if(currentAffiliateUrl){
    // Track affiliate click
    if(CU){DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('affiliateClicks').put(Date.now());}
    window.open(currentAffiliateUrl,'_blank');
  } else {
    toast('Link abhi available nahi');
  }
}

function renderPYQListFull(pyqs,el){
  if(!pyqs||!pyqs.length){
    el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-file-alt"></i><p>Koi PYQ nahi</p></div>';return;
  }
  const hasMem=GU&&GU.membership==='active';
  el.innerHTML=pyqs.map(p=>{
    const locked=p.locked&&!hasMem;
    return`<div class="res-card">
      <div class="res-ic pyq"><i class="fas fa-file-alt"></i></div>
      <div class="res-info">
        <h4>${esc(p.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc(p.subject||'')} • ${esc(p.desc||'')}</p>
        <div class="res-tags">
          <span class="rtag ${locked?'paid':'free'}">${locked?'<i class="fas fa-lock"></i> Premium':'<i class="fas fa-unlock"></i> Free'}</span>
          <span class="rtag blue"><i class="fas fa-download"></i> ${fmtL(p.dlCount||0)}</span>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="res-actions">
        <button class="dl-btn ${locked?'locked':''}" onclick="event.stopPropagation();handleResDownload('${p.id}','pyq',${locked})">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'download'}"></i>
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

    (p.title||'').toLowerCase().includes(q)||
    (p.subject||'').toLowerCase().includes(q)
  );
  renderPYQListFull(filtered,$('pyqFullList'));
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   VIDEOS
══════════════════════════════════════ */
let _vidOff = null;
function loadVideos(stream){
  const vl=$('vidList');
  const cached=CACHE.getStale('vids_'+stream);
  if(cached&&cached.length)renderVideoList(cached,stream);
  else vl.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading videos...</p></div>';
  if(_vidOff){try{_vidOff();}catch(e){}_vidOff=null;}
  const vids={};
  _vidOff = DB.videos(stream).map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.title){delete vids[key];}
    else vids[key]={id:key,...data};
    const list=Object.values(vids);
    CACHE.set('vids_'+stream,list);
    renderVideoList(list,stream);
  });
}

let _allVids=[];
function renderVideoList(vids,stream){
  _allVids=vids;_allVids_stream=stream;
  const vl=$('vidList');
  if(!vids.length){vl.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-video-slash"></i><p>Koi video nahi hai abhi</p></div>';return;}
  const hasMem=GU&&GU.membership==='active';
  const show=vids.slice(0,3);
  vl.innerHTML=show.map(v=>{
    const locked=v.paid&&!hasMem;
    return`<div class="vcard" onclick="${locked?'openMem()':'playVideo(\''+v.id+'\',\''+stream+'\')'}">
      <div class="vthumb">
        ${v.thumb?`<img src="${v.thumb}" alt="" loading="lazy">`:'<i class="fas fa-play-circle" style="font-size:28px;color:var(--p);"></i>'}
        <div class="vplay"><i class="fas fa-play"></i></div>
        ${locked?'<div class="vlock"><i class="fas fa-lock" style="color:#fff;font-size:18px;"></i></div>':''}
      </div>
      <div class="vinfo">
        <h4>${esc(v.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc(v.desc||'')}</p>
        <div class="vtag ${locked?'paid':'free'}">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'play-circle'}"></i>${locked?'Members Only':'Free Watch'}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}


function loadProfileVideos(){
  const vl=$('profileVidList');
  if(!vl)return;
  const cached=CACHE.getStale('vids_'+activeStream);
  if(cached&&cached.length){
    renderVideoListInEl(cached,vl);return;
  }
  const vids=[];const vs=new Set();
  DB.videos(activeStream).map().once((data,key)=>{
    if(data&&data.title&&!vs.has(key)){vs.add(key);vids.push({id:key,...data});}
  });
  setTimeout(()=>renderVideoListInEl(vids,vl),1400);
}

function renderVideoListInEl(vids,vl){
  const hasMem=GU&&GU.membership==='active';
  if(!vids.length){
    vl.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-video-slash"></i><p>Koi video nahi hai abhi</p></div>';
    return;
  }
  vl.innerHTML=vids.map(v=>{
    const locked=v.paid&&!hasMem;
    return`<div class="vcard" onclick="${locked?'openMem()':'playVideo(\''+v.id+'\',\''+activeStream+'\')'}">
      <div class="vthumb">
        ${v.thumb?`<img src="${v.thumb}" alt="" loading="lazy">`:'<i class="fas fa-play-circle" style="font-size:28px;color:var(--p);"></i>'}
        <div class="vplay"><i class="fas fa-play"></i></div>
        ${locked?'<div class="vlock"><i class="fas fa-lock" style="color:#fff;font-size:18px;"></i></div>':''}
      </div>
      <div class="vinfo">
        <h4>${esc(v.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc(v.desc||'')}</p>
        <div class="vtag ${locked?'paid':'free'}">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'play-circle'}"></i>
          ${locked?'Members Only':'Free Watch'}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function playVideo(id,stream){
  openSP('vidSP');
  const cached=CACHE.getStale('vids_'+stream);
  const v=cached?.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(v)applyVideo(v);
  else DB.videos(stream).get(id).once(data=>{if(data)applyVideo({id,...data});});
}

function applyVideo(v) {
  const ve = $('vidEl');

  // Pehle sab band karo
  try { ve.pause(); } catch(e) {}
  ve.src = '';

  const url = v.url || v.videoUrl || v.link || '';
  if (!url) {
    _hideVidSpinner();
    // Koi error text nahi — bas spinner ghoomta rahe
    // User back karke doosra video choose kar sakta hai
    return;
  }

  const isYT = url.includes('youtube.com') || url.includes('youtu.be');

  $('vidTitle').textContent  = v.title || 'Video';
  $('vidFull').textContent   = v.title || '';
  $('vidDesc').textContent   = v.desc  || '';

  // Spinner dikhao
  _showVidSpinner();

  if (isYT) {
    // ── YouTube ──────────────────────────────
    const m    = url.match(/(?:v=|youtu\.be\/)([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{11})/);
    const ytId = m ? m[1] : '';
    if (!ytId) { _hideVidSpinner(); return; }

    // Video element hide
    ve.style.display = 'none';
    ve.src = '';

    // vpWrap — YouTube ke liye fixed height
    const vpWrap = $('vpWrap');
    vpWrap.style.height    = '56vw';
    vpWrap.style.maxHeight = '340px';
    vpWrap.style.position  = 'relative';

    // iframe banao ya reuse karo
    // Purana iframe hamesha hatao — fresh banao
// Purana iframe hamesha hatao — fresh banao
    let ytFrame = document.getElementById('ytPlayerFrame');
    if (ytFrame) {
      try { ytFrame.src = 'about:blank'; } catch(e) {}
      try { ytFrame.parentNode.removeChild(ytFrame); } catch(e) {}
      ytFrame = null;
    }
    ytFrame = document.createElement('iframe');
    ytFrame.id = 'ytPlayerFrame';
    ytFrame.allow = 'autoplay;encrypted-media;fullscreen;picture-in-picture';
    ytFrame.allowFullscreen = true;
    ytFrame.style.cssText = `
      position:absolute;
      top:0;left:0;
      width:100%;height:100%;
      border:none;
      z-index:5;
      background:#000;
    `;
    vpWrap.appendChild(ytFrame);

    ytFrame.style.display = 'block';

    // onload — spinner hatao
    ytFrame.onload = () => _hideVidSpinner();

    // src set karo
    ytFrame.src = `https://www.youtube.com/embed/${ytId}?autoplay=1&rel=0&controls=1&modestbranding=1`;

    // Custom controls hide — YT ke apne hain
    $('vCtrl').style.display = 'none';

    // Safety fallback — 6 sec mein spinner hatao
    setTimeout(() => _hideVidSpinner(), 6000);

  } else {
    // ── MP4 ──────────────────────────────────
    const ytFrame = document.getElementById('ytPlayerFrame');
    if (ytFrame) { ytFrame.style.display = 'none'; ytFrame.src = ''; }

    // vpWrap reset
    const vpWrap = $('vpWrap');
    vpWrap.style.height    = '';
    vpWrap.style.maxHeight = '';

    ve.style.display = 'block';
    $('vCtrl').style.display = '';

    ve.src = url;
    ve.load();

    // Events
    ve.oncanplay  = () => { _hideVidSpinner(); adjustVideoSize(ve); ve.play().catch(()=>{}); };
    ve.onplaying  = () => _hideVidSpinner();
    ve.onwaiting  = () => _showVidSpinner();
    ve.onstalled  = () => _showVidSpinner();

    // Error — koi text nahi, sirf spinner ghoomta rahe
    ve.onerror = () => {
      // Spinner ghoomta rahe — user khud back karega
      // _showVidSpinner() already chal raha hai
    };

    ve.ontimeupdate = () => {
      const c = ve.currentTime, d = ve.duration || 0;
      $('vCur').textContent = fmtT(c);
      $('vDur').textContent = fmtT(d);
      if (d) $('vSeek').value = (c / d) * 100;
    };

    // Play button icon update
    ve.onpause = () => { if($('vPlayBtn')) $('vPlayBtn').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-play"></i>'; };
    ve.onplay  = () => { if($('vPlayBtn')) $('vPlayBtn').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-pause"></i>'; };

    showVCtrl();

    // Safety fallback — 10 sec mein spinner hatao
    setTimeout(() => _hideVidSpinner(), 10000);
  }

  loadRecommendedVideos(v.id, v);
}

function adjustVideoSize(ve){
  const vw = ve.videoWidth, vh = ve.videoHeight;
  if(!vw || !vh) return;
  const wrap = $('vpWrap');
  const isPortraitVideo = vh > vw;
  const isLandscape = window.innerWidth > window.innerHeight;
  
  if(isPortraitVideo){
    const maxH = isLandscape ? window.innerHeight : Math.min(window.innerHeight * 0.55, 420);
    wrap.style.height = maxH + 'px';
    ve.style.height = maxH + 'px';
    ve.style.width = 'auto';
    ve.style.maxWidth = '100%';
    ve.style.maxHeight = maxH + 'px';
  } else {
    wrap.style.height = '';
    ve.style.height = 'auto';
    ve.style.width = '100%';
    ve.style.maxHeight = '';
  }
}

window.addEventListener('popstate', function(e) {
  if (_spStack.length > 0) {
    const topId = _spStack[_spStack.length - 1];

    // ✅ Video SP ke liye special handling
    if (topId === 'vidSP') {
      closeVideo();
      return;
    }

    _origCloseSP(topId);
    _spStack.pop();
  }
});
window.addEventListener('resize', ()=>{
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  if(ve && ve.src) adjustVideoSize(ve);
});

function showVidLoader(show, msg){
  let ld=$('vidLoader');
  if(!ld){
    ld=document.createElement('div');
    ld.id='vidLoader';
    // Controls ke peeche, unse upar nahi — z-index:8 (controls z-index se kam)
    ld.style.cssText='position:absolute;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,.45);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;z-index:8;';
    ld.innerHTML=`<div style="width:28px;height:28px;border:2.5px solid rgba(255,255,255,.25);border-top-color:#fff;border-radius:50%;animation:sp .8s linear infinite;"></div>`;
    $('vpWrap').appendChild(ld);
  }
  ld.style.display = show ? 'flex' : 'none';
}

function showVidError(){
  let ld=$('vidLoader');
  if(!ld) return;
  ld.style.cssText='position:absolute;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,.72);display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;z-index:8;';
  ld.style.display='flex';
  ld.innerHTML=`
    <i class="fas fa-wifi-slash" style="font-size:22px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.5);margin-bottom:8px;"></i>
    <div style="color:rgba(255,255,255,.85);font-size:12px;margin-bottom:10px;">Video load nahi hua</div>
    <button onclick="retryVideo()" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.18);color:#fff;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.3);border-radius:16px;padding:6px 16px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;"><i class="fas fa-redo"></i> Retry</button>
  `;
}

function retryVideo(){
  const ve=$('vidEl');
  showVidLoader(true,'Retry ho raha hai...');
  ve.load();
  ve.play().catch(()=>{});
}
function closeVideo() {
  const ve = $('vidEl');

  // ✅ MP4 — hard stop
  try { ve.pause(); } catch(e) {}
  try { ve.removeAttribute('src'); } catch(e) {}
  try { ve.load(); } catch(e) {}
  try { ve.srcObject = null; } catch(e) {}

  // ✅ Saare event listeners remove karo
  ve.oncanplay   = null;
  ve.onplaying   = null;
  ve.onwaiting   = null;
  ve.onstalled   = null;
  ve.onerror     = null;
  ve.ontimeupdate = null;
  ve.onpause     = null;
  ve.onplay      = null;

  // ✅ YouTube iframe — completely destroy karo
  const ytFrame = document.getElementById('ytPlayerFrame');
  if (ytFrame) {
    // src blank karne se bhi audio aa sakta hai — isliye remove karo
    try {
      ytFrame.contentWindow.postMessage('{"event":"command","func":"stopVideo","args":""}', '*');
    } catch(e) {}
    ytFrame.src = 'about:blank';
    ytFrame.style.display = 'none';
    // Parent se hata do completely
    try { ytFrame.parentNode.removeChild(ytFrame); } catch(e) {}
  }

  // ✅ vpWrap reset
  const vpWrap = $('vpWrap');
  if (vpWrap) {
    vpWrap.style.height = '';
    vpWrap.style.maxHeight = '';
  }

  // ✅ Controls reset
  const vCtrl = $('vCtrl');
  if (vCtrl) { vCtrl.style.display = ''; vCtrl.classList.remove('hide'); }

  // ✅ Play button reset
  const vPlayBtn = $('vPlayBtn');
  if (vPlayBtn) vPlayBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-play"></i>';

  // ✅ Progress reset
  const vSeek = $('vSeek');
  if (vSeek) vSeek.value = 0;
  const vCur = $('vCur');
  if (vCur) vCur.textContent = '0:00';
  const vDur = $('vDur');
  if (vDur) vDur.textContent = '0:00';

  // ✅ Spinner hide
  _hideVidSpinner();

  // ✅ SP band karo
  // ✅ SP band karo + Stack update
  _origCloseSP('vidSP');
  const _vidIdx = _spStack.lastIndexOf('vidSP');
  if (_vidIdx !== -1) _spStack.splice(_vidIdx, 1);

  // ✅ Extra safety — 300ms baad bhi check karo
  setTimeout(() => {
    const ve2 = $('vidEl');
    if (ve2) {
      try { ve2.pause(); } catch(e) {}
      try { ve2.removeAttribute('src'); } catch(e) {}
      try { ve2.load(); } catch(e) {}
    }
    const yt2 = document.getElementById('ytPlayerFrame');
    if (yt2) {
      try { yt2.src = 'about:blank'; } catch(e) {}
      try { yt2.parentNode.removeChild(yt2); } catch(e) {}
    }
  }, 300);
}
/* ══ CUSTOM SUBJECT PAGES ══ */
let customPageStack=[];

function openCustomPage(title, htmlCode, icon) {
  $('customPageTitle').textContent = title || 'Page';
  renderCustomHTML($('customPageBody'), htmlCode, title);
  openSP('customPageSP'); // ← history push hoga
  customPageStack = [];
}

function closeCustomPage(){
  closeSP('customPageSP');
  $('customPageBody').innerHTML='';
}

function renderCustomHTML(container, htmlCode, pageTitle){
  const iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
  iframe.style.cssText = 'width:100%;height:100%;border:none;min-height:calc(100vh - 60px);';
  iframe.setAttribute('sandbox','allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-forms');
  const isDark = document.body.classList.contains('dark');

  // ✅ YEH ADD KARO — user data inject
  const userDataScript = `<script>var _USER={
    membership:${JSON.stringify(GU.membership||null)},
    membershipStream:${JSON.stringify(GU.membershipStream||null)},
    isAdmin:${JSON.stringify(GU.isAdmin||false)},
    uid:${JSON.stringify(CU?CU.uid:null)}
  };<\/script>`;

  const injectedCSS = `<style>:root{--p:#4f46e5;--bg:${isDark?'#0b0a1e':'#f1f2ff'};--sur:${isDark?'#141330':'#ffffff'};--tx:${isDark?'#eeeeff':'#0f0d2e'};--txm:${isDark?'#8885b0':'#6b7194'};--bd:${isDark?'#2a2850':'#e4e6f8'};--ok:#10b981;--err:#ef4444;--font:'DM Sans',sans-serif;}*{box-sizing:border-box;margin:0;padding:0;}body{font-family:var(--font);background:var(--bg);color:var(--tx);padding:14px;}</style><link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet"><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.5.0/css/all.min.css">`;

  const bridgeScript = `<script>
    function openSubPage(title,htmlCode){window.parent.postMessage({type:'openSubPage',title,htmlCode},'*');}
    function goBack(){window.parent.postMessage({type:'goBack'},'*');}
    function openInApp(url,title){window.parent.postMessage({type:'openUrl',url,title},'*');}
    function openMembership(){window.parent.postMessage({type:'openMem'},'*');}
  <\/script>`;

  // ✅ userDataScript pehle inject karo
  iframe.srcdoc = `<!DOCTYPE html><html><head>${injectedCSS}${userDataScript}${bridgeScript}</head><body>${htmlCode}</body></html>`;
  container.innerHTML = '';
  container.appendChild(iframe);
  window.addEventListener('message', handleIframeMsg);
}

function handleIframeMsg(e){
  if(!e.data||!e.data.type) return;
  if(e.data.type==='openSubPage'){
    openSubPage(e.data.title, e.data.htmlCode);
  }
  else if(e.data.type==='goBack'){
    closeSP('customSubPageSP');
  }
  // ✅ YEH DO NEW CASES ADD KARO
  else if(e.data.type==='openUrl'){
    $('apkWebTitle').textContent = e.data.title || 'Content';
    $('apkWebFrame').src = e.data.url || '';
    openSP('apkWebSP');
  }
  else if(e.data.type==='openMem'){
    openMem();
  }
}

function openSubPage(title, htmlCode) {
  $('customSubPageTitle').textContent = title || 'Page';
  renderCustomHTML($('customSubPageBody'), htmlCode, title);
  openSP('customSubPageSP'); // ← ye ab history push karega automatically
}

/* ══ ADMIN — SUBJECT MANAGER ══ */
let subjMgrStream='science';

function openSubjManager(){
  closeMenu();
  if(!GU.isAdmin){toast('Admin only!');return;}
  openSP('subjManagerSP');
  loadSubjMgrList('science');
}

function switchSubjMgr(stream,btn){
  document.querySelectorAll('#subjMgrTabs .tbtn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');
  subjMgrStream=stream;
  loadSubjMgrList(stream);
}

function loadSubjMgrList(stream){
  const el=$('subjMgrList');
  el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading...</p></div>';
  const items=[];const seen=new Set();
  const defaultList=SUBJECTS[stream]||[];
  defaultList.forEach((s,i)=>{
    const id='def_'+stream+'_'+i;
    if(!seen.has(id)){seen.add(id);items.push({id,name:s.n,icon:s.ic,locked:s.l,isDefault:true});}
  });
  DB.subjects(stream).map().once((data,key)=>{
    if(data&&data.name&&!seen.has(key)){seen.add(key);items.push({id:key,...data,isDefault:false});}
  });
  setTimeout(()=>renderSubjMgrList(items,el),800);
}


function renderSubjMgrList(items,el){
  if(!items.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-book"></i><p>Koi subject nahi</p></div>';return;}
  el.innerHTML=items.map(s=>`
    <div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r2);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);padding:13px;margin-bottom:9px;">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:11px;">
        
        <!-- Icon -->
        <div style="width:42px;height:42px;border-radius:11px;background:var(--plight);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:18px;color:var(--p);flex-shrink:0;">
          <i class="${s.icon||s.ic||'fas fa-book'}"></i>
        </div>
        
        <!-- Info -->
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
          <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;">${esc(s.name||'Subject')}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txm);margin-top:2px;">
            <span style="background:var(--plight);color:var(--p);padding:1px 6px;border-radius:6px;font-family:monospace;font-size:9px;">${s.id}</span>
            &nbsp;•&nbsp;${s.isDefault?'Default':'Custom'}
            &nbsp;•&nbsp;${s.customPage?'<span style="color:var(--ok)"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> Page Added</span>':'<span style="color:var(--txm)">No Page</span>'}
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Action Buttons -->
        <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;flex-shrink:0;">
          <button class="btn bsm bp" onclick="editSubjectPage('${s.id}','${esc(s.name)}')" title="Edit Page">
            <i class="fas fa-code"></i>
          </button>
          <button class="btn bsm" style="background:var(--err);color:#fff;" onclick="deleteSubject('${s.id}','${esc(s.name)}',${s.isDefault})" title="Delete">
            <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Lock/Free Toggle Row -->
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-top:11px;padding-top:10px;border-top:1.5px solid var(--bd);">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;">
          <i class="fas fa-${s.locked?'lock':'unlock'}" style="color:${s.locked?'var(--err)':'var(--ok)'};font-size:14px;" id="lockic_${s.id}"></i>
          <div>
            <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;" id="locktxt_${s.id}">${s.locked?'Premium Only':'Free for All'}</div>
            <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txm);">${s.locked?'Sirf members dekh sakte hain':'Sab students dekh sakte hain'}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <!-- Toggle Switch -->
        <div onclick="toggleSubjectLock('${s.id}','${esc(s.name)}',${s.locked?'true':'false'},${s.isDefault})"
          style="width:52px;height:28px;border-radius:14px;background:${s.locked?'var(--err)':'var(--ok)'};cursor:pointer;position:relative;transition:background .3s;flex-shrink:0;"
          id="locktgl_${s.id}">
          <div style="position:absolute;top:4px;${s.locked?'right:4px':'left:4px'};width:20px;height:20px;background:#fff;border-radius:50%;transition:all .3s;box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.2);"
            id="locktglthumb_${s.id}">
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function toggleSubjectLock(id, name, currentLocked, isDefault){
  const newLocked = currentLocked === true || currentLocked === 'true' ? false : true;
  
  // UI turant update karo
  const ic = $('lockic_'+id);
  const txt = $('locktxt_'+id);
  const tgl = $('locktgl_'+id);
  const thumb = $('locktglthumb_'+id);
  
  if(ic){
    ic.className = 'fas fa-'+(newLocked?'lock':'unlock');
    ic.style.color = newLocked?'var(--err)':'var(--ok)';
  }
  if(txt) txt.textContent = newLocked?'Premium Only':'Free for All';
  if(tgl) tgl.style.background = newLocked?'var(--err)':'var(--ok)';
  if(thumb) thumb.style.cssText = `position:absolute;top:4px;${newLocked?'right:4px':'left:4px'};width:20px;height:20px;background:#fff;border-radius:50%;transition:all .3s;box-shadow:0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.2);`;

  // GUN mein save karo
  if(isDefault === true || isDefault === 'true'){
    // Default subject — GUN mein naya entry banao
    const newId = 'custom_lock_'+id+'_'+Date.now();
    const stream = id.split('_')[0] === 'def' ? subjMgrStream : subjMgrStream;
    
    // Default list se data lo
    const defaultList = SUBJECTS[subjMgrStream]||[];
    const parts = id.split('_');
    const idx = parseInt(parts[parts.length-1]);
    const s = defaultList[idx];
    
    if(s){
      DB.subjects(subjMgrStream).get(id).put({
        id:id,
        name:s.n||name,
        icon:s.ic||'fas fa-book',
        locked:newLocked,
        customPage:'',
        createdAt:Date.now()
      });
    }
  } else {
    // Custom subject — seedha update karo
    DB.subjects(subjMgrStream).get(id).get('locked').put(newLocked);
  }

  toast((newLocked?'🔒 '+name+' — Premium Only':'🔓 '+name+' — Free for All'));
  
  // Local _subjectsData bhi update karo
  if(window._subjectsData){
    const subj = window._subjectsData.find(x=>x.id===id);
    if(subj) subj.locked = newLocked;
  }
}

async function addNewSubject(){
  const r1=await caInput('Subject Name','Subject ka naam:','Mathematics');
  if(r1.btn!=='save'||!r1.input)return;
  const r2=await caInput('Icon Class','FontAwesome icon class:','fas fa-calculator');
  if(r2.btn!=='save'||!r2.input)return;
  const r3=await showAlert('fas fa-lock','warn','Locked?','Premium members ke liye locked hoga?',[{l:'Haan — Locked',c:'ca-danger',v:'yes'},{l:'Nahi — Free',c:'ca-primary',v:'no'}]);
  const locked=r3.btn==='yes';
  const id='custom_'+Date.now();
  DB.subjects(subjMgrStream).get(id).put({id,name:r1.input,icon:r2.input,locked,customPage:'',createdAt:Date.now()});
  toast('Subject add ho gaya! ✅');
  setTimeout(()=>loadSubjMgrList(subjMgrStream),600);
}

async function editSubjectPage(id,name){
  const r=await caInput(name+' — Page HTML','HTML/CSS/JS code paste karo:','<h1>Hello!</h1>');
  if(r.btn!=='save')return;
  const html=r.input||'';
  if(id.startsWith('def_')){
    const newId='custom_'+id+'_'+Date.now();
    const parts=id.split('_');
    const stream=parts[1];const idx=parseInt(parts[2]);
    const s=SUBJECTS[stream]?.[idx];
    if(s){DB.subjects(subjMgrStream).get(newId).put({id:newId,name:s.n,icon:s.ic,locked:s.l,customPage:html,createdAt:Date.now()});}
  } else {
    DB.subjects(subjMgrStream).get(id).get('customPage').put(html);
  }
  toast('Page save ho gaya! ✅');
  setTimeout(()=>loadSubjMgrList(subjMgrStream),600);
}

async function deleteSubject(id,name,isDefault){
  const r=await caConfirm('Delete Subject','Kya "'+name+'" delete karna chahte ho?','Delete');
  if(r.btn!=='yes')return;
  if(isDefault){toast('Default subjects delete nahi hote');return;}
  DB.subjects(subjMgrStream).get(id).put(null);
  toast(name+' delete ho gaya');
  setTimeout(()=>loadSubjMgrList(subjMgrStream),600);
}

/* ══ YAHAN KHATAM ══ */

/* ══ VIDEO CONTROLS IMPROVED ══ */
let _vSeeking = false;
let _vCtrlTO = null;
let _vAutoHideTO = null;

// Touch/Click se controls show/hide
function showVCtrl(){
  const ctrl = $('vCtrl');
  if(!ctrl) return;
  ctrl.classList.remove('hide');
  clearTimeout(_vCtrlTO);
  _vCtrlTO = setTimeout(()=>{
    const ve = $('vidEl');
    if(ve && !ve.paused) ctrl.classList.add('hide');
  }, 4000);
}

function hideVCtrl(){
  clearTimeout(_vCtrlTO);
  $('vCtrl')?.classList.add('hide');
}

// vpWrap click — toggle controls
$('vpWrap').addEventListener('click', function(e){
  if(e.target.closest('.vbtn') || e.target.closest('input')) return;
  const ctrl = $('vCtrl');
  if(ctrl.classList.contains('hide')){
    showVCtrl();
  } else {
    hideVCtrl();
  }
});

// Play / Pause
function vPlay(){
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  const btn = $('vPlayBtn');
  if(!ve) return;
  if(ve.paused){
    ve.play().catch(()=>{});
    if(btn) btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-pause"></i>';
    // Auto hide after play
    showVCtrl();
  } else {
    ve.pause();
    if(btn) btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-play"></i>';
    // Keep controls visible when paused
    showVCtrl();
    clearTimeout(_vCtrlTO);
  }
}

// Back 10s
function vBack(){
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  if(!ve) return;
  ve.currentTime = Math.max(0, ve.currentTime - 10);
  showVCtrl();
  // Flash indicator
  _showSeekFlash('-10s');
}

// Forward 10s
function vFwd(){
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  if(!ve) return;
  ve.currentTime = Math.min(ve.duration||0, ve.currentTime + 10);
  showVCtrl();
  _showSeekFlash('+10s');
}

// Seek flash indicator
function _showSeekFlash(txt){
  let fl = $('seekFlash');
  if(!fl){
    fl = document.createElement('div');
    fl.id = 'seekFlash';
    fl.style.cssText = 'position:absolute;top:50%;left:50%;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);background:rgba(0,0,0,.6);color:#fff;font-size:14px;font-weight:800;padding:8px 18px;border-radius:20px;pointer-events:none;z-index:15;transition:opacity .3s;';
    $('vpWrap').appendChild(fl);
  }
  fl.textContent = txt;
  fl.style.opacity = '1';
  clearTimeout(fl._to);
  fl._to = setTimeout(()=>{ fl.style.opacity='0'; }, 700);
}

// Scrub
let _scrubActive = false;
function vSeekStart(){ _scrubActive = true; }
function vSeekEnd(){
  _scrubActive = false;
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  const s = $('vSeek');
  if(ve && ve.duration) ve.currentTime = (s.value/100)*ve.duration;
}
function vScrub(s){
  if(!_scrubActive) return;
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  if(ve && ve.duration){
    ve.currentTime = (s.value/100)*ve.duration;
    $('vCur').textContent = fmtT(ve.currentTime);
  }
  showVCtrl();
}

// Fullscreen — landscape force
// Fullscreen — landscape force
function vFS(){
  const btn = $('vFSBtn');
  const ytFrame = document.getElementById('ytPlayerFrame');
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  const wrap = $('vpWrap');
  
  // Check kar — abhi fullscreen mein hai?
  const isFS = wrap.classList.contains('yt-landscape-forced') || 
               document.fullscreenElement || 
               document.webkitFullscreenElement;
  
  if(isFS){
    // EXIT fullscreen
    wrap.classList.remove('yt-landscape-forced');
    wrap.removeAttribute('style');
    wrap.style.aspectRatio = '16/9';
    wrap.style.background = '#000';
    wrap.style.position = 'relative';
    wrap.style.width = '100%';
    wrap.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    
    // Header + Info restore
    const hdr = $('vidSP')?.querySelector('.sp-hdr');
    const info = $('vidInfoSection');
    if(hdr) hdr.style.display = '';
    if(info) info.style.display = '';
    
    // ytFrame reset
    if(ytFrame){
      ytFrame.style.cssText = `
        position:absolute;top:0;left:0;
        width:100%;height:100%;
        border:none;z-index:5;background:#000;
      `;
    }
    
    if(btn) btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-expand"></i>';
    document.body.style.overflow = '';
    
    // Native fullscreen bhi exit karo
    try{
      if(document.exitFullscreen) document.exitFullscreen();
      else if(document.webkitExitFullscreen) document.webkitExitFullscreen();
    }catch(e){}
    
    // Orientation unlock
    try{ screen.orientation.unlock(); }catch(e){}
    
  } else {
    // ENTER fullscreen
    
    // Header hide
    const hdr = $('vidSP')?.querySelector('.sp-hdr');
    const info = $('vidInfoSection');
    if(hdr) hdr.style.display = 'none';
    if(info) info.style.display = 'none';
    
    // vpWrap ko CSS se rotate karke landscape banao
    wrap.classList.add('yt-landscape-forced');
    
    // ytFrame fit karo
    if(ytFrame){
      ytFrame.style.cssText = `
        position:absolute;top:0;left:0;
        width:100%;height:100%;
        border:none;z-index:5;background:#000;
      `;
    }
    
    // MP4 ke liye native fullscreen try karo
    if(!ytFrame || ytFrame.style.display === 'none'){
      try{
        if(wrap.requestFullscreen){
          wrap.requestFullscreen();
        } else if(wrap.webkitRequestFullscreen){
          wrap.webkitRequestFullscreen();
        } else if(ve.webkitEnterFullscreen){
          ve.webkitEnterFullscreen();
        }
      }catch(e){}
    }
    
    // Landscape orientation lock try
    try{
      screen.orientation.lock('landscape-primary').catch(()=>{});
    }catch(e){}
    
    if(btn) btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-compress"></i>';
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    
    showVCtrl();
  }
}
// Next Video
/* ══ VIDEO ACCESS CHECKER ══ */
function canWatchVideo(v){
  if(!v) return false;
  
  // Free video — sab dekh sakte hain
  if(!v.paid) return true;
  
  // No membership — sirf free
  if(!GU || !GU.membership) return false;
  
  const plan = GU.membership;        // 'batch','pro','infinity'
  const stream = GU.membershipStream; // 'science','arts','commerce','10th'
  
  // Video ka stream match karo
  // infinity plan = stream check ki zarurat nahi, sab access
  if(plan === 'infinity') return true;
  
  // Video ka stream match karo (sirf non-infinity plans ke liye)
  if(v.stream && v.stream !== stream && stream !== 'all') return false;
  
  if(plan === 'pro'){
    // Pro aur batch level videos dekh sakta hai
    if(!v.planLevel || v.planLevel === 'batch' || v.planLevel === 'pro') return true;
    return false;
  }
  
  if(plan === 'batch'){
    // Sirf batch level videos
    if(!v.planLevel || v.planLevel === 'batch') return true;
    return false;
  }
  
  // Koi bhi paid plan hai — paid video dekh sakta hai
  return true;
}

// Accessible videos filter karo
function getAccessibleVideos(){
  if(!_recVidsAll || !_recVidsAll.length) return [];
  return _recVidsAll.filter(v => canWatchVideo(v));
}

// Next Video — sirf accessible
function vNextVideo(){
  const accessible = getAccessibleVideos();
  if(!accessible.length){
    _showSeekFlash('No Videos');
    return;
  }
  
  // Current video accessible list mein dhundho
  const curIdx = accessible.findIndex(v => v.id === _currentVidId);
  const nextIdx = curIdx + 1 >= accessible.length ? 0 : curIdx + 1;
  const next = accessible[nextIdx];
  
  if(!next){
    _showSeekFlash('No Next');
    return;
  }
  
  _showSeekFlash('Next ▶');
  switchRecVideo(next.id);
}

// Previous Video — sirf accessible
function vPrevVideo(){
  const accessible = getAccessibleVideos();
  if(!accessible.length){
    _showSeekFlash('No Videos');
    return;
  }
  
  const curIdx = accessible.findIndex(v => v.id === _currentVidId);
  const prevIdx = curIdx - 1 < 0 ? accessible.length - 1 : curIdx - 1;
  const prev = accessible[prevIdx];
  
  if(!prev){
    _showSeekFlash('No Prev');
    return;
  }
  
  _showSeekFlash('◀ Prev');
  switchRecVideo(prev.id);
}

// Auto Next — video end hone par sirf accessible mein
$('vidEl').addEventListener('ended', ()=>{
  const accessible = getAccessibleVideos();
  if(!accessible.length){
    // Koi accessible video nahi — membership prompt
    setTimeout(()=>{
      toast('Aur videos ke liye membership lo! 🎓');
    }, 500);
    return;
  }
  // 2 second baad next accessible video
  setTimeout(()=> vNextVideo(), 2000);
});

// Buffering detect
$('vidEl').addEventListener('waiting', ()=>{
  $('vidBufRing')?.classList.add('show');
});
$('vidEl').addEventListener('canplay', ()=>{
  $('vidBufRing')?.classList.remove('show');
});
$('vidEl').addEventListener('playing', ()=>{
  $('vidBufRing')?.classList.remove('show');
  $('vPlayBtn').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-pause"></i>';
});
$('vidEl').addEventListener('pause', ()=>{
  $('vPlayBtn').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-play"></i>';
  showVCtrl();
  clearTimeout(_vCtrlTO);
});

// Time update
$('vidEl').addEventListener('timeupdate', ()=>{
  if(_scrubActive) return;
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  const d = ve.duration || 0;
  const c = ve.currentTime;
  $('vCur').textContent = fmtT(c);
  $('vDur').textContent = fmtT(d);
  if(d) $('vSeek').value = (c/d)*100;
});

const SCATS=[
  {id:'all',ic:'fas fa-th-large',l:'Sab',c:'linear-gradient(135deg,#4f46e5,#7c3aed)'},
  {id:'pdf',ic:'fas fa-file-pdf',l:'PDF',c:'linear-gradient(135deg,#ef4444,#f97316)'},
  {id:'apk',ic:'fab fa-android',l:'APK',c:'linear-gradient(135deg,#10b981,#059669)'},
  {id:'video',ic:'fas fa-play-circle',l:'Video',c:'linear-gradient(135deg,#f59e0b,#ef4444)'},
  {id:'notes',ic:'fas fa-sticky-note',l:'Notes',c:'linear-gradient(135deg,#0ea5e9,#6366f1)'},
  {id:'test',ic:'fas fa-check-square',l:'Test',c:'linear-gradient(135deg,#f43f5e,#f97316)'},
];

const DSTORE=[];

function loadStoreCats(){
  $('storeCats').innerHTML=SCATS.map(c=>`
    <div class="scat" onclick="setStoreCat('${c.id}')">
      <div class="scatic" style="background:${c.c};color:#fff;"><i class="${c.ic}"></i></div>
      <p>${c.l}</p>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

let _storeOff = null;
function loadStoreItems(){
  // Default items hamesha base mein
  const base={};
  DSTORE.forEach(i=>base[i.id]=i);
  storeItems=Object.values(base);
  renderStore(storeItems);renderHomeFree();
  if(_storeOff){try{_storeOff();}catch(e){}_storeOff=null;}
  _storeOff = DB.storeItems().map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.title){delete base[key];}
    else base[key]={id:key,...data};
    storeItems=Object.values(base);
    CACHE.set('store',storeItems);
    renderStore(storeItems);
    renderHomeFree();
  });
}
function renderStore(items){
  const g=$('storeGrid');
  if(!items.length){g.innerHTML='<div class="empty" style="grid-column:1/-1;"><i class="fas fa-search"></i><p>Koi item nahi mila</p></div>';return;}
  g.innerHTML=items.map(it=>`
    <div class="stcard" onclick="openStoreItem('${it.id}')">
      <div class="stthmb">
        ${it.imgUrl?`<img src="${it.imgUrl}" alt="" loading="lazy">`:`<i class="${it.ic||'fas fa-file'}"></i>`}
        <div class="sttype"><i class="fas fa-${it.type==='pdf'?'file-pdf':it.type==='apk'?'android':it.type==='video'?'play-circle':'file'}"></i> ${(it.type||'FILE').toUpperCase()}</div>
        ${it.locked?'<div class="stlck"><i class="fas fa-lock"></i></div>':''}
      </div>
      <div class="stbody">
        <h4>${esc(it.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc(it.desc||'')}</p>
        <div class="stars">${'★'.repeat(Math.round(it.rating||4))}${'☆'.repeat(5-Math.round(it.rating||4))} <span style="color:var(--txm);font-size:9px;">${it.rating||4.5}</span></div>
        <div class="stprice ${it.locked?'':'free'}"><i class="fas fa-${it.locked?'lock':'unlock'}"></i> ${it.locked?'Members Only':(it.price||'Free')}</div>
        <button class="instbtn" onclick="event.stopPropagation();doInstall('${it.id}')">
          <i class="fas fa-${it.locked?'lock':'download'}"></i> ${it.locked?'Unlock':'Install/Open'}
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function renderHomeFree(){
  const free=storeItems.filter(i=>!i.locked).slice(0,4);
  const g=$('homeFree');if(!g)return;
  g.innerHTML=free.map(it=>`
    <div class="stcard" onclick="openStoreItem('${it.id}')">
      <div class="stthmb"><i class="${it.ic||'fas fa-file'}"></i><div class="sttype">${(it.type||'').toUpperCase()}</div></div>
      <div class="stbody"><h4>${esc(it.title)}</h4><div class="stprice free"><i class="fas fa-unlock"></i> Free</div></div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function loadHomeFree(){renderHomeFree();}
function setStoreCat(cat){
  storeCat=cat;
  const q=$('storeSrch').value.toLowerCase();
  let f=storeItems;
  if(cat!=='all')f=f.filter(i=>i.type===cat);
  if(q)f=f.filter(i=>(i.title||'').toLowerCase().includes(q));
  renderStore(f);
  // Amazon card sirf 'all' mein dikhe
  const amzCard=$('storeAmzCard');
  if(amzCard)amzCard.style.display=cat==='all'?'block':'none';
}
function filterStore(q){
  q=(q||'').toLowerCase();
  let f=storeItems;
  if(storeCat!=='all')f=f.filter(i=>i.type===storeCat);
  if(q)f=f.filter(i=>(i.title||'').toLowerCase().includes(q)||(i.desc||'').toLowerCase().includes(q));
  renderStore(f);
  // Amazon card search mein bhi hide karo
  const amzCard=$('storeAmzCard');
  if(amzCard)amzCard.style.display=(!q&&storeCat==='all')?'block':'none';
}
function openStoreItem(id){
  const it=storeItems.find(i=>i.id===id);if(!it)return;
  
  // Direct open karo — type ke hisaab se
  GU && GU.membership === 'active';
  const locked = it.locked && !hasMem;
  
  if(locked){ openMem(); return; }
  
  // PDF
  if(it.type === 'pdf' || it.pdfUrl){
    const url = it.url || it.pdfUrl || '';
    if(!url){ toast('PDF abhi available nahi'); return; }
    openPDFViewer(it.title, it.desc||'', url, url);
    return;
  }
  
  // Video
  if(it.type === 'video'){
    const url = it.url || it.videoUrl || '';
    if(!url){ toast('Video abhi available nahi'); return; }
    $('vidTitle').textContent = it.title || 'Video';
    $('vidFull').textContent = it.title || '';
    $('vidDesc').textContent = it.desc || '';
    const ve = $('vidEl');
    ve.src = '';
    openSP('vidSP');
    _showVidSpinner();
    setTimeout(()=>{
      ve.src = url;
      ve.load();
      ve.oncanplay = ()=>{ _hideVidSpinner(); ve.play().catch(()=>{}); adjustVideoSize(ve); };
      ve.onerror = ()=>{ _hideVidSpinner(); };
    }, 150);
    loadRecommendedVideos('', it);
    return;
  }
  
  // APK
  if(it.type === 'apk'){
    showApkPopup(it);
    return;
  }
  
  // Notes / Test / Default
  if(it.url || it.pdfUrl){
    openPDFViewer(it.title, it.desc||'', it.url||it.pdfUrl, it.url||it.pdfUrl);
    return;
  }
  
  // Kuch nahi — modal dikhao
  selItem=it;
  $('smThm').innerHTML=it.imgUrl?`<img src="${it.imgUrl}" alt="">`:`<i class="${it.ic||'fas fa-file'}"></i>`;
  $('smTitle').textContent=it.title||'';
  $('smDesc').textContent=it.desc||'';
  $('smMeta').innerHTML=`<span><i class="fas fa-download"></i> ${it.dl||'N/A'}</span><span><i class="fas fa-hdd"></i> ${it.size||'N/A'}</span><span><i class="fas fa-star" style="color:var(--warn)"></i> ${it.rating||4.5}</span>`;
  const btn=$('smActBtn');
  btn.innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-download"></i> Download';
  btn.onclick=()=>{
    const url=it.url||it.pdfUrl;
    if(url) window.open(url,'_blank');
    else toast('Link abhi available nahi');
  };
  openOv('smOv');
}

function doInstall(id){
  const it = storeItems.find(i => i.id === id);
  if(!it) return;
  if(it.locked && !GU.membership){ openMem(); return; }
  
  // APK
  if(it.type === 'apk'){
    showApkPopup(it);
    return;
  }
  
  // PDF / Notes
  if(it.type === 'pdf' || it.type === 'notes' || it.pdfUrl){
    const url = it.url || it.pdfUrl || '';
    if(!url){ toast('PDF abhi available nahi'); return; }
    openPDFViewer(it.title, it.desc||'', url, url);
    return;
  }
  
  // Video
  if(it.type === 'video'){
    const url = it.url || it.videoUrl || '';
    if(!url){ toast('Video abhi available nahi'); return; }
    $('vidTitle').textContent = it.title || 'Video';
    $('vidFull').textContent = it.title || '';
    $('vidDesc').textContent = it.desc || '';
    const ve = $('vidEl');
    ve.src = '';
    openSP('vidSP');
    _showVidSpinner();
    setTimeout(()=>{
      ve.src = url;
      ve.load();
      ve.oncanplay = ()=>{ _hideVidSpinner(); ve.play().catch(()=>{}); adjustVideoSize(ve); };
    }, 150);
    return;
  }
  
  // Default
  const url = it.url || it.pdfUrl;
  if(url) window.open(url, '_blank');
  else toast(it.title + ' — Link admin se milega 📥');
}

// Admin Plans GUN path
const DB_PLANS=()=>gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('adminPlans');

// Cache for loaded plans
let _adminPlansCache = {};

function renderPlans(stream){
  activePlanStream=stream;
  // Default fallback
  const defaultList=PLANS[stream]||PLANS.science;

  // Pehle default render karo
  _renderPlanCards(defaultList, stream);

  // GUN se admin plans load karo
  DB_PLANS().get(stream).on(data=>{
    if(!data) return;
    const merged = defaultList.map((p,i)=>{
      const key = i===0?'basic':'premium';
      const adminPlan = data[key];
      if(adminPlan && adminPlan.features){
        return {
          ...p,
          n: adminPlan.name || p.n,
          o: adminPlan.origPrice || p.o,
          p: adminPlan.price || p.p,
          f: (adminPlan.features||'').split('\n').filter(x=>x.trim()),
          desc: adminPlan.desc || ''
        };
      }
      return p;
    });
    _adminPlansCache[stream] = merged;
    _renderPlanCards(merged, stream);
  });
}

function _renderPlanCards(list,stream){
  $('planCon').innerHTML=`
  <div style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:14px;">
    <div style="display:inline-block;background:var(--g1);color:#fff;border-radius:20px;padding:5px 16px;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;">
      <i class="fas fa-graduation-cap" style="margin-right:6px;"></i>UTKAL +2 BATCH 2026
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Plan Cards Horizontal Scroll -->
  <div style="display:flex;gap:11px;overflow-x:auto;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:18px;scrollbar-width:none;margin-bottom:16px;">

  ${list.map((p,i)=>{
    let finalPrice=p.p;
    if(promoApplied&&promoDiscount>0) finalPrice=Math.round(p.p*(1-promoDiscount/100));
    const saving=p.p-finalPrice;
    const isPopular=p.tag&&p.tag.includes('Popular');
    const isBest=p.tag&&p.tag.includes('Value');
    const bgGrad=isPopular?'var(--g2)':isBest?'var(--g1)':'linear-gradient(135deg,#374151,#1f2937)';
    return`<div style="min-width:200px;background:${bgGrad};border-radius:var(--r);padding:16px 14px;color:#fff;position:relative;flex-shrink:0;box-shadow:var(--e2);">
      ${p.tag?`<div style="position:absolute;top:-10px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);background:#fff;color:${isPopular?'var(--s)':'var(--p)'};font-size:10px;font-weight:800;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:20px;white-space:nowrap;box-shadow:var(--e1);">${p.tag}</div>`:''}
      <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:16px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:4px;margin-top:${p.tag?'14px':'0'};">${p.n}</div>

      <div style="font-size:11px;opacity:.8;text-decoration:line-through;">₹${p.o}</div>
      <div style="font-size:26px;font-weight:800;font-family:var(--fdisp);line-height:1.1;">₹${finalPrice}</div>
      <div style="font-size:10px;opacity:.8;margin-bottom:10px;">/ ${p.per}</div>
      ${saving>0?`<div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);border-radius:8px;padding:3px 8px;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;">🎉 ₹${saving} OFF!</div>`:''}
<button onclick="selectPlan('${p.key}',${finalPrice},'${stream}')"
        style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:none;border-radius:10px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.92);color:${isPopular?'var(--s)':isBest?'var(--p)':'#1f2937'};font-size:12px;font-weight:800;cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--font);transition:all .2s;">
        ${p.btn}
      </button>
    </div>`;
  }).join('')}
  </div>

  <!-- Comparison Table -->
  <div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);overflow:hidden;margin-bottom:14px;">

    <!-- Header Row -->
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr repeat(${list.length},60px);background:var(--g1);padding:10px 12px;gap:4px;align-items:center;">
      <div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:#fff;opacity:.85;">Features</div>
      ${list.map(p=>`<div style="text-align:center;font-size:10px;font-weight:800;color:#fff;line-height:1.3;">${p.n}</div>`).join('')}
    </div>

    <!-- Feature Rows -->
    ${list[0].f.map(cat=>`
      <!-- Category Header -->
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:7px;padding:9px 12px;background:var(--sur3);border-top:1.5px solid var(--bd);">
        <i class="${cat.ic}" style="color:var(--p);font-size:13px;"></i>
        <span style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx);">${cat.cat}</span>
      </div>
      <!-- Items -->
      ${cat.items.map(item=>{
        return`<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr repeat(${list.length},60px);padding:8px 12px;gap:4px;align-items:center;border-top:1px solid var(--bd);">
          <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--txm);line-height:1.4;">${item.l}</div>
          ${list.map(p=>{
            const catIdx=list[0].f.findIndex(c=>c.cat===cat.cat);
            const planCat=p.f[catIdx];
            const planItem=planCat?planCat.items.find(x=>x.l===item.l):null;
            const has=planItem?planItem.h:false;
            return`<div style="text-align:center;">
              <i class="fas fa-${has?'check-circle':'times-circle'}" style="font-size:14px;color:${has?'var(--ok)':'var(--err)'};opacity:${has?1:.4};"></i>
            </div>`;
          }).join('')}
        </div>`;
      }).join('')}
    `).join('')}
  </div>

  <!-- Bottom Urgency -->
  <div style="background:var(--g4);border-radius:var(--r2);padding:11px 14px;text-align:center;color:#fff;margin-bottom:10px;">
    <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:3px;">🔥 Limited Seats Only (50 Students)</div>
    <div style="font-size:11px;opacity:.9;">⏳ Offer Ending Soon — Abhi Join Karo!</div>
  </div>
  `;
}
function switchPlan(s,btn){
  document.querySelectorAll('#planTabs .tbtn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');renderPlans(s);
}

function checkRefCode(code){
  if(!code||code.length<5){usedRef=null;discountApplied=false;$('discC').classList.remove('show');return;}
  DB.users().map().once((data,key)=>{
    if(data&&data.referralCode===code&&key!==CU?.uid){
      usedRef={uid:key,code};discountApplied=true;
      $('discC').classList.add('show');
      $('discMsg').textContent='₹10 discount mila! Code: '+code+' ✅';
      renderPlans(activePlanStream);
    }
  });
}


/* ══ PROMO CODE SYSTEM ══ */
const DB_PROMO=()=>gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('promoCodes');

function checkPromoLive(val){
  const msg=$('promoMsg');
  if(!val||val.length<3){msg.style.display='none';return;}
  // Sirf uppercase show karo
  $('promoInp').value=val.toUpperCase();
}

async function applyPromoCode(){
  const code = $('promoInp').value.trim().toUpperCase();
  if(!code){ _showPromoMsg('Code daalo pehle','warn'); return; }
  if(!CU){ toast('Pehle login karo'); return; }

  _showPromoMsg('🔍 Checking...','info');

  const applyBtn = document.querySelector('#promoSection .btn.bp');
  if(applyBtn){ applyBtn.disabled=true; applyBtn.innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>'; }

  const tryLoad = () => new Promise(resolve => {
    let done = false;
    DB_PROMO().get(code).once(d => {
      if(done) return;
      if(d !== null && d !== undefined){ done=true; resolve(d); }
    });
    const off = DB_PROMO().get(code).on(d => {
      if(done) return;
      if(d !== null && d !== undefined){ done=true; try{off();}catch(e){} resolve(d); }
    });
    setTimeout(() => { if(!done){ done=true; try{off();}catch(e){} resolve(null); } }, 4000);
  });

  let data = await tryLoad();
  if(!data){
    _showPromoMsg('⏳ Dobara try kar raha hai...','info');
    await new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,1500));
    data = await tryLoad();
  }

  if(applyBtn){ applyBtn.disabled=false; applyBtn.innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Apply'; }

  // ❌ Code exist nahi
  if(!data || data._deleted === true || !data.code){
    _showPromoMsg('❌ Code exist nahi karta — Sahi code daalo','err');
    return;
  }

  // ❌ Limit check
  const usedCount = parseInt(data.usedCount)||0;
  const maxUse = parseInt(data.maxUse)||0;
  if(maxUse > 0 && usedCount >= maxUse){
    _showPromoMsg('❌ Is code ki limit khatam ho gayi','err');
    return;
  }

  // ❌ Discount valid?
  const discount = parseInt(data.discount)||0;
  if(discount <= 0 || discount > 100){
    _showPromoMsg('❌ Invalid code','err');
    return;
  }

  // ❌ Same user ne pehle use kiya?
  const usedBy = data.usedBy || {};
  if(usedBy[CU.uid]){
    _showPromoMsg('❌ Aap yeh code pehle already use kar chuke hain — Dobara use nahi hoga! ⚠️','err');
    // Alert bhi dikhao
    setTimeout(()=>{
      caAlert('Code Already Used!', `Aapne "${code}" code pehle already use kar liya hai. Ek baar use kiya hua code dobara nahi lagega.`);
    }, 300);
    return;
  }

  // ✅ VALID — Apply karo
  const promoSaveData = {
    code: code,
    discount: discount,
    appliedAt: Date.now(),
    savedBy: CU.uid
  };

  promoApplied = true;
  promoDiscount = discount;
  promoCode = code;
  promoData = data;

  // Save karo — dono jagah
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').put(promoSaveData);
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid, JSON.stringify(promoSaveData));

  // UI update
  if($('promoInputWrap')) $('promoInputWrap').style.display='none';
  if($('promoSuccess')){
    $('promoSuccess').style.display='flex';
    $('promoSuccessMsg').textContent=`${discount}% OFF Apply Ho Gaya! 🎉`;
    $('promoSuccessDesc').textContent=`Code: ${code} — 24 ghante mein expire hoga ⏰`;
  }
  _showPromoMsg('','hide');
  renderPlans(activePlanStream);

  // 24hr expiry timer start karo
  _startPromoExpiryTimer(24*60*60*1000);
  // Admin watch start karo
  _watchActivePromo(code);

  toast(`✅ ${discount}% OFF apply ho gaya! Code: ${code}`);
}
function showPromoMsg(msg,type){
  const el=$('promoMsg');
  if(type==='hide'||!msg){el.style.display='none';return;}
  el.style.display='block';
  const colors={info:'var(--p)',warn:'var(--warn)',error:'var(--err)',ok:'var(--ok)'};
  el.style.color=colors[type]||'var(--txm)';
  el.innerHTML=`<i class="fas fa-${type==='error'?'times-circle':type==='ok'?'check-circle':'info-circle'}"></i> ${msg}`;
}
function removePromo(){
  promoApplied=false; promoDiscount=0; promoCode=''; promoData=null;

  if(_promoWatchOff){ try{_promoWatchOff();}catch(e){} _promoWatchOff=null; }

  if(CU){
    DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('activePromo').put(null);
    // ✅ LocalStorage bhi clear karo
    localStorage.removeItem('esv07_activePromo_'+CU.uid);
  }

  _clearPromoState();
  renderPlans(activePlanStream);
  toast('Promo code remove ho gaya');
}

// selectPlan mein promo use record karo
// Existing selectPlan ke andar submitPayment ke saath yeh add hoga automatically
function recordPromoUse(code, uid){
  if(!code || !uid) return;
  DB_PROMO().get(code).once(data=>{
    if(!data) return;
    const usedBy = data.usedBy || {};
    usedBy[uid] = Date.now();
    DB_PROMO().get(code).put({
      ...data,
      usedCount: (data.usedCount||0) + 1,
      usedBy: usedBy
    });
    // Payment ke baad activePromo clear karo — 24hr expiry bhi remove
    DB.users().get(uid).get('activePromo').put(null);
    localStorage.removeItem('esv07_activePromo_'+uid);
    clearTimeout(window._promoExpTO);
  });
}
