`;

// QR video load karo GUN se
let _qrVidLoaded = false;
const _qrVidRef = DB.settings().get('qrVideo').on(vData => {
  if(_qrVidLoaded) return;
  const inner = document.getElementById('qrVidInner');
  const empty = document.getElementById('qrVidEmpty');
  if(!inner) return;
  if(!vData || !vData.url) return;
  _qrVidLoaded = true;
  try{ _qrVidRef.off(); }catch(e){}
  empty.style.display = 'none';
  const isYT = vData.url.includes('youtube.com') || vData.url.includes('youtu.be');
  if(isYT){
    const m = vData.url.match(/(?:v=|youtu\.be\/)([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{11})/);
    const ytId = m ? m[1] : '';
    if(!ytId) return;
    inner.innerHTML = `<iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/${ytId}?controls=0&modestbranding=1&rel=0" 
      style="width:100%;height:100%;border:none;" allow="autoplay;encrypted-media" allowfullscreen></iframe>`;
  } else {
    inner.innerHTML = `<video src="${vData.url}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;" 
      controls playsinline preload="metadata"></video>`;
  }
});
  ssImgUrl=null;ssXHR=null;
  ['payName','payUpi','payMobile','payRef'].forEach(id=>{if($(id))$(id).value='';});
  if($('ssIn'))$('ssIn').value='';
  if($('ssUploadBtn'))$('ssUploadBtn').style.display='flex';
  if($('ssPreviewWrap'))$('ssPreviewWrap').style.display='none';
  if($('ssLoadWrap'))$('ssLoadWrap').style.display='none';
  if($('ssFill'))$('ssFill').style.width='0';
  if($('paySubmitBtn')){
    $('paySubmitBtn').disabled=true;
    $('paySubmitBtn').innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-lock"></i> Pehle Screenshot Upload Karo';
  }
  discountApplied=false;usedRef=null;
  $('discC').classList.remove('show');
  openOv('payOv');
}


let ssXHR=null;
function handleSS(e){
  const file=e.target.files[0];if(!file)return;
  // Show loading
  $('ssUploadBtn').style.display='none';
  $('ssPreviewWrap').style.display='none';
  $('ssLoadWrap').style.display='block';
  $('ssFill').style.width='0';
  $('ssLoadTxt').textContent='Uploading...';
  $('paySubmitBtn').disabled=true;
  ssImgUrl=null;

  const form=new FormData();form.append('image',file);
  const xhr=new XMLHttpRequest();ssXHR=xhr;
  xhr.open('POST',`https://api.imgbb.com/1/upload?key=${IMGBB}`);
  xhr.upload.onprogress=ev=>{
    if(ev.lengthComputable){
      const pct=Math.round(ev.loaded/ev.total*100);
      $('ssFill').style.width=pct+'%';
      $('ssLoadTxt').textContent='Uploading... '+pct+'%';
    }
  };
  xhr.onload=()=>{
    ssXHR=null;
    try{
      const d=JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
      ssImgUrl=d.data.url;
      $('ssprev').src=ssImgUrl;
      $('ssLoadWrap').style.display='none';
      $('ssPreviewWrap').style.display='block';
      $('paySubmitBtn').disabled=false;
      $('paySubmitBtn').innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i> Payment Request Bhejo';
      toast('Screenshot ready! ✅');
    }catch{
      cancelSS();toast('Upload fail hua — Try again');
    }
  };
  xhr.onerror=()=>{ssXHR=null;cancelSS();toast('Upload fail hua');};
  xhr.send(form);
}

function cancelSS(){
  if(ssXHR){ssXHR.abort();ssXHR=null;}
  ssImgUrl=null;
  $('ssIn').value='';
  $('ssLoadWrap').style.display='none';
  $('ssPreviewWrap').style.display='none';
  $('ssUploadBtn').style.display='flex';
  $('paySubmitBtn').disabled=true;
  toast('Screenshot cancel ho gaya');
}

function submitPayment(){
  if(!CU){doLogin();return;}
  const name=($('payName').value||'').trim();
  const upi=($('payUpi').value||'').trim();
  const mobile=($('payMobile').value||'').trim();
  const ref=($('payRef').value||'').trim();
  if(!name){toast('ନିଜର ନାମ ଲେଖନ୍ତୁ ✍️');return;}
  if(!upi){toast('ଆପଣଙ୍କ ଏକାଉଣ୍ଡରେ ଥିବା ନାମ ଲେଖନ୍ତୁ 💳');return;}
  if(!ssImgUrl){toast('ସ୍ରିନସଟ ଅପଲୋଡ କରନ୍ତୁ! 📸');return;}

  // Button loading
  $('paySubmitBtn').disabled=true;
  $('paySubmitBtn').innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Bhej Raha Hai...';

  const reqId='pay_'+Date.now()+'_'+CU.uid.substring(0,6);
  const req={
    id:reqId,
    userId:CU.uid,
    userName:name||GU.name||'User',
    userPhoto:GU.photo||CU.photoURL||DAV,
    plan:selPlan?.plan,
    amount:selPlan?.price,
    stream:selPlan?.stream,
    upiId:upi,
    mobile:mobile||'',
    screenshot:ssImgUrl,
    usedRefCode:usedRef?.code||ref||'',
refUid:usedRef?.uid||'',
promoCode:promoCode||'',
    status:'pending',
    membershipExpiry: getOneYearFromNow(),
    membershipStream: selPlan?.stream,
    membershipPlan: selPlan?.planKey||selPlan?.plan,
    ts:Date.now()
  };
  DB.paymentRequests().get(reqId).put(req);

// ✅ Admin tak pohanchane ke liye:
gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('memRequests').get(CU.uid).put({
  uid: CU.uid,
  name: name || GU.name || 'User',
  email: CU.email || '',
  stream: selPlan?.stream,
  plan: selPlan?.planKey || selPlan?.plan,
  status: 'pending',
  amount: selPlan?.price,
  screenshot: ssImgUrl,
  requestedAt: Date.now()
});
DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('membership').put('pending');
GU.membership = 'pending';
GU.membershipStream = selPlan?.stream;
GU.membershipPlan = selPlan?.planKey || selPlan?.plan;

// Yeh line add karo submitPayment ke andar DB.paymentRequests ke baad:
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('pendingPlan').put({
    plan: selPlan?.planKey || selPlan?.plan,
    stream: selPlan?.stream,
    amount: selPlan?.price,
    reqId: reqId,
    ts: Date.now()
  });

  // Promo use record
  if(promoApplied&&promoCode&&CU){
    recordPromoUse(promoCode,CU.uid);
  }

  // Admin chat mein message bhejo with all details
  const chatId=getChatId(CU.uid,ADMIN_UID);
  const msgId='pmsg_'+Date.now();
  const msgText=`💳 PAYMENT REQUEST\n━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n👤 Naam: ${name}\n📱 UPI: ${upi}${mobile?'\n📞 Mobile: '+mobile:''}${ref?'\n🎁 Ref Code: '+ref:''}${promoCode?'\n🎟️ Promo: '+promoCode:''}\n💰 Amount: ₹${selPlan?.price}\n📚 Plan: ${selPlan?.plan} (${selPlan?.stream})\n━━━━━━━━━━━━━━`;

  const payMsg={
    id:msgId,
    senderId:CU.uid,
    senderName:GU.name||'User',
    senderPhoto:GU.photo||DAV,
    text:msgText,
    img:ssImgUrl,
    seen:false,
    ts:Date.now(),
    isPayReq:true
  };
  DB.chats().get(chatId).get(msgId).put(payMsg);

  // ✅ Cache mein save karo — chat open hone par turant bubble dikhega
  chatAllLoaded.add(msgId);
  chatMsgsList.push(payMsg);
  chatMsgsList.sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts);
  CACHE.set('msgs_'+CU.uid, chatMsgsList.slice(-100));

  // Referral reward
  // Referral reward — per new user sirf ek baar

  if(usedRef?.uid && CU?.uid){
    // CU (new user) ne pehle kisi ka bhi referral use kiya hai check karo
    DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('referralUsed').once(alreadyUsed=>{
      if(alreadyUsed){
        // Is user ne pehle hi kisi ka referral use kar liya tha
        return;
      }
      // Reward dene wale ka data lo
      DB.users().get(usedRef.uid).once(d=>{
        if(!d)return;
        // CU ke account mein mark karo — referral use ho gaya
        DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('referralUsed').put({
          by: usedRef.uid,
          code: usedRef.code,
          at: Date.now()
        });
        // Referring user ko reward do
        DB.users().get(usedRef.uid).put({
          ...d,
          referrals:(d.referrals||0)+1,
          earnings:(d.earnings||0)+29
        });
      });
    });
  }

  startPayTimer(CU.uid);

  // Popup band karo, chat kholo
  closeOv('payOv');
  toast('Payment request bhej di! ✅');

  setTimeout(()=>{
    openAdminChat();
    setTimeout(()=>toast('Screenshot + details admin ko bhej diya gaya! 📤'),600);
  },400);
}
 
  

function startPayTimer(uid){
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_payStart_'+uid,Date.now());
  let secs=3600;
  $('payTimer').classList.add('show');
  clearInterval(payTimerInt);
  payTimerInt=setInterval(()=>{
    secs--;
    if(secs<=0){clearInterval(payTimerInt);$('payTimer').classList.remove('show');return;}
    const m=Math.floor(secs/60),s=secs%60;
    $('payTimerTxt').textContent=`Verify ho raha hai... ${m}:${s<10?'0':''}${s}`;
  },1000);
}

function checkPayTimer(uid){
  const start=parseInt(localStorage.getItem('esv07_payStart_'+uid)||'0');
  if(!start)return;
  const rem=3600-Math.floor((Date.now()-start)/1000);
  if(rem>0){
    let secs=rem;$('payTimer').classList.add('show');clearInterval(payTimerInt);
    payTimerInt=setInterval(()=>{
      secs--;
      if(secs<=0){clearInterval(payTimerInt);$('payTimer').classList.remove('show');localStorage.removeItem('esv07_payStart_'+uid);return;}
      const m=Math.floor(secs/60),s=secs%60;
      $('payTimerTxt').textContent=`Verify ho raha hai... ${m}:${s<10?'0':''}${s}`;
    },1000);
  }
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   REFERRAL
══════════════════════════════════════ */
function copyRef(){
  const c=$('refDisp').textContent;
  navigator.clipboard?.writeText(c).then(()=>toast('Code copy ho gaya! 📋')).catch(()=>{
    // Fallback
    const ta=document.createElement('textarea');ta.value=c;document.body.appendChild(ta);ta.select();document.execCommand('copy');document.body.removeChild(ta);toast('Copied!');
  });
  closeOv('refOv');
}
function shareRef(){
  if(!CU)return;
  const c=$('refDisp').textContent;
  const msg=`EduSagar join karo — India ka best study platform! 🎓\nMera code ${c} use karo ₹10 off ke liye.\n${window.location.href}`;
  if(navigator.share){navigator.share({title:'EduSagar',text:msg}).catch(()=>{});}
  else copyRef();
  closeOv('refOv');
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   AI ADMIN CHAT
══════════════════════════════════════ */
let chatAllLoaded=new Set(),chatMsgsList=[];

function initAdminChat(){
  if(!CU)return;
  const msgs=$('chatMsgs');
  // Poora clear karo
  msgs.innerHTML='';
  chatAllLoaded=new Set();
  chatMsgsList=[];

  const chatId=getChatId(CU.uid,ADMIN_UID);
  if(chatGunOff){chatGunOff();chatGunOff=null;}

  // Pehle cache se load karo — instant
  const cached=CACHE.getStale('msgs_'+CU.uid);
  if(cached&&cached.length){
    cached.sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts).forEach(m=>{
      if(!deletedMsgs.has(m.id)){
        chatAllLoaded.add(m.id);
        chatMsgsList.push(m);
        renderBubble(m);
      }
    });
  }

  // GUN se live updates
  const tempMsgs={};
  chatGunOff=DB.chats().get(chatId).map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.ts||deletedMsgs.has(key))return;
    tempMsgs[key]={id:key,...data};
    clearTimeout(window._chatRenderTO);
    window._chatRenderTO=setTimeout(()=>{
      const sorted=Object.values(tempMsgs).sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts);
      sorted.forEach(m=>{
        if(!chatAllLoaded.has(m.id)){
          chatAllLoaded.add(m.id);
          chatMsgsList.push(m);
          renderBubble(m);
        }
      });
      CACHE.set('msgs_'+CU.uid,sorted.slice(-100));
    },500);
    // Seen update
    if(data.seen&&chatAllLoaded.has(key)){
      const si=document.getElementById('seen_'+key);
      if(si)si.innerHTML='<i class="fas fa-check-double" style="color:#7dd3fc;"></i>';
    }
    if(data.senderId!==CU.uid&&!data.seen){
      DB.chats().get(chatId).get(key).get('seen').put(true);
    }
  });

  // Agar koi message nahi toh welcome dikhao
  setTimeout(()=>{
    if(chatMsgsList.length===0&&Object.keys(tempMsgs).length===0){
      showWelcomeMsg();
    }
  },1500);
}
  

function showWelcomeMsg(){
  const msgs=$('chatMsgs');if(!msgs||!CU)return;
  const ti=$('tyInd');if(ti){ti.querySelector('span').textContent='AI typing';}
  setTimeout(()=>{
    if(ti)ti.classList.remove('show');
    const wMsg={
      id:'welcome_'+CU.uid.substring(0,8),
      senderId:ADMIN_UID,senderName:'EduSagar AI',senderPhoto:genAv('AI'),
      text:`Namaste ${GU.name||CU.displayName||''}! 🙏\n\nMain EduSagar AI Assistant hoon. Aap mujhse kuch bhi puch sakte hain:\n\n📚 Books aur PYQ ke baare mein\n🎬 Video lectures kaise dekhen\n💳 Membership kaise lein\n🎁 Referral code kaise use karein\n\nKaise help kar sakta hoon? 😊`,
      seen:true,ts:Date.now(),isAI:true
    };
    renderBubble(wMsg);
    // Save to GUN
    const chatId=getChatId(CU.uid,ADMIN_UID);
    DB.chats().get(chatId).get(wMsg.id).put(wMsg);
  },1500);
}

async function sendMsg(){
  const inp=$('msgInp');const txt=inp.value.trim();
  if(!txt&&!selImg)return;
  if(!CU){toast('Pehle login karo');return;}
  $('sndBtn').disabled=true;
  const chatId=getChatId(CU.uid,ADMIN_UID);
  const msgId='m'+Date.now()+Math.random().toString(36).substring(2,5);
  const msg={
    id:msgId,senderId:CU.uid,senderName:GU.name||CU.displayName||'User',
    senderPhoto:GU.photo||CU.photoURL||DAV,
    text:txt,img:selImg||null,seen:false,ts:Date.now()
  };
  
DB.chats().get(chatId).get(msgId).put(msg);

  // Turant bubble dikhao
  renderBubble(msg);

  // ✅ Cache mein save karo — reopen par bhi dikhega
  chatAllLoaded.add(msgId);
  chatMsgsList.push(msg);
  chatMsgsList.sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts);
  CACHE.set('msgs_'+CU.uid, chatMsgsList.slice(-100));

  const msgs=$('chatMsgs');
  if(msgs) msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;

  inp.value='';selImg=null;
  $('sndBtn').disabled=false;

  // AI Response
  if(txt){
    const ti=$('tyInd');
    if(ti){ti.querySelector('span').textContent='AI typing';ti.classList.add('show');}
    setTimeout(()=>generateAIResponse(txt,chatId),800);
  }
}

async function generateAIResponse(userMsg,chatId){
  let response='';
  // Try API key from settings
  let aiKey='';
  await new Promise(res=>{DB.settings().get('aiKey').once(k=>{if(k)aiKey=k;res();});setTimeout(res,400);});
  if(aiKey){
    try{
      const r=await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages',{
        method:'POST',
        headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json','x-api-key':aiKey,'anthropic-version':'2023-06-01'},
        body:JSON.stringify({model:'claude-haiku-4-5-20251001',max_tokens:400,system:AI_SYSTEM,messages:[{role:'user',content:userMsg}]})
      });
      const d=await r.json();
      response=d.content?.[0]?.text||'';
    }catch{}
  }
  if(!response)response=smartReply(userMsg);
  const ti=$('tyInd');if(ti)ti.classList.remove('show');
  const aiId='ai'+Date.now();
  DB.chats().get(chatId).get(aiId).put({
    id:aiId,senderId:ADMIN_UID,senderName:'EduSagar AI',senderPhoto:genAv('AI'),
    text:response,seen:true,ts:Date.now(),isAI:true
  });
}

function smartReply(msg){
  const m=msg.toLowerCase();
  if(/member|premium|plan|join|fee|cost|price/.test(m))
    return'Membership ke liye Premium button dabao ya plans sheet open karo. Science/Arts/Commerce ₹499 Basic, ₹999 Premium. 10th ₹399 se shuru. Saari PYQ, Books, Videos unlock ho jaengi! 💎';
  if(/pyq|previous|paper|board/.test(m))
    return'PYQ (Previous Year Questions) Books tab mein milenge. Free wale bina login ke padh sakte ho. Premium PYQ ke liye membership chahiye. Download button bhi hai! 📄';
  if(/book|pdf|ncert|notes/.test(m))
    return'Books aur PDFs Books tab mein milte hain. NCERT se reference books tak sab available hai. Download button se save kar sakte ho. Premium books ke liye membership lo. 📚';
  if(/video|lecture|class/.test(m))
    return'Video lectures Books tab mein milte hain. Free videos seedha dekh sakte ho. Premium videos ke liye membership chahiye. HD quality mein available hain! 🎬';
  if(/refer|code|friend|share/.test(m))
    return'Profile tab mein apna referral code milega. Code share karo — friend ko ₹10 off aur aapko ₹29 ka reward milega! Jitne zyada friends, utna zyada earning! 🎁';
  if(/pay|upi|payment|screenshot/.test(m))
    return'Payment ke liye: 1) Premium button dabao 2) Plan chunein 3) UPI se pay karo 4) Screenshot yahan bhejo. Admin 24 ghante mein verify karega aur membership activate kar dega! 💳';
  if(/login|sign|google|account/.test(m))
    return'Login ke liye: Menu (⋮) mein jaao → Login/Sign Up dabao → Google se login karo. Ek click mein ho jaata hai! 🔐';
  if(/download|dl|install/.test(m))
    return'Download karne ke liye: Books/PYQ card ke side mein download button (⬇) hai. Free content bina membership ke download ho sakta hai. Premium content ke liye membership chahiye. 📥';
  if(/amazon|buy|kharid/.test(m))
    return'Books tab mein Amazon section hai! Recommended books wahan se kharido — best deals milte hain. Is link se kharidne par EduSagar ko bhi support milta hai. 🛒';
  if(/hello|hi|namaste|helo|hey/.test(m))
    return`Namaste! 🙏 Main EduSagar AI hoon. Kaise help kar sakta hoon?\n\n• Membership ke baare mein\n• Books/PYQ download\n• Video lectures\n• Payment help`;
  if(/thank|dhanyawad|shukriya|acha|nice|great/.test(m))
    return'Aapka swagat hai! 😊 Koi bhi sawaal ho toh zaroor puchein. EduSagar ke saath padhai aur achi ho! 🎓';
  return`Samajh gaya! 🤔 Iske baare mein main aapki madad karunga.\n\nAap specifically puchein jaise:\n• "PYQ kaise download karein"\n• "Membership kaise lein"\n• "Konsa plan better hai"\n\nAdmin bhi yahan available hain aur jaldi reply karenge! 👨‍💼`;
}

function onMsgKey(e){if(e.key==='Enter'&&!e.shiftKey){sendMsg();}}

function renderBubble(data){
  if(!CU)return;
  const msgs=$('chatMsgs');
  if(!msgs||document.getElementById('row_'+data.id))return;
  if(deletedMsgs.has(data.id))return;
  const isMine=data.senderId===CU.uid;
  const isAI=data.isAI||data.senderId===ADMIN_UID;
  const av=isMine?(GU.photo||CU.photoURL||DAV):(data.senderPhoto||genAv('Admin'));
  const row=document.createElement('div');
  row.className='mrow '+(isMine?'sent':'recv');
  row.id='row_'+data.id;
  row.innerHTML=`
    <img class="mavsm" src="${av}" alt="" onerror="this.src='${DAV}'" loading="lazy">
    <div>
      <div class="bbl ${isMine?'sent':(isAI?'ai-msg':'recv')}" id="bbl_${data.id}">
        ${data.img?`<img src="${data.img}" alt="" loading="lazy" onclick="event.stopPropagation();openImgPopup('${data.img}')">`:''}
        ${data.isPayReq?`<div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.15);border-radius:8px;padding:6px 9px;margin-bottom:6px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;"><i class="fas fa-credit-card"></i> Payment Request</div>`:''}
${data.isWithdrawReq && GU && GU.isAdmin ? `
  <div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.15);border-radius:8px;padding:6px 9px;margin:6px 0;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;">
    <i class="fas fa-money-bill-wave"></i> Withdraw Request — ₹${data.withdrawAmount||0}
  </div>
  <button onclick="adminAcceptWithdraw('${data.withdrawReqId}','${data.withdrawUid}',${data.withdrawAmount||0})" 
    style="background:var(--g3);color:#fff;border:none;border-radius:8px;padding:6px 14px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;margin-top:4px;">
    <i class="fas fa-check"></i> Yes — Accept
  </button>
` : ''}
        ${data.text?`<span style="white-space:pre-line;">${esc(data.text)}</span>`:''}
        ${isAI&&!isMine?`<div style="font-size:9px;opacity:.65;margin-top:4px;"><i class="fas fa-robot"></i> AI Assistant</div>`:''}
        <div class="bmeta ${isMine?'r':''}">
          ${fmtTime(data.ts||Date.now())}
          ${isMine?`<span id="seen_${data.id}">${data.seen?'<i class="fas fa-check-double" style="color:#7dd3fc;"></i>':'<i class="fas fa-check"></i>'}</span>`:''}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
  row.querySelector('.bbl').addEventListener('click',()=>{
    pendingDel={id:data.id,isMine};
    $('dAllBtn').style.display=isMine?'flex':'none';
    $('delBg').classList.add('open');
  });
  const tyInd=msgs.querySelector('#tyInd');
if(tyInd)msgs.insertBefore(row,tyInd);
else msgs.appendChild(row);
msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;
}

function closeDelBg(){$('delBg').classList.remove('open');pendingDel=null;}
function doDelete(type){
  if(!pendingDel||!CU)return;
  if(type==='all'&&pendingDel.isMine){
    const chatId=getChatId(CU.uid,ADMIN_UID);
    DB.chats().get(chatId).get(pendingDel.id).put(null);
  }
  deletedMsgs.add(pendingDel.id);
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_dm',JSON.stringify([...deletedMsgs]));
  const row=document.getElementById('row_'+pendingDel.id);if(row)row.remove();
  closeDelBg();toast('Message delete ho gaya');
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   FILE UPLOAD
══════════════════════════════════════ */

let chatImgXHR=null;
function handleFileSelect(e){
  const file=e.target.files[0];if(!file)return;
  // Preview dikhao
  const reader=new FileReader();
  reader.onload=ev=>{
    $('chatImgPrev').src=ev.target.result;
    $('chatImgPreview').style.display='block';
    $('chatImgLoader').style.display='flex';
    $('chatImgPrev').style.filter='blur(3px)';
    $('chatImgCross').style.display='none';
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  
  $('sndBtn').disabled=true;
  const form=new FormData();form.append('image',file);
  const xhr=new XMLHttpRequest();chatImgXHR=xhr;
  xhr.open('POST',`https://api.imgbb.com/1/upload?key=${IMGBB}`);
  xhr.onload=()=>{
    chatImgXHR=null;
    try{
      selImg=JSON.parse(xhr.responseText).data.url;
      // Upload done — clear dikhao
      $('chatImgPrev').style.filter='none';
      $('chatImgLoader').style.display='none';
      $('chatImgCross').style.display='flex';
      $('sndBtn').disabled=false;
      toast('Image ready ✅');
    }catch{cancelChatImg();toast('Upload fail hua');}
  };
  xhr.onerror=()=>{chatImgXHR=null;cancelChatImg();toast('Upload fail hua');};
  xhr.send(form);
}

function cancelChatImg(){
  if(chatImgXHR){chatImgXHR.abort();chatImgXHR=null;}
  selImg=null;
  $('fileIn').value='';
  $('chatImgPreview').style.display='none';
  $('chatImgPrev').src='';
  $('chatImgPrev').style.filter='none';
  $('chatImgLoader').style.display='none';
  $('sndBtn').disabled=false;
}


function cancelUpload(){if(uploadXHR)uploadXHR.abort();selImg=null;$('imLdr').classList.remove('show');$('sndBtn').disabled=false;$('fileIn').value='';toast('Upload cancel hua');}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   GROUP CHAT
══════════════════════════════════════ */
let grpLoaded=new Set(),grpMsgsList=[];

function initGroupChat(){
  if(!CU){toast('Pehle login karo');closeSP('groupChatSP');doLogin();return;}
  const msgs=$('groupMsgs');
  msgs.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:20px;"><div class="spin" style="margin:0 auto;"></div></div>';

  // Member count
  DB.groupMembers().once(data=>{
    const cnt=data?Object.keys(data).filter(k=>k!=='_').length:0;
    $('groupMemberCount').textContent=`${Math.max(cnt,1)} members online • Community`;
  });

  // Register as member
  DB.groupMembers().get(CU.uid).put({uid:CU.uid,name:GU.name||'User',photo:GU.photo||DAV,joined:Date.now()});

  if(grpGunOff)grpGunOff();
  

  grpGunOff=DB.groupChat().map().on((data,key)=>{
    if(!data||!data.ts||deletedMsgs.has(key))return;
    if(grpLoaded.has(key))return;
    grpLoaded.add(key);
    grpMsgsList.push({id:key,...data});
    grpMsgsList.sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts);
    renderGrpBubble({id:key,...data},msgs);
  });

  // Welcome if empty
  setTimeout(()=>{
    if(grpMsgsList.length===0){
      const wId='grpwelcome';
      if(!grpLoaded.has(wId)){
        DB.groupChat().get(wId).put({
          id:wId,senderId:'system',senderName:'EduSagar',senderPhoto:genAv('ES'),
          text:'EduSagar Group Chat mein swagat hai! 🎉 Yahan sab students aur admin baat kar sakte hain.',
          ts:Date.now()-1000
        });
      }
    }
  },2000);
}

function renderGrpBubble(data,msgs){
  if(!msgs||document.getElementById('grp_'+data.id))return;
  if(!CU)return;
  const isMine=data.senderId===CU.uid;
  const isSystem=data.senderId==='system';
  const isAdmin=data.isAdmin||data.senderId===ADMIN_UID;

  if(isSystem){
    const sep=document.createElement('div');
    sep.id='grp_'+data.id;
    sep.className='date-sep';
    sep.innerHTML=`<span>${esc(data.text||'')}</span>`;
    msgs.appendChild(sep);msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;return;
  }

  const av=isMine?(GU.photo||CU.photoURL||DAV):(data.senderPhoto||DAV);
  const row=document.createElement('div');
  row.className='mrow '+(isMine?'sent':'recv');
  row.id='grp_'+data.id;
  row.innerHTML=`
    <img class="mavsm" src="${av}" alt="" onerror="this.src='${DAV}'" loading="lazy">
    <div>
      ${!isMine?`<div class="grp-sender">${esc(data.senderName||'User')}${isAdmin?'<span class="abadge" style="margin-left:4px;"><i class="fas fa-shield-alt"></i></span>':''}</div>`:''}
      <div class="bbl ${isMine?'sent':(isAdmin?'ai-msg':'recv')}">
        ${data.img?`<img src="${data.img}" alt="" loading="lazy" onclick="event.stopPropagation();openImgPopup('${data.img}')">`:''}
        ${data.text?`<span style="white-space:pre-line;">${esc(data.text)}</span>`:''}
        <div class="bmeta ${isMine?'r':''}">${fmtTime(data.ts||Date.now())}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
  msgs.appendChild(row);msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;
}

function sendGrpMsg(){
  const inp=$('grpMsgInp');const txt=inp.value.trim();
  if(!txt&&!grpSelImg)return;
  if(!CU){toast('Pehle login karo');return;}
  const msgId='grp'+Date.now()+Math.random().toString(36).substring(2,4);
  DB.groupChat().get(msgId).put({
    id:msgId,senderId:CU.uid,senderName:GU.name||CU.displayName||'User',
    senderPhoto:GU.photo||CU.photoURL||DAV,
    text:txt,img:grpSelImg||null,isAdmin:GU.isAdmin||false,ts:Date.now()
  });
  inp.value='';grpSelImg=null;
}

function onGrpKey(e){if(e.key==='Enter')sendGrpMsg();}

function handleGrpFile(e){
  const file=e.target.files[0];if(!file)return;
  toast('Image upload ho rahi hai...');
  const form=new FormData();form.append('image',file);
  fetch(`https://api.imgbb.com/1/upload?key=${IMGBB}`,{method:'POST',body:form})
    .then(r=>r.json())
    .then(d=>{grpSelImg=d.data.url;toast('Image ready — Send karo 📤');})
    .catch(()=>toast('Upload fail hua'));
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   EDIT PROFILE
══════════════════════════════════════ */
function saveProfile(){
  if(!CU){doLogin();return;}
  const name=$('editName').value.trim();
  if(!name){toast('Naam daalo');return;}
  $('saveIc').className='fas fa-spinner fa-spin';
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).put({name});
  CU.updateProfile({displayName:name})
    .then(()=>{
      GU.name=name;CACHE.set('user_'+CU.uid,GU);
      $('saveIc').className='fas fa-check';
      $('profName').textContent=name;
      $('refOvName').textContent=name;
      toast('Profile update ho gayi! ✅');
      setTimeout(()=>closeSP('editSP'),900);
    })
    .catch(()=>{$('saveIc').className='fas fa-times';toast('Update fail hua');});
}

let avXHR=null;
function uploadAvatar(e){
  const file=e.target.files[0];if(!file)return;
  // Spinner show, blur, disable button
  $('editAv').style.filter='blur(4px)';
  $('avSpinner').style.display='block';
  $('avCancelBtn').style.display='flex';
  $('avCamBtn').style.display='none';
  $('saveProfileBtn').disabled=true;
  toast('Avatar upload ho raha hai...');
  
  const form=new FormData();form.append('image',file);
  const xhr=new XMLHttpRequest();avXHR=xhr;
  xhr.open('POST',`https://api.imgbb.com/1/upload?key=${IMGBB}`);
  xhr.onload=()=>{
    avXHR=null;
    try{
      const url=JSON.parse(xhr.responseText).data.url;
      $('editAv').src=url;$('profAv').src=url;$('refOvAv').src=url;
      DB.users().get(CU.uid).put({photo:url});
      CU.updateProfile({photoURL:url});
      GU.photo=url;CACHE.set('user_'+CU.uid,GU);
      // Reset
      $('editAv').style.filter='none';
      $('avSpinner').style.display='none';
      $('avCancelBtn').style.display='none';
      $('avCamBtn').style.display='flex';
      $('saveProfileBtn').disabled=false;
      toast('Avatar update ho gaya! 🖼️');
    }catch{cancelAvatarUpload();toast('Upload fail hua');}
  };
  xhr.onerror=()=>{avXHR=null;cancelAvatarUpload();toast('Upload fail hua');};
  xhr.send(form);
}

function cancelAvatarUpload(){
  if(avXHR){avXHR.abort();avXHR=null;}
  $('avIn').value='';
  $('editAv').style.filter='none';
  $('avSpinner').style.display='none';
  $('avCancelBtn').style.display='none';
  $('avCamBtn').style.display='flex';
  $('saveProfileBtn').disabled=false;
  toast('Upload cancel ho gaya');
}

async function setAiKey(){
  closeMenu();
  const r=await caInput('AI Key Set Karo','Claude Haiku API key daalo:','sk-ant-...');
  if(r.btn==='save'&&r.input){
    DB.settings().get('aiKey').put(r.input);
    toast('AI key save ho gayi! ✅ Chat ab AI-powered hai!');
  }
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   SERVICE WORKER (Offline Support)
══════════════════════════════════════ */
if('serviceWorker' in navigator){
  try{
    const swCode=`
const CACHE_NAME='edusagar-v07';
const ASSETS=['/'];
self.addEventListener('install',e=>{e.waitUntil(caches.open(CACHE_NAME).then(c=>c.addAll(ASSETS).catch(()=>{})));self.skipWaiting();});
self.addEventListener('activate',e=>{e.waitUntil(caches.keys().then(k=>Promise.all(k.filter(n=>n!==CACHE_NAME).map(n=>caches.delete(n)))));});
self.addEventListener('fetch',e=>{if(e.request.method!=='GET')return;e.respondWith(caches.match(e.request).then(r=>r||fetch(e.request).then(res=>{if(res&&res.status===200&&e.request.url.startsWith(self.location.origin)){const rc=res.clone();caches.open(CACHE_NAME).then(c=>c.put(e.request,rc));}return res;}).catch(()=>null)));});`;
    const blob=new Blob([swCode],{type:'application/javascript'});
    const url=URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    navigator.serviceWorker.register(url).catch(()=>{});
  }catch{}
}


/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   HISTORY-BASED BACK NAVIGATION
   Device back button support + proper
   nested page stack management
══════════════════════════════════════ */

// SP stack — track karo kaun kaun se pages open hain order mein
let _spStack = [];

// Original openSP override karo
const _origOpenSP = openSP;
window.openSP = function(id) {
  _origOpenSP(id);
  _spStack.push(id);
  // Browser history mein push karo
  history.pushState({ spId: id, stackLen: _spStack.length }, '', '');
};

// Original closeSP override karo
const _origCloseSP = closeSP;
window.closeSP = function(id) {
  _origCloseSP(id);
  // Stack se remove karo
  const idx = _spStack.lastIndexOf(id);
  if (idx !== -1) _spStack.splice(idx, 1);
};

// Amazon Full Page ke liye special openSP (bina history duplication)
function openSP_noHistory(id) {
  _origOpenSP(id);
  // Stack mein add karo but history push mat karo
  _spStack.push(id);
}

// Device back button press hone par
window.addEventListener('popstate', function(e) {
  if (_spStack.length > 0) {
    const topId = _spStack[_spStack.length - 1];
    _origCloseSP(topId);
    _spStack.pop();
    // Agar amazon viewer close kiya aur full list abhi bhi open hai — sahi hai
    // Kuch extra nahi karna
  }
  // Agar koi SP nahi tha toh browser normally navigate karega
});

// Jab app load ho, ek base history entry push karo
// Taaki pehli baar back press par app close na ho
history.replaceState({ base: true }, '', '');

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   AMAZON NESTED NAVIGATION FIX
   amazonFullSP → amazonViewSP → back → 
   amazonFullSP (not main)
══════════════════════════════════════ */

// Existing openAmazonItem ko override karo
const _origOpenAmazonItem = openAmazonItem;
window.openAmazonItem = function(id) {
  const it = _amzItems.find(x => x.id === id);
  if (!it) return;
  currentAffiliateUrl = it.affiliateUrl || '';
  $('amzViewTitle').textContent = it.title || 'Product';
  $('amzViewImg').src = it.imgUrl || '';
  $('amzViewName').textContent = it.title || '';
  $('amzViewDesc').textContent = it.desc || '';
  $('amzViewPrice').textContent = it.price || 'Amazon par check karein';
  if (CU) DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('amzClicks').put((Date.now()) + '_' + id);
  // Normal openSP use karo — history stack mein add hoga
  openSP('amazonViewSP');
};

// closeVideo bhi history-aware banao


// openAdminChat bhi openSP use kare
const _origOpenAdminChat = openAdminChat;
window.openAdminChat = function() {
  
  openSP('chatInterfaceSP'); // ye ab history push karega
  const msgs = $('chatMsgs');
  msgs.innerHTML = '';
  const cached = CACHE.getStale('msgs_' + CU.uid);
  if (cached && cached.length) {
    chatAllLoaded = new Set();
    chatMsgsList = [];
    cached.sort((a, b) => a.ts - b.ts).forEach(m => {
      if (!deletedMsgs.has(m.id)) {
        chatAllLoaded.add(m.id);
        chatMsgsList.push(m);
        renderBubble(m);
      }
    });
    msgs.scrollTop = msgs.scrollHeight;
  }
  if (chatGunOff) { chatGunOff(); chatGunOff = null; }
  const chatId = getChatId(CU.uid, ADMIN_UID);
  chatGunOff = DB.chats().get(chatId).map().on((data, key) => {
    if (!data || !data.ts || deletedMsgs.has(key)) return;
    if (chatAllLoaded.has(key)) {
      if (data.seen) {
        const si = document.getElementById('seen_' + key);
        if (si) si.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-double" style="color:#7dd3fc;"></i>';
      }
      return;
    }
    chatAllLoaded.add(key);
    chatMsgsList.push({ id: key, ...data });
    chatMsgsList.sort((a, b) => a.ts - b.ts);
    CACHE.set('msgs_' + CU.uid, chatMsgsList.slice(-100));
    renderBubble({ id: key, ...data });
    if (data.senderId !== CU.uid && !data.seen) {
      DB.chats().get(chatId).get(key).get('seen').put(true);
    }
  });
  if (!cached || !cached.length) {
    setTimeout(() => { if (chatMsgsList.length === 0) showWelcomeMsg(); }, 1500);
  }
};

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   RECOMMENDED VIDEOS
══════════════════════════════════════ */
let _recVidsAll = [];
let _currentVidId = '';

function loadRecommendedVideos(currentId, currentVid){
  _currentVidId = currentId || '';
  const el = $('recVidList');
  if(!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading...</p></div>';
  
  // Cache se pehle load karo
  const cached = CACHE.getStale('vids_' + activeStream);
  if(cached && cached.length){
    _recVidsAll = cached.filter(v => v.id !== _currentVidId);
    // Shuffle for random feel
    _recVidsAll = shuffleArr(_recVidsAll);
    renderRecVideos(_recVidsAll, el);
    return;
  }
  
  // GUN se load karo
  const vids = []; const vs = new Set();
  DB.videos(activeStream).map().once((data, key) => {
    if(data && data.title && !vs.has(key)){ vs.add(key); vids.push({id:key,...data}); }
  });
  setTimeout(()=>{
    _recVidsAll = vids.filter(v => v.id !== _currentVidId);
    _recVidsAll = shuffleArr(_recVidsAll);
    CACHE.set('vids_' + activeStream, [...vids]);
    renderRecVideos(_recVidsAll, el);
  }, 900);
}

function shuffleArr(arr){
  const a = [...arr];
  for(let i = a.length-1; i > 0; i--){
    const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i+1));
    [a[i], a[j]] = [a[j], a[i]];
  }
  return a;
}

function renderRecVideos(vids, el){
  if(!el) return;
  if(!vids || !vids.length){
    el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-video-slash"></i><p>Koi recommended video nahi</p></div>';
    return;
  }
  
  el.innerHTML = vids.map(v => {
    const canWatch = canWatchVideo(v);
    const locked = !canWatch;
    
    // Lock reason badge
    let lockReason = '';
    if(locked){
      if(!GU || !GU.membership){
        lockReason = 'Login & Join';
      } else if(GU.membership === 'batch' && v.planLevel === 'pro'){
        lockReason = 'Pro Plan';
      } else if(GU.membership === 'batch' && v.planLevel === 'infinity'){
        lockReason = 'Infinity Plan';
      } else if(GU.membership === 'pro' && v.planLevel === 'infinity'){
        lockReason = 'Infinity Plan';
      } else {
        lockReason = 'Members Only';
      }
    }
    
    return `<div class="vcard" onclick="switchRecVideo('${v.id}')" style="cursor:pointer;${locked?'opacity:.75;':''}">
      <div class="vthumb">
        ${v.thumb ? `<img src="${v.thumb}" alt="" loading="lazy">` : '<i class="fas fa-play-circle" style="font-size:28px;color:var(--p);"></i>'}
        <div class="vplay"><i class="fas fa-play"></i></div>
        ${locked ? `<div class="vlock">
          <div style="text-align:center;">
            <i class="fas fa-lock" style="color:#fff;font-size:16px;display:block;margin-bottom:3px;"></i>
            <span style="color:#fff;font-size:8px;font-weight:700;">${lockReason}</span>
          </div>
        </div>` : ''}
      </div>
      <div class="vinfo">
        <h4>${esc(v.title)}</h4>
        <p>${esc(v.desc||'')}</p>
        <div class="vtag ${locked?'paid':'free'}">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'play-circle'}"></i>
          ${locked ? lockReason : 'Free Watch'}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}
function switchRecVideo(id){
  // Cache se video dhundho
  let v = null;
  const cached = CACHE.getStale('vids_' + activeStream);
  if(cached) v = cached.find(x => x.id === id);
  
  if(v){
    // Access check
    if(!canWatchVideo(v)){
      // Membership prompt with plan info
      const plan = GU?.membership;
      if(!plan){
        toast('Is video ke liye membership chahiye! 🔒');
      } else if(plan === 'batch'){
        toast('Yeh video Pro ya Infinity plan mein hai! ⬆️');
      } else if(plan === 'pro'){
        toast('Yeh video Infinity plan mein hai! ⬆️');
      }
      setTimeout(()=> openMem(), 800);
      return;
    }
    // Scroll to top
    const sp = $('vidSP');
    const body = sp.querySelector('.sp-body');
    if(body) body.scrollTop = 0;
    applyVideo(v);
    // Search clear karo
    const srch = $('recVidSrch');
    if(srch) srch.value = '';
  } else {
    DB.videos(activeStream).get(id).once(data => {
      if(!data){ toast('Video load nahi hua'); return; }
      if(data.paid && !hasMem){ openMem(); return; }
      applyVideo({id, ...data});
    });
  }
}

function filterRecVideos(q){
  q = (q||'').toLowerCase();
  const filtered = q
    ? _recVidsAll.filter(v =>
        (v.title||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
        (v.desc||'').toLowerCase().includes(q)
      )
    : _recVidsAll;
  renderRecVideos(filtered, $('recVidList'));
}
/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   LAZY LOADER SYSTEM
══════════════════════════════════════ */
let _lazyObs = null;
function setupLazyLoader(){
  if(_lazyObs) return;
  _lazyObs = new IntersectionObserver((entries)=>{
    entries.forEach(e=>{
      if(e.isIntersecting) e.target.classList.add('visible');
    });
  },{threshold:0.08});
}
function lazyWatch(el){
  if(!el||!_lazyObs) return;
  el.classList.add('lazy-item');
  _lazyObs.observe(el);
}

══════════════════════════════════════ */

  _origNavTo(page, el);

  if(page === 'home'){
    renderHomeFeed();
    renderStories();
  }
  if(page === 'books'){
    loadSubjects(activeStream);
    loadPYQs(activeStream);
    loadBooks(activeStream);
    loadVideos(activeStream);
    loadAmazonItems();
  }
  if(page === 'store') loadStoreItems();
  if(page === 'profile'){
    renderMemCard();
    
  }
};

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   MEMBERSHIP EXPIRY — April 29 har saal
══════════════════════════════════════ */
function getOneYearFromNow(){
  const now = new Date();
  // Exactly +1 year — same date, same month, next year
  return new Date(now.getFullYear() + 1, now.getMonth(), now.getDate(), 23, 59, 59).getTime();
}

function checkMembershipExpiry(uid){
  if(!uid) return;
  DB.users().get(uid).once(data=>{
    if(!data || !data.membership) return;
    const expTs = data.membershipExpiry || 0;
    if(!expTs){
      // Purani membership — expiry set karo
      const newExp = getOneYearFromNow();
      DB.users().get(uid).get('membershipExpiry').put(newExp);
      GU.membershipExpiry = newExp;
      return;
    }
    if(Date.now() > expTs){
      // Expire ho gaya!
      DB.users().get(uid).put({
        ...data,
        membership: null,
        membershipExpiry: null,
        membershipStream: null
      });
      // Circle bhi hatao
      DB.members().get(uid).put(null);
      GU.membership = null;
      GU.membershipExpiry = null;
      applyGU();
      renderStories();
      toast('Aapki membership expire ho gayi — Renew karein! ⚠️');
    } else {
      // Valid hai — timer dikhao
      showExpiryBadge(expTs);
    }
  });
}

function showExpiryBadge(expTs){
  const days = Math.ceil((expTs - Date.now()) / (1000*60*60*24));
  const memBtn = document.querySelector('.hdr-r .btn.bp');
  if(memBtn && GU.membership){
    if(days <= 30){
      memBtn.innerHTML = `<i class="fas fa-crown"></i> ${days}d left`;
      memBtn.style.background = days<=7 ? 'var(--g4)' : 'var(--g3)';
    }
  }
}

}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   DOWNLOAD MANAGER — IndexedDB
══════════════════════════════════════ */

// IndexedDB setup
let _dlDB = null;

function initDownloadDB(){
  return new Promise((resolve, reject)=>{
    const req = indexedDB.open('EduSagarDownloads', 1);
    req.onupgradeneeded = e => {
      const db = e.target.result;
      if(!db.objectStoreNames.contains('downloads')){
        const store = db.createObjectStore('downloads', {keyPath:'id'});
        store.createIndex('ts', 'ts');
      }
    };
    req.onsuccess = e => { _dlDB = e.target.result; resolve(_dlDB); };
    req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
  });
}

async function getDB(){
  if(_dlDB) return _dlDB;
  return await initDownloadDB();
}

// Download item save karo
async function saveDownload(item){
  const db = await getDB();
  return new Promise((resolve, reject)=>{
    const tx = db.transaction('downloads', 'readwrite');
    tx.objectStore('downloads').put(item);
    tx.oncomplete = () => resolve();
    tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error);
  });
}

// Sab downloads lo
async function getAllDownloads(){
  const db = await getDB();
  return new Promise((resolve, reject)=>{
    const tx = db.transaction('downloads', 'readonly');
    const req = tx.objectStore('downloads').index('ts').getAll();
    req.onsuccess = () => resolve((req.result||[]).reverse());
    req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
  });
}

// Ek download delete karo
async function deleteDownload(id){
  const db = await getDB();
  return new Promise((resolve, reject)=>{
    const tx = db.transaction('downloads', 'readwrite');
    tx.objectStore('downloads').delete(id);
    tx.oncomplete = () => resolve();
    tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error);
  });
}

// Sab downloads delete karo
async function clearAllDownloads(){
  const r = await caConfirm('Clear Downloads','Sab downloaded files delete ho jaengi?','Delete All');
  if(r.btn !== 'yes') return;
  const db = await getDB();
  const tx = db.transaction('downloads', 'readwrite');
  tx.objectStore('downloads').clear();
  renderDownloadsSection();
  toast('Sab downloads clear ho gayi ✅');
}

/* ══ MAIN DOWNLOAD FUNCTION ══ */
async function downloadPDF(item){
  if(!item || !item.url){
    toast('Download link available nahi ⚠️');
    return;
  }

  // Already downloaded check
  const db = await getDB();
  const existing = await new Promise(res=>{
    const tx = db.transaction('downloads','readonly');
    const req = tx.objectStore('downloads').get(item.id);
    req.onsuccess = ()=> res(req.result);
    req.onerror = ()=> res(null);
  });

  if(existing && existing.blob){
    toast('Pehle se downloaded hai! ✅');
    openDownloadedFile(existing);
    return;
  }

  // Download card create karo
  const dlId = item.id + '_' + Date.now();
  const dlItem = {
    id: item.id,
    title: item.title || 'File',
    type: item.type || 'pdf',
    url: item.url,
    size: item.size || '',
    subject: item.subject || '',
    ts: Date.now(),
    status: 'downloading',
    progress: 0,
    blob: null,
    blobUrl: null
  };

  await saveDownload(dlItem);
  renderDownloadsSection();
  toast('Download shuru ho rahi hai... 📥');

  // Show downloads section
  const ds = $('downloadsSection');
  if(ds) ds.style.display = 'block';

  try{
    // Fetch with progress tracking
    const response = await fetch(item.url);
    if(!response.ok) throw new Error('Network error');

    const contentLength = response.headers.get('content-length');
    const total = parseInt(contentLength || '0');
    let loaded = 0;
    const chunks = [];

    const reader = response.body.getReader();

    while(true){
      const {done, value} = await reader.read();
      if(done) break;
      chunks.push(value);
      loaded += value.length;

      // Progress update
      const pct = total > 0 ? Math.round((loaded/total)*100) : 0;
      dlItem.progress = pct;
      dlItem.status = 'downloading';
      updateDownloadCard(item.id, pct, 'prog');
    }

    // Blob banao
    const blob = new Blob(chunks, {type: 'application/pdf'});
    const blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);

    // Array buffer save karo (IndexedDB ke liye)
    const arrayBuffer = await blob.arrayBuffer();

    dlItem.status = 'done';
    dlItem.progress = 100;
    dlItem.blob = arrayBuffer;
    dlItem.blobUrl = null; // Session mein regenerate karenge
    dlItem.fileSize = blob.size;

    await saveDownload(dlItem);
    updateDownloadCard(item.id, 100, 'done');
    renderDownloadsSection();
    toast(`"${item.title}" download ho gaya! ✅`);

    // Auto open
    setTimeout(()=> openDownloadedFile({...dlItem, blob: arrayBuffer}), 500);

  } catch(err){
    dlItem.status = 'error';
    await saveDownload(dlItem);
    updateDownloadCard(item.id, 0, 'err');
    toast('Download fail hua — Retry karo ❌');
  }
}

// Download card UI update
function updateDownloadCard(id, pct, status){
  const card = document.getElementById('dlcard_'+id);
  if(!card) return;
  const prog = card.querySelector('.dl-prog');
  const stat = card.querySelector('.dl-status');
  if(prog) prog.style.width = pct + '%';
  if(stat){
    stat.className = 'dl-status ' + status;
    if(status === 'done') stat.textContent = '✅ Download Complete';
    else if(status === 'err') stat.textContent = '❌ Download Failed — Retry karo';
    else stat.textContent = `⬇️ Downloading... ${pct}%`;
  }
}

// Downloaded file open karo
function openDownloadedFile(item){
  if(!item.blob){
    toast('File data nahi mila, dobara download karo');
    return;
  }
  try{
    const blob = new Blob([item.blob], {type: 'application/pdf'});
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    // PDF viewer mein kholo
    $('pdfViewTitle').textContent = item.title || 'PDF';
    $('pdfViewSubtitle').textContent = (item.subject||'') + ' • Offline';
    $('pdfDownloadBtn').href = url;
    $('pdfDownloadBtn').style.display = 'flex';
    $('pdfFrame').src = url;
    openSP('pdfViewSP');
  } catch(e){
    toast('File open nahi hui');
  }
}

/* ══ DOWNLOADS SECTION RENDER ══ */
async function renderDownloadsSection(){
  const container = $('downloadsList');
  const section = $('downloadsSection');
  if(!container) return;

  const downloads = await getAllDownloads();

  if(!downloads || !downloads.length){
    if(section) section.style.display = 'none';
    container.innerHTML = `<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-inbox"></i><p>Koi downloaded file nahi</p></div>`;
    return;
  }

  if(section) section.style.display = 'block';

  container.innerHTML = downloads.map(dl => `
    <div class="dl-manager-card" id="dlcard_${dl.id}">
      <div class="dl-ic-wrap">
        <i class="fas fa-file-pdf"></i>
      </div>
      <div class="dl-info">
        <h4>${esc(dl.title)}</h4>
        <p>
          ${dl.subject ? dl.subject + ' • ' : ''}
          ${dl.fileSize ? formatBytes(dl.fileSize) + ' • ' : ''}
          ${new Date(dl.ts).toLocaleDateString('en-IN')}
          ${dl.status === 'done' ? ' <span class="offline-badge"><i class="fas fa-wifi-slash"></i> Offline</span>' : ''}
        </p>
        <div class="dl-prog-wrap" ${dl.status === 'done' ? 'style="display:none"' : ''}>
          <div class="dl-prog" style="width:${dl.progress||0}%"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="dl-status ${dl.status === 'done' ? 'done' : dl.status === 'error' ? 'err' : 'prog'}">
          ${dl.status === 'done' ? '✅ Downloaded' : dl.status === 'error' ? '❌ Failed' : `⬇️ ${dl.progress||0}%`}
        </div>
      </div>
      ${dl.status === 'done' ? `
        <button class="dl-open-btn" onclick="openDownloadedFile_byId('${dl.id}')">
          <i class="fas fa-eye"></i> Open
        </button>
      ` : ''}
      <button class="dl-del-btn" onclick="removeDownload('${dl.id}')">
        <i class="fas fa-times"></i>
      </button>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

async function openDownloadedFile_byId(id){
  const db = await getDB();
  const item = await new Promise(res=>{
    const tx = db.transaction('downloads','readonly');
    const req = tx.objectStore('downloads').get(id);
    req.onsuccess = ()=> res(req.result);
    req.onerror = ()=> res(null);
  });
  if(item) openDownloadedFile(item);
  else toast('File nahi mili');
}

async function removeDownload(id){
  await deleteDownload(id);
  renderDownloadsSection();
  toast('File remove ho gayi');
}

function formatBytes(bytes){
  if(!bytes) return '';
  if(bytes < 1024) return bytes + ' B';
  if(bytes < 1024*1024) return (bytes/1024).toFixed(1) + ' KB';
  return (bytes/(1024*1024)).toFixed(1) + ' MB';
}

window.addEventListener('offline', ()=>{
  const banner = $('offlineRedirectBanner');
  if(banner) banner.style.display = 'flex';
  // Profile tab pe redirect karo downloads dekhne ke liye
  setTimeout(()=>{
    const anyDownloads = $('downloadsList')?.children?.length > 0;
    if(anyDownloads){
      toast('Offline! Downloaded files profile mein hain 📁');
    }
  }, 500);
});

window.addEventListener('online', ()=>{
  const banner = $('offlineRedirectBanner');
  if(banner) banner.style.display = 'none';
  // Online hone par bhi downloads section rahe
});

/* ══ MEMBERSHIP CARD FIX ══ */
function renderMemCard(){
  const c = $('memCard');
  if(!c) return;
 
  if(!GU || !GU.membership){
    c.innerHTML = `
      <div class="mem-card none" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="openMem()">
        <i class="fas fa-lock" style="font-size:22px;"></i>
        <div style="flex:1;">
          <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;">Koi Membership Nahi</div>
          <div style="font-size:11px;opacity:.9;">Premium features unlock karein</div>
        </div>
        <button class="btn bsm" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.25);color:#fff;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.3);">Join Now</button>
      </div>`;
    return;
  }
  const planNames = {
    batch: 'Batch',
    pro: 'Pro',
    infinity: 'Infinity Pro'
  };
  const streamNames = {
    science: 'Science',
    arts: 'Arts',
    commerce: 'Commerce',
    '10th': '10th Class'
  };
 
  const plan = planNames[GU.membershipPlan || GU.membership] || (GU.membership || '').toUpperCase();
  const stream = streamNames[GU.membershipStream] || GU.membershipStream || '';
  const expTs = GU.membershipExpiry || 0;
  const days = expTs ? Math.ceil((expTs - Date.now()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) : null;
  const isExpiring = days !== null && days <= 7 && days > 0;
  const isExpired = days !== null && days <= 0;
 
  c.innerHTML = `
    <div class="mem-card active" style="background:${isExpired ? 'var(--g4)' : isExpiring ? 'linear-gradient(135deg,#f59e0b,#ef4444)' : 'var(--g3)'};">
      <div style="flex-shrink:0;">
        <i class="fas fa-crown" style="font-size:24px;"></i>
      </div>
      <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
        <div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:800;">${stream} — ${plan}</div>
        <div style="font-size:11px;opacity:.9;margin-top:2px;">
          ${isExpired
            ? '⚠️ Membership expire ho gayi — Renew karo'
            : isExpiring
              ? `⏰ Sirf ${days} din bacha hai!`
              : days !== null
                ? `Valid till: ${new Date(expTs).toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {day:'numeric', month:'short', year:'numeric'})}`
                : 'Active Membership ✓'
          }
        </div>
      </div>
      <i class="fas fa-${isExpired ? 'exclamation-circle' : 'check-circle'}" style="font-size:20px;flex-shrink:0;"></i>
    </div>
 
    <!-- Quick Links -->
    <div style="display:flex;gap:9px;margin-top:10px;">
    <button onclick="navTo('books',$('nav-books'))" style="flex:1;padding:10px;border:none;border-radius:12px;background:var(--plight);color:var(--p);font-size:12px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--font);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:6px;">
        <i class="fas fa-book-open"></i> My Courses
      </button>
      <button onclick="openMem()" style="flex:1;padding:10px;border:1.5px solid var(--bd);border-radius:12px;background:var(--sur2);color:var(--txm);font-size:12px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--font);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:6px;">
        <i class="fas fa-sync-alt"></i> ${isExpired ? 'Renew' : 'Upgrade'}
      </button>
    </div>`;
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   APK POPUP SYSTEM
══════════════════════════════════════ */
let _currentApkItem = null;

function showApkPopup(item){
  _currentApkItem = item;
  $('apkPopupTitle').textContent = item.title || 'App';
  $('apkPopupDesc').textContent = item.desc || '';
  const ic = $('apkPopupIc');
  if(ic) ic.innerHTML = `<i class="${item.ic || 'fab fa-android'}"></i>`;
  const bg = $('apkPopupBg');
  bg.style.display = 'flex';
  document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
}

function closeApkPopup(){
  $('apkPopupBg').style.display = 'none';
  document.body.style.overflow = '';
  _currentApkItem = null;
}

function openApkWebsite(){
  if(!_currentApkItem) return;
  const url = _currentApkItem.webUrl || _currentApkItem.url || '';
  closeApkPopup();
  if(!url){ toast('Web link available nahi'); return; }
  // App ke andar naya page kholo
  $('apkWebTitle').textContent = _currentApkItem.title || 'Website';
  $('apkWebFrame').src = url;
  openSP('apkWebSP');
}

function downloadApkFile(){
  if(!_currentApkItem) return;
  const url = _currentApkItem.url || _currentApkItem.apkUrl || '';
  closeApkPopup();
  if(!url){ toast('APK link available nahi'); return; }
  // Direct download
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  a.download = (_currentApkItem.title || 'app') + '.apk';
  a.target = '_blank';
  document.body.appendChild(a);
  a.click();
  document.body.removeChild(a);
  toast('APK download shuru ho gaya... 📲');
}
/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   WATERMARK SYSTEM
   true  = sabko dikhao (members + non-members)
   false = sirf non-members ko dikhao
══════════════════════════════════════ */
const WATERMARK_FOR_ALL = true; // ← yahan se control karo

function initWatermark(){
  // Turant bhi try karo, splash ke baad bhi
  applyWatermark();
  setTimeout(()=>{ applyWatermark(); }, 1000);
  setTimeout(()=>{ applyWatermark(); }, 2700);
  setTimeout(()=>{ applyWatermark(); }, 5000);
}

function applyWatermark(){
  const wm = $('appWatermark');
  if(!wm){ console.log('WM not found'); return; }
  
  // Force show — seedha style set karo, class pe depend mat karo
  if(WATERMARK_FOR_ALL){
    wm.style.opacity = '1';
    wm.style.visibility = 'visible';
    wm.classList.add('show');
    return;
  }

  GU && GU.membership === 'active';
  if(hasMem){
    wm.style.opacity = '0';
    wm.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    wm.classList.remove('show');
  } else {
    wm.style.opacity = '1';
    wm.style.visibility = 'visible';
    wm.classList.add('show');
  }
}
/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   USER PROFILE SYSTEM
══════════════════════════════════════ */

function openUserProfile(uid, name){
  
  
  // Khud ka profile — profile page open karo
  if(CU && uid === CU.uid){
    navTo('profile', $('nav-profile'));
    return;
  }
  
  // Membership overlay force close karo
  closeOv('memOv');
  closeOv('payOv');
  
  // Dusre ka profile
  $('userProfileTitle').textContent = name || 'Profile';
  $('userProfileBody').innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading...</p></div>';
  $('userProfilePrivateBadge').style.display = 'none';
  openSP('userProfileSP');
  
  // URL mein profile ID set karo for sharing
  history.replaceState({}, '', '?profile='+uid);
  
  // GUN se data load karo
  // GUN se data load karo — retry with timeout
  let dataLoaded = false;
  
  gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('users').get(uid).on(function(data, key, msg, ev){
    if(dataLoaded) return;
    if(!data || !data.name){
      // 3 second wait karo — GUN slow ho sakta hai
      setTimeout(()=>{
        if(!dataLoaded){
          // Dobara try karo
          gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('users').get(uid).once(d2=>{
            if(d2 && d2.name){
              dataLoaded = true;
              if(ev) ev.off();
              if(d2.isPrivate){
                showPrivateProfile();
              } else {
                renderUserProfilePage(uid, d2);
              }
            } else {
              $('userProfileBody').innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-user-slash"></i><p>Profile nahi mila</p></div>';
            }
            
            
            
          });
        }
      }, 3000);
      return;
    }
    dataLoaded = true;
    if(ev) ev.off();
    if(data.isPrivate){
      showPrivateProfile();
      return;
    }
    renderUserProfilePage(uid, data);
  });
  
  function showPrivateProfile(){
    $('userProfilePrivateBadge').style.display = 'flex';
    $('userProfileBody').innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i><p>Loading...</p></div>';
    setTimeout(()=>{
      $('userProfileBody').innerHTML = `
        <div style="text-align:center;padding:60px 20px;">
          <div style="width:80px;height:80px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--sur2);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;margin:0 auto 16px;">
            <i class="fas fa-lock" style="font-size:32px;color:var(--txm);"></i>
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family:var(--fdisp);margin-bottom:8px;">This Profile is Private</h3>
          <p style="color:var(--txm);font-size:13px;">Is user ne apna profile private kar rakha hai</p>
        </div>`;
    }, 1500);
  }   // ← showPrivateProfile band

}     // ← YEH ADD KARO — openUserProfile band
  










function renderUserProfilePage(uid, data){
  const isVerified = (data.likes||0) >= 1000;
  const memberNames = {
    science:'Science',arts:'Arts',commerce:'Commerce','10th':'10th Class'
  };
  const profileUrl = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname + '?profile=' + uid;
  
  $('userProfileTitle').textContent = data.name || 'Profile';
  
  $('userProfileBody').innerHTML = `
    <!-- Hero -->
    <div style="background:var(--g1);border-radius:var(--r);padding:28px 18px 22px;text-align:center;margin-bottom:14px;position:relative;overflow:hidden;">
      <div style="position:absolute;top:-20px;right:-20px;width:100px;height:100px;border-radius:50%;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);"></div>
      <img src="${data.photo||DAV}" style="width:82px;height:82px;border-radius:50%;border:3px solid rgba(255,255,255,.8);object-fit:cover;display:block;margin:0 auto 10px;" onerror="this.src='${DAV}'">
      <h2 style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:20px;color:#fff;margin-bottom:4px;">
        ${esc(data.name||'User')}
        ${isVerified ? '<span style="color:#facc15;font-size:14px;margin-left:4px;" title="1k+ likes">✓</span>' : ''}
      </h2>
      ${data.membership ? `
        <div style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);border-radius:20px;padding:4px 12px;margin-top:4px;font-size:11px;color:#fff;font-weight:700;">
          <i class="fas fa-crown" style="color:#facc15;"></i>
          ${memberNames[data.membershipStream]||data.membershipStream||''} ${(data.membership||'').toUpperCase()} Member
        </div>
      ` : `
        <div style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.12);border-radius:20px;padding:4px 12px;margin-top:4px;font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);">
          <i class="fas fa-user"></i> Free Member
        </div>
      `}
      <!-- Stats -->
      <div style="display:flex;margin-top:16px;border-top:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.2);padding-top:14px;gap:0;">
        <div style="flex:1;text-align:center;border-right:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.2);">
          <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:800;font-family:var(--fdisp);color:#fff;" id="upLikeCount">${fmtL(data.likes||0)}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);">Likes</div>
        </div>
        <div style="flex:1;text-align:center;border-right:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.2);">
          <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:800;font-family:var(--fdisp);color:#fff;">${data.referrals||0}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);">Referrals</div>
        </div>
        <div style="flex:1;text-align:center;">
          <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:800;font-family:var(--fdisp);color:#fff;">${data.courses||0}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);">Courses</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- Like + Share Buttons -->
    <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;margin-bottom:14px;">
      <button id="upLikeBtn" onclick="toggleProfileLike('${uid}')"
        style="flex:1;padding:13px;border:2px solid var(--bd);border-radius:var(--r2);background:var(--sur);font-size:13px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:8px;font-family:var(--font);color:var(--tx);transition:all .2s;">
        <i id="upLikeIc" class="${_profileLiked.has(uid)?'fas':'far'} fa-heart" style="color:${_profileLiked.has(uid)?'var(--s)':'var(--txm)'};font-size:18px;"></i>
        <span id="upLikeTxt">${fmtL(data.likes||0)}</span>
      </button>
      <button onclick="shareUserProfile('${uid}','${esc(data.name||'User')}')"
        style="flex:1;padding:13px;border:none;border-radius:var(--r2);background:var(--g1);color:#fff;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:8px;font-family:var(--font);">
        <i class="fas fa-share-alt"></i> Share
      </button>
    </div>
    
    <!-- Info Card -->
    <div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);padding:16px;margin-bottom:14px;">

      <div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--txm);line-height:2.2;">

        ${data.membershipExpiry ? `<div><i class="fas fa-calendar-alt" style="color:var(--ok);margin-right:8px;width:16px;"></i>

      <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:15px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:11px;"><i class="fas fa-users" style="color:var(--p);margin-right:7px;"></i>Other Members</div>
      <div class="srow" id="otherProfilesRow" style="padding-bottom:8px;"></div>
    </div>

  // Live like count
  // Live like count — direct gun path, fast update
  gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('users').get(uid).get('likes').on(count=>{
    if(count === null || count === undefined) return;
    const el=$('upLikeCount');
    const el2=$('upLikeTxt');
    if(el) el.textContent = fmtL(count);
    if(el2) el2.textContent = fmtL(count);
  });
  
  // Profile data bhi live update karo
  gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('users').get(uid).on(data=>{
    if(!data || !data.name) return;
    // Name update
    const title = $('userProfileTitle');
    if(title) title.textContent = data.name;
  });
  
  // Load other members
  loadOtherProfiles(uid);
}

// Profile likes
let _profileLiked = new Set(JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('esv07_plikes')||'[]'));


    function toggleProfileLike(uid){
  if(!CU){ toast('Like karne ke liye login karo'); return; }
  
  const ic=$('upLikeIc');
  const txt=$('upLikeTxt');
  const countEl=$('upLikeCount');
  
  // Optimistic UI — turant update karo
  const isLiked = _profileLiked.has(uid);
  const curDisplay = parseInt(countEl?.textContent?.replace('k','000').replace('.','') || '0');
  
  if(isLiked){
    _profileLiked.delete(uid);
    if(ic){ ic.className='far fa-heart'; ic.style.color='var(--txm)'; }
    // Optimistic count
    const newCount = Math.max(0, curDisplay - 1);
    if(txt) txt.textContent = fmtL(newCount);
    if(countEl) countEl.textContent = fmtL(newCount);
  } else {
    _profileLiked.add(uid);
    if(ic){ ic.className='fas fa-heart'; ic.style.color='var(--s)'; }
    // Optimistic count
    const newCount = curDisplay + 1;
    if(txt) txt.textContent = fmtL(newCount);
    if(countEl) countEl.textContent = fmtL(newCount);
  }
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_plikes', JSON.stringify([..._profileLiked]));
  
  // GUN mein actual value se update karo
  gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('users').get(uid).get('likes').once(current=>{
    const cur = parseInt(current) || 0;
    const newVal = _profileLiked.has(uid) ? cur + 1 : Math.max(0, cur - 1);
    gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('users').get(uid).get('likes').put(newVal);
  });
}
    

function shareUserProfile(uid, name){
  const url = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname + '?profile=' + uid;
  // Fix: text mein URL mat daalo, url alag pass karo
  const msg = `${name} ka EduSagar profile dekho! 🎓`;
  if(navigator.share){
    navigator.share({title:'EduSagar Profile — '+name, text:msg, url:url}).catch(()=>{});
  } else {
    navigator.clipboard?.writeText(url).then(()=>toast('Profile link copy ho gaya! 📋'));
  }
}

function loadOtherProfiles(currentUid){
  const row=$('otherProfilesRow');
  if(!row) return;
  row.innerHTML='<div class="empty" style="padding:10px;"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i></div>';
  
  const members=[];const ms=new Set();
  // Longer timeout — GUN slow load
  gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('members').map().once((data,key)=>{
    if(data&&data.name&&data.photo&&!ms.has(key)&&key!==currentUid){
      ms.add(key);
      members.push({...data,uid:key});
    }
  });
  
  setTimeout(()=>{
    if(!members.length){
      row.innerHTML='<div style="padding:10px;font-size:12px;color:var(--txm);">Koi aur member nahi abhi</div>';
      return;
    }
    const show=members.slice(0,12);
    row.innerHTML=show.map(u=>`
      <div class="sit" onclick="closeSP('userProfileSP');setTimeout(()=>openUserProfile('${u.uid}','${esc(u.name||'User')}'),300);">
        <div class="sring"><img src="${u.photo||DAV}" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.src='${DAV}'"></div>
        <p>${esc((u.name||'User').substring(0,7))}</p>
      </div>
    `).join('');
  }, 2000);
}

// Deep link — URL se profile open karo
function checkProfileDeepLink(){
  const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
  const profileUid = params.get('profile');
  if(profileUid){
    setTimeout(()=>{
      DB.users().get(profileUid).once(data=>{
        if(data&&data.name) openUserProfile(profileUid, data.name);
      });
    }, 2800); // Splash ke baad
  }
}

// Admin — kisi ka like badhao
async function adminBoostLike(uid){
  if(!GU.isAdmin){ toast('Admin only!'); return; }
  const r = await caInput('Like Boost','Kitne likes add karne hain?','100');
  if(r.btn!=='save'||!r.input) return;
  const add = parseInt(r.input)||0;
  DB.users().get(uid).get('likes').once(cur=>{
    DB.users().get(uid).get('likes').put((cur||0)+add);
    toast(`+${add} likes add ho gaye ✅`);
  });
}
// Auth change hone par bhi check karo
// applyGU() ke andar call hoga automatically
/* ══ PRIVACY TOGGLE ══ */
function toggleProfilePrivacy(){
  if(!CU) return;
  const tgl=$('privacyTgl');
  const txt=$('privacyStatusTxt');
  const isNowPrivate = !tgl.classList.contains('on');
  
  // UI turant update karo
  tgl.classList.toggle('on', isNowPrivate);
  GU.isPrivate = isNowPrivate;
  
  if(txt){
    txt.textContent = isNowPrivate
      ? 'Private — Sirf aap dekh sakte hain'
      : 'Public — Sab dekh sakte hain';
  }
  
  // GUN mein poora user object update karo (nested put kaam nahi karta)
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).once(data=>{
    DB.users().get(CU.uid).put({...data, isPrivate: isNowPrivate});
  });
  
  // LocalStorage mein bhi save karo — instant
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_privacy_'+CU.uid, isNowPrivate ? '1' : '0');
  
  toast(isNowPrivate ? 'Profile Private ho gaya 🔒' : 'Profile Public ho gaya 🌐');
}

function applyPrivacyState(){
  const tgl=$('privacyTgl');
  const txt=$('privacyStatusTxt');
  if(!tgl) return;
  
  // LocalStorage se fast read
  const lsVal = CU ? localStorage.getItem('esv07_privacy_'+CU.uid) : null;
  const isPrivate = lsVal !== null ? lsVal === '1' : (GU.isPrivate||false);
  
  tgl.classList.toggle('on', isPrivate);
  if(txt) txt.textContent = isPrivate
    ? 'Private — Sirf aap dekh sakte hain'
    : 'Public — Sab dekh sakte hain';
}
/* ══ SELF LIKE ══ */
function selfLikeToggle(){
  if(!CU) return;
  const uid = CU.uid;
  DB.users().get(uid).get('likes').once(cur=>{
    const c = cur||0;
    if(_profileLiked.has('self_'+uid)){
      _profileLiked.delete('self_'+uid);
      DB.users().get(uid).get('likes').put(Math.max(0,c-1));
    } else {
      _profileLiked.add('self_'+uid);
      DB.users().get(uid).get('likes').put(c+1);
    }
    localStorage.setItem('esv07_plikes',JSON.stringify([..._profileLiked]));
  });
}

function watchMyLikes(){
  if(!CU) return;
  DB.users().get(CU.uid).get('likes').on(count=>{
    const el=$('myLikeCount');
    if(el) el.textContent = fmtL(count||0)+' likes';
  });
}
function shareMyProfile(){
  if(!CU) return;
  shareUserProfile(CU.uid, GU.name||'User');
}

  // Poora user object watch karo — sirf membership nahi
  
function _showVidSpinner() {
  let wrap = document.getElementById('vidSpinWrap');
  if (!wrap) {
    wrap = document.createElement('div');
    wrap.id = 'vidSpinWrap';
    wrap.className = 'vid-spinner-wrap';
    wrap.innerHTML = `
      <div class="vid-spin-ring"></div>
      <div class="vid-spin-txt">Video load ho raha hai...</div>
    `;
    const vpWrap = $('vpWrap');
    if (vpWrap) vpWrap.appendChild(wrap);
  }
  wrap.classList.remove('hide');
}

function _hideVidSpinner() {
  const wrap = document.getElementById('vidSpinWrap');
  if (wrap) wrap.classList.add('hide');
}

// ── Purane showVidLoader / showVidError ko override karo ──────────
function showVidLoader(show) {
  if (show) _showVidSpinner();
  else      _hideVidSpinner();
}

// showVidError — koi error text nahi, sirf spinner
function showVidError() {
  _showVidSpinner(); // Bas spinner ghoomta rahe
}

function retryVideo() {
  const ve = $('vidEl');
  _showVidSpinner();
  ve.load();
  ve.play().catch(() => {});
}
function openHowToUseVideo(){
  // GUN se how-to-use video load karo
  DB.settings().get('howToUseVideo').once(vData => {
    if(!vData || !vData.url){
      toast('Admin ne abhi How to Use video add nahi ki');
      return;
    }
    // vidSP mein open karo
    $('vidTitle').textContent = vData.title || 'How to Use';
    $('vidFull').textContent = vData.title || 'How to Use — Payment Guide';
    $('vidDesc').textContent = vData.desc || 'Payment kaise karein — step by step guide';
    openSP('vidSP');
    _showVidSpinner();
    
    const isYT = vData.url.includes('youtube.com') || vData.url.includes('youtu.be');
    const ve = $('vidEl');
    
    if(isYT){
      ve.style.display = 'none';
      const vpWrap = $('vpWrap');
      vpWrap.style.height = '56vw';
      vpWrap.style.maxHeight = '340px';
      
      let ytFrame = document.getElementById('ytPlayerFrame');
      if(ytFrame){ 
        try{ytFrame.src='about:blank';}catch(e){}
        try{ytFrame.parentNode.removeChild(ytFrame);}catch(e){}
      }
      ytFrame = document.createElement('iframe');
      ytFrame.id = 'ytPlayerFrame';
      ytFrame.allow = 'autoplay;encrypted-media;fullscreen';
      ytFrame.allowFullscreen = true;
      ytFrame.style.cssText = 'position:absolute;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;border:none;z-index:5;';
      ytFrame.onload = () => _hideVidSpinner();
      const m = vData.url.match(/(?:v=|youtu\.be\/)([a-zA-Z0-9_-]{11})/);
      ytFrame.src = `https://www.youtube.com/embed/${m?m[1]:''}?autoplay=1&rel=0&controls=1`;
      vpWrap.appendChild(ytFrame);
      $('vCtrl').style.display = 'none';
    } else {
      ve.style.display = 'block';
      ve.src = vData.url;
      ve.load();
      ve.oncanplay = () => { _hideVidSpinner(); ve.play().catch(()=>{}); };
      $('vCtrl').style.display = '';
    }

    // Neeche Terms dikhao — search box nahi
    const recSrchWrap = document.querySelector('#vidInfoSection > div:first-child');
    if(recSrchWrap) recSrchWrap.style.display = 'none';
    
    // Terms link dikhao
    let termsLink = document.getElementById('vidTermsLink');
    if(!termsLink){
      termsLink = document.createElement('div');
      termsLink.id = 'vidTermsLink';
      termsLink.style.cssText = 'text-align:center;padding:12px 0 4px;';
      termsLink.innerHTML = `<span onclick="openSP(\'termsSP\')" style="color:var(--p);font-size:13px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--fdisp);">
        <i class="fas fa-file-contract"></i> Terms and Conditions for EduSagar
      </span>`;
      const vidDesc = document.getElementById('vidDesc');
      if(vidDesc) vidDesc.after(termsLink);
    }
    termsLink.style.display = 'block';
    
    // Recommended videos section hide karo
    const recSection = document.querySelector('#vidInfoSection > div:last-child');
    // Keep it — sirf search box hide
  });
}
document.addEventListener('visibilitychange',()=>{
  if(document.hidden){
    clearInterval(window._carTimer);
  } else {
    clearInterval(window._carTimer);
    window._carTimer=setInterval(()=>carMove(1),12000);
  }
});

  if(!frame.src || frame.src === window.location.href || frame.src === 'about:blank' || frame.src === ''){
    frame.src = 'https://edustudents72.blogspot.com/';
  }
  openSP('sanuSP');
}

    frame.src = 'https://eduestudents.blogspot.com/';
