/* ══ HOME PYQ + BOOKS STREAM SWITCHER ══ */
let _homePBStream = 'science';

function switchHomePyqBook(stream, btn){
  document.querySelectorAll('#homePyqBookTabs .tbtn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');
  _homePBStream = stream;
  loadHomePYQ(stream);
  loadHomeBooks(stream);
}

function loadHomePYQ(stream){
  const el = $('homePyqList');
  if(!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:8px;">...</div>';
  const pyqs = {};
  DB.pyqs(stream).map().on((data, key)=>{
    if(data && data.title){ pyqs[key]={id:key,...data}; }
    else { delete pyqs[key]; }
    const list = Object.values(pyqs).slice(0,3);
    if(!list.length){ el.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.7);padding:8px;">Koi PYQ nahi abhi</div>'; return; }
    GU && GU.membership === 'active';
    el.innerHTML = list.map(p=>{
      const locked = p.locked && !hasMem;
      const clickFn = locked ? 'openMem()' : "openPDFViewer('"+p.title.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+"','"+((p.subject||'').replace(/'/g,"\\'"))+"','"+((p.pdfUrl||''))+"','"+((p.dlUrl||p.pdfUrl||''))+"')";
      return `<div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.15);border-radius:10px;padding:10px 12px;margin-bottom:7px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;cursor:pointer;" onclick="${clickFn}">
        <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'file-alt'}" style="color:#fff;font-size:16px;flex-shrink:0;"></i>
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
          <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:#fff;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">${esc(p.title)}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);">${esc(p.subject||'')} ${locked?'• Premium':''}</div>
        </div>
        <button onclick="event.stopPropagation();handleResDownload('${p.id}','pyq',${locked})" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);border:none;color:#fff;width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:50%;cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-shrink:0;">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'download'}"></i>
        </button>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  });
}

function loadHomeBooks(stream){
  const el = $('homeBooksListSec');
  if(!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:8px;"><div class="spin" style="width:18px;height:18px;border-width:2px;margin:0 auto;border-top-color:#fff;border-color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);"></div></div>';
  const books = {}; let hasData = false;
  DB.books(stream).map().on((data, key)=>{
    if(data && data.title){ books[key]={id:key,...data}; }
    else { delete books[key]; }
    const list = Object.values(books).slice(0,3);

    if(!list.length){ el.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.7);padding:8px;">Koi book nahi abhi</div>'; return; }
    GU && GU.membership === 'active'; 
    el.innerHTML = list.map(b=>{
      const locked = b.locked && !hasMem;
      const clickFn = locked ? 'openMem()' : "openPDFViewer('"+b.title.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+"','"+((b.subject||'').replace(/'/g,"\\'"))+"','"+((b.pdfUrl||''))+"','"+((b.dlUrl||b.pdfUrl||''))+"')";
      return `<div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.15);border-radius:10px;padding:10px 12px;margin-bottom:7px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;cursor:pointer;" onclick="${clickFn}">
        <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'book'}" style="color:#fff;font-size:16px;flex-shrink:0;"></i>
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
          <div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:#fff;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">${esc(b.title)}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);">${esc(b.subject||'')} ${locked?'• Premium':''}</div>
        </div>
        <button onclick="event.stopPropagation();handleResDownload('${b.id}','book',${locked})" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);border:none;color:#fff;width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:50%;cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-shrink:0;">
          <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'download'}"></i>
        </button>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  }, 1200);
}
/* ══ WITHDRAW SYSTEM ══ */
let _withdrawXHR = null;

function checkWithdrawBtn(){
  const btn = $('withdrawBtn');
  if(!btn || !CU) return;
  const earn = GU.earnings || 0;
  const lastReq = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('esv07_wdraw_'+CU.uid)||'0');
  const elapsed = Date.now() - lastReq;
  const cooldown = 24*60*60*1000;
  
  if(earn >= 100){
    btn.style.display = 'block';
    if(lastReq && elapsed < cooldown){
      btn.style.background = '#ef4444';
      btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-clock"></i> Sent';
      btn.onclick = null;
      btn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
    } else {
      btn.style.background = 'var(--g3)';
      btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-money-bill-wave"></i> Withdraw';
      btn.onclick = openWithdrawPopup;
      btn.style.cursor = 'pointer';
    }
  } else {
    btn.style.display = 'none';
  }
}

let _wdrawImgUrl = null;

function openWithdrawPopup(){
  if(!CU){ toast('Login karo pehle'); return; }
  const earn = GU.earnings || 0;
  if(earn < 100){ toast('₹100 se kam hai — withdraw nahi ho sakta'); return; }

  showAlert('fas fa-money-bill-wave','ok','Withdraw Request',
    'Apna QR Code aur details bhejo — Admin verify karega',
    [{l:'Send Request',c:'ca-primary',v:'open'},{l:'Cancel',c:'ca-ghost',v:'cancel'}]
  ).then(r=>{
    if(r.btn !== 'open') return;
    _openWithdrawSheet();
  });
}

function _openWithdrawSheet(){
  // Sheet banao
  let sheet = $('withdrawSheet');
  if(!sheet){
    sheet = document.createElement('div');
    sheet.id = 'withdrawSheet';
    sheet.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,.6);backdrop-filter:blur(5px);z-index:99999;display:flex;align-items:flex-end;justify-content:center;';
    sheet.innerHTML = `
      <div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:24px 24px 0 0;width:100%;max-width:520px;padding:22px 18px 36px;animation:slideUp .3s ease;" onclick="event.stopPropagation()">
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:16px;">
          <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:18px;font-weight:800;"><i class="fas fa-money-bill-wave" style="color:var(--ok);margin-right:8px;"></i>Withdraw ₹${GU.earnings||0}</div>
          <button onclick="closeWithdrawSheet()" style="background:var(--sur2);border:none;width:30px;height:30px;border-radius:50%;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;color:var(--txm);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>
        </div>

        <!-- QR Upload -->
        <div style="margin-bottom:13px;">
          <label style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txm);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;display:block;margin-bottom:5px;">QR Code Upload Karo</label>
          <input type="file" id="wdrawQrIn" accept="image/*" onchange="uploadWdrawQR(event)" style="display:none;">
          <div id="wdrawQrBtn" onclick="$('wdrawQrIn').click()" style="width:100%;padding:13px;border:2.5px dashed var(--bd);border-radius:14px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:10px;cursor:pointer;background:var(--sur2);">
            <i class="fas fa-qrcode" style="font-size:20px;color:var(--txm);"></i>
            <span style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:var(--txm);">QR Code Select Karo</span>
          </div>
          <div id="wdrawQrPreview" style="display:none;position:relative;border-radius:14px;overflow:hidden;border:2px solid var(--ok);margin-top:6px;">
            <img id="wdrawQrImg" style="width:100%;max-height:180px;object-fit:contain;display:block;" alt="">
            <button onclick="cancelWdrawQR()" style="position:absolute;top:8px;right:8px;width:26px;height:26px;border-radius:50%;background:rgba(239,68,68,.9);color:#fff;border:none;cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>
          </div>
          <div id="wdrawQrLoader" style="display:none;text-align:center;padding:10px;font-size:12px;color:var(--txm);"><div class="spin" style="width:20px;height:20px;border-width:2px;margin:0 auto 6px;"></div>Uploading...</div>
        </div>

        <!-- Mobile -->
        <div style="margin-bottom:13px;">
          <label style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txm);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;display:block;margin-bottom:5px;">Mobile Number</label>
          <input type="tel" id="wdrawMobile" class="finp" placeholder="10 digit mobile number" maxlength="10">
        </div>

        <!-- UPI ID -->
        <div style="margin-bottom:13px;">
          <label style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txm);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;display:block;margin-bottom:5px;">UPI ID</label>
          <input type="text" id="wdrawUpi" class="finp" placeholder="yourname@upi">
        </div>

        <!-- Description -->
        <div style="margin-bottom:16px;">
          <label style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--txm);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;display:block;margin-bottom:5px;">Description (Optional)</label>
          <input type="text" id="wdrawDesc" class="finp" placeholder="Kuch likhna ho toh...">
        </div>

        <button onclick="submitWithdrawRequest()" id="wdrawSendBtn" style="width:100%;padding:13px;border:none;border-radius:14px;background:var(--g3);color:#fff;font-size:14px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--font);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:9px;">
          <i class="fas fa-paper-plane"></i> Send to Admin
        </button>
        <p style="text-align:center;font-size:10px;color:var(--txm);margin-top:8px;">Admin verify karega — ₹${GU.earnings||0} aapke account mein bhejega</p>
      </div>
    `;
    sheet.onclick = (e)=>{ if(e.target===sheet) closeWithdrawSheet(); };
    document.body.appendChild(sheet);
  } else {
    sheet.style.display = 'flex';
  }
  _wdrawImgUrl = null;
}

function closeWithdrawSheet(){
  const s = $('withdrawSheet');
  if(s) s.style.display = 'none';
  _wdrawImgUrl = null;
}

function uploadWdrawQR(e){
  const file = e.target.files[0]; if(!file) return;
  $('wdrawQrBtn').style.display = 'none';
  $('wdrawQrLoader').style.display = 'block';
  $('wdrawQrPreview').style.display = 'none';
  
  const form = new FormData(); form.append('image', file);
  const xhr = new XMLHttpRequest(); _withdrawXHR = xhr;
  xhr.open('POST', `https://api.imgbb.com/1/upload?key=${IMGBB}`);
  xhr.onload = ()=>{
    _withdrawXHR = null;
    try{
      _wdrawImgUrl = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText).data.url;
      $('wdrawQrImg').src = _wdrawImgUrl;
      $('wdrawQrLoader').style.display = 'none';
      $('wdrawQrPreview').style.display = 'block';
      toast('QR ready ✅');
    } catch{ cancelWdrawQR(); toast('Upload fail — retry karo'); }
  };
  xhr.onerror = ()=>{ _withdrawXHR=null; cancelWdrawQR(); toast('Upload fail'); };
  xhr.send(form);
}

function cancelWdrawQR(){
  if(_withdrawXHR){ _withdrawXHR.abort(); _withdrawXHR=null; }
  _wdrawImgUrl = null;
  $('wdrawQrIn').value = '';
  $('wdrawQrBtn').style.display = 'flex';
  $('wdrawQrLoader').style.display = 'none';
  $('wdrawQrPreview').style.display = 'none';
}

function submitWithdrawRequest(){
  if(!CU) return;
  if(!_wdrawImgUrl){ toast('QR Code upload karo pehle 📸'); return; }
  const mobile = ($('wdrawMobile').value||'').trim();
  const upi = ($('wdrawUpi').value||'').trim();
  const desc = ($('wdrawDesc').value||'').trim();
  if(!mobile){ toast('Mobile number daalo'); return; }
  if(!upi){ toast('UPI ID daalo'); return; }

  const btn = $('wdrawSendBtn');
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Sending...';

  const reqId = 'wdraw_' + Date.now() + '_' + CU.uid.substring(0,6);
  
  // Admin chat mein bhejo
  const chatId = getChatId(CU.uid, ADMIN_UID);
  const msgId = 'wdmsg_' + Date.now();
  const msgText = `💰 WITHDRAW REQUEST\n━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n👤 Name: ${GU.name||'User'}\n📱 Mobile: ${mobile}\n💳 UPI: ${upi}\n💵 Amount: ₹${GU.earnings||0}\n📝 Desc: ${desc||'N/A'}\n━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\nReq ID: ${reqId}`;

  const payMsg={
    id:msgId,
    senderId:CU.uid,
    senderName:GU.name||'User',
    senderPhoto:GU.photo||DAV,
    text:msgText,
    img:ssImgUrl,
    seen:false,
    ts:Date.now(),
    isPayReq:true
  };
  DB.chats().get(chatId).get(msgId).put(payMsg);

  // ✅ Cache mein save karo — chat open hone par turant dikhega
  chatAllLoaded.add(msgId);
  chatMsgsList.push(payMsg);
  chatMsgsList.sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts);
  CACHE.set('msgs_'+CU.uid, chatMsgsList.slice(-100));

  // GUN mein withdraw request save karo
  gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('withdrawRequests').get(reqId).put({
    id: reqId,
    uid: CU.uid,
    name: GU.name||'User',
    photo: GU.photo||DAV,
    mobile, upi, desc,
    qrImg: _wdrawImgUrl,
    amount: GU.earnings||0,
    status: 'pending',
    ts: Date.now()
  });

  // Cooldown set karo
  localStorage.setItem('esv07_wdraw_'+CU.uid, Date.now());

  // Button red karo
  const wBtn = $('withdrawBtn');
  if(wBtn){
    wBtn.style.background = '#ef4444';
    wBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-clock"></i> Sent';
    wBtn.onclick = null;
    wBtn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
  }

  closeWithdrawSheet();
  toast('Withdraw request send ho gayi! Admin verify karega ✅');

  // Admin chat kholo
  setTimeout(()=> openAdminChat(), 500);
}

/* ══ ADMIN WITHDRAW ACCEPT — Admin ke liye ══ */
// Admin ke chat mein "Yes Accept" button dikhega
// Yeh renderBubble mein handle hoga
function adminAcceptWithdraw(reqId, uid, amount){
  if(!GU || !GU.isAdmin){ toast('Admin only!'); return; }
  caConfirm('Accept Withdraw?', `₹${amount} is user se minus karein?`, 'Yes Accept').then(r=>{
    if(r.btn !== 'yes') return;
    // User ki earnings minus karo
    DB.users().get(uid).once(data=>{
      if(!data) return;
      const newEarn = Math.max(0, (data.earnings||0) - amount);
      DB.users().get(uid).put({...data, earnings: newEarn});
      // Request complete mark karo
      gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('withdrawRequests').get(reqId).get('status').put('done');
      toast(`✅ ₹${amount} minus ho gaya! User ko payment karo.`);
    });
  });
}

function openSubjectContentPage(subjectId, subjectName, icon){
  $('customPageTitle').textContent = subjectName;
  const body = $('customPageBody');
  body.innerHTML = `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;height:200px;"><div class="spin" style="width:32px;height:32px;border-width:3px;"></div></div>`;
  openSP('customPageSP');

  const DB_SUBJ = () => gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('subjectContent').get(activeStream).get(subjectId);
  const items = {};

  DB_SUBJ().get('items').map().on((data, key) => {
    if(data && data.name) items[key] = {id:key,...data};
  });

  setTimeout(() => {
    const list = Object.values(items).sort((a,b)=>(a.order||0)-(b.order||0));
    renderSubjectContentPage(body, list, subjectId, subjectName);
  }, 1200);
}

function renderSubjectContentPage(body, items, subjectId, subjectName){
  GU && GU.membership === 'active';
  
  // Chapters aur Sets alag karo
  const chapters = items.filter(i => i.type === 'chapter');
  const setGroups = items.filter(i => i.type === 'set');

  let html = `
    <div style="padding:14px;">
      <!-- Header -->
      <div style="background:var(--g1);border-radius:var(--r);padding:16px 18px;margin-bottom:16px;color:#fff;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:13px;">
        <div style="width:46px;height:46px;border-radius:13px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:22px;flex-shrink:0;">
          <i class="${icon||'fas fa-book'}"></i>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:17px;font-weight:800;">+2 Second Year</div>
          <div style="font-size:12px;opacity:.85;margin-top:2px;">${esc(subjectName)}</div>
        </div>
        <!-- List/Grid toggle -->
        <div style="margin-left:auto;display:flex;gap:6px;">
          <button id="viewToggleBtn" onclick="toggleContentView()" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);border:none;color:#fff;width:34px;height:34px;border-radius:50%;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:14px;">
            <i class="fas fa-th-large" id="viewToggleIc"></i>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>`;

  if(!items.length){
    html += `<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-inbox"></i><p>Admin ne abhi content add nahi kiya</p></div>`;
  } else {
    // Chapters section
    if(chapters.length){
      html += `<div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:15px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:11px;"><i class="fas fa-book-open" style="color:var(--p);margin-right:7px;"></i>Chapters</div>`;
      html += `<div id="chaptersList" style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px;margin-bottom:18px;">`;
      chapters.forEach(ch => {
        const locked = ch.isPaid && !hasMem;
        html += `
          <div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r2);border:1.5px solid ${locked?'var(--bd)':'var(--bds)'};padding:14px;position:relative;cursor:pointer;transition:all .22s;"
            onclick="${locked?'openMem()':'openChapterPage(\''+ch.id+'\',\''+esc(ch.name)+'\',\''+subjectId+'\')'}"
            onmouseover="this.style.transform='translateY(-2px)';this.style.boxShadow='0 6px 20px rgba(79,70,229,.15)'"
            onmouseout="this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow=''">
            <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:8px;">
              <span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;background:${locked?'rgba(239,68,68,.1)':'rgba(16,185,129,.1)'};color:${locked?'var(--err)':'var(--ok)'};">
                <i class="fas fa-${locked?'lock':'unlock'}"></i> ${locked?'Premium':'Free'}
              </span>
            </div>
            <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx);line-height:1.4;margin-bottom:10px;">${esc(ch.name)}</div>
            ${locked?'':
              `<div style="display:flex;gap:5px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
                <span style="font-size:9px;background:var(--plight);color:var(--p);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">MCQ</span>
                ${ch.has2mark?'<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(249,115,22,.1);color:#f97316;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">2 Mark</span>':''}
                ${ch.has3mark?'<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(245,158,11,.1);color:var(--warn);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">3 Mark</span>':''}
                ${ch.hasLong?'<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(239,68,68,.1);color:var(--err);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">Long Q</span>':''}
              </div>`
            }
          </div>`;
      });
      html += `</div>`;
    }

    // Sets section
    if(setGroups.length){
      html += `<div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:15px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:11px;"><i class="fas fa-tasks" style="color:var(--ok);margin-right:7px;"></i>Practice Sets</div>`;
      html += `<div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);padding:16px;margin-bottom:14px;">`;
      html += `<div id="setsList" style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:8px;">`;
      setGroups.forEach(s => {
        const locked = s.isPaid && !hasMem;
        html += `
          <div style="background:${locked?'var(--sur2)':'var(--plight)'};border:1.5px solid ${locked?'var(--bd)':'var(--bds)'};border-radius:10px;padding:12px 8px;text-align:center;cursor:pointer;transition:all .2s;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:${locked?'var(--txm)':'var(--p)'};"
            onclick="${locked?'openMem()':'openChapterPage(\''+s.id+'\',\''+esc(s.name)+'\',\''+subjectId+'\')'}"
            onmouseover="this.style.background='var(--p)';this.style.color='#fff'"
            onmouseout="this.style.background='${locked?'var(--sur2)':'var(--plight)'}';this.style.color='${locked?'var(--txm)':'var(--p)'}'">
            ${locked?'<i class="fas fa-lock" style="display:block;margin-bottom:4px;font-size:14px;"></i>':''}
            ${esc(s.name)}
          </div>`;
      });
      html += `</div></div>`;
    }
  }

  html += `</div>`;
  body.innerHTML = html;
  
  // View toggle state
  window._contentViewGrid = true;
}

// List/Grid toggle
function toggleContentView(){
  window._contentViewGrid = !window._contentViewGrid;
  const chapList = document.getElementById('chaptersList');
  const setList = document.getElementById('setsList');
  const ic = document.getElementById('viewToggleIc');
  
  if(chapList){
    chapList.style.gridTemplateColumns = window._contentViewGrid ? '1fr 1fr' : '1fr';
  }
  if(setList){
    setList.style.gridTemplateColumns = window._contentViewGrid ? '1fr 1fr' : '1fr';
    if(!window._contentViewGrid){
      // List view mein sets full width
      setList.querySelectorAll('div').forEach((el,i,arr) => {
        if(arr.length % 2 !== 0 && i === arr.length-1){
          el.style.gridColumn = '1/-1';
        }
      });
    }
  }
  if(ic) ic.className = window._contentViewGrid ? 'fas fa-th-large' : 'fas fa-list';
}

// Chapter/Set content page
function openChapterPage(chapterId, chapterName, subjectId){
  // customSubPageSP use karo
  $('customSubPageTitle').textContent = chapterName;
  const body = $('customSubPageBody');
  body.innerHTML = `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;height:200px;"><div class="spin" style="width:32px;height:32px;border-width:3px;"></div></div>`;
  openSP('customSubPageSP');

  const DB_CH = () => gun.get('edu_sagar_v07').get('subjectContent').get(activeStream).get(subjectId).get('items').get(chapterId);
  
  DB_CH().get('mcq').once(mcqData => {
    DB_CH().get('content').once(contentData => {
      renderChapterContentPage(body, chapterId, chapterName, mcqData, contentData);
    });
  });
}

function renderChapterContentPage(body, chapterId, chapterName, mcqData, contentData){
  const mcqs = mcqData ? Object.values(mcqData).filter(x=>x&&x.q) : [];
  const sections = contentData ? contentData : {};

  let html = `<div style="padding:14px;">`;

  // MCQ Section
  if(mcqs.length){
    html += `
      <div style="margin-bottom:18px;">
        <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:15px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:12px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;">
          <span><i class="fas fa-pen" style="color:var(--p);margin-right:7px;"></i>MCQ Questions</span>
          <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;">
            <button onclick="toggleMcqView()" style="background:var(--plight);color:var(--p);border:none;border-radius:8px;padding:5px 10px;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;">
              <i class="fas fa-th-large" id="mcqViewIc"></i>
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="mcqContainer">
          ${renderMCQs(mcqs)}
        </div>
        <button id="resultBtn" onclick="showMCQResult()" style="width:100%;padding:12px;border:none;border-radius:12px;background:var(--g1);color:#fff;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;margin-top:12px;display:none;">
          <i class="fas fa-chart-bar"></i> View Results
        </button>
      </div>`;
  }

  // 2 Mark Section
  if(sections.mark2){
    html += `
      <div style="margin-bottom:14px;">
        <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:14px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;color:var(--tx);">
          <i class="fas fa-star" style="color:#f97316;margin-right:6px;"></i>2 Mark Questions
        </div>
        ${renderPDFCards(sections.mark2, '2mark')}
      </div>`;
  }

  // 3 Mark Section
  if(sections.mark3){
    html += `
      <div style="margin-bottom:14px;">
        <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:14px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;color:var(--tx);">
          <i class="fas fa-star" style="color:var(--warn);margin-right:6px;"></i>3 Mark Questions
        </div>
        ${renderPDFCards(sections.mark3, '3mark')}
      </div>`;
  }

  // Long Questions Section
  if(sections.longQ){
    html += `
      <div style="margin-bottom:14px;">
        <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:14px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;color:var(--tx);">
          <i class="fas fa-fire" style="color:var(--err);margin-right:6px;"></i>Long Questions
        </div>
        ${renderPDFCards(sections.longQ, 'longq')}
      </div>`;
  }

  if(!mcqs.length && !sections.mark2 && !sections.mark3 && !sections.longQ){
    html += `<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-inbox"></i><p>Content abhi available nahi</p></div>`;
  }

  html += `</div>`;
  body.innerHTML = html;

  // MCQ answers track karo
  window._mcqAnswers = {};
  window._mcqTotal = mcqs.length;
  window._mcqData = mcqs;
  checkResultBtn();
}

function renderMCQs(mcqs){
  if(!mcqs.length) return '';
  return mcqs.map((q, idx) => `
    <div id="mcq_${idx}" style="background:var(--sur);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);border-radius:var(--r2);padding:14px;margin-bottom:10px;">
      <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;line-height:1.6;">
        ${idx+1}. ${esc(q.q||'')}
      </div>
      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px;" id="opts_${idx}">
        ${(q.opts||[]).map((opt,oi) => `
          <div onclick="selectMCQ(${idx},${oi},'${q.ans||0}')" id="opt_${idx}_${oi}"
            style="padding:9px 13px;border:1.5px solid var(--bd);border-radius:9px;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .2s;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:9px;">
            <span style="width:22px;height:22px;border-radius:50%;border:1.5px solid var(--bd);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;flex-shrink:0;">${String.fromCharCode(2805+oi)}</span>
            ${esc(opt)}
          </div>
        `).join('')}
      </div>
      <div id="exp_${idx}" style="display:none;background:var(--sur3);border-radius:9px;padding:10px 12px;margin-top:9px;font-size:11px;color:var(--txm);line-height:1.6;">
        <i class="fas fa-lightbulb" style="color:var(--warn);margin-right:5px;"></i>${esc(q.exp||'')}
      </div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function selectMCQ(qIdx, optIdx, correctAns){
  if(window._mcqAnswers && window._mcqAnswers[qIdx] !== undefined) return; // Already answered
  
  window._mcqAnswers[qIdx] = optIdx;
  const correctIdx = parseInt(correctAns);
  const isCorrect = optIdx === correctIdx;
  
  // Color options
  const optsEl = document.getElementById('opts_'+qIdx);
  if(!optsEl) return;
  optsEl.querySelectorAll('[id^="opt_'+qIdx+'_"]').forEach((el, oi) => {
    el.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
    if(oi === correctIdx){
      el.style.borderColor = 'var(--ok)';
      el.style.background = 'rgba(16,185,129,.12)';
      el.style.color = 'var(--ok)';
    } else if(oi === optIdx && !isCorrect){
      el.style.borderColor = 'var(--err)';
      el.style.background = 'rgba(239,68,68,.1)';
      el.style.color = 'var(--err)';
    }
  });
  
  // Show explanation
  const expEl = document.getElementById('exp_'+qIdx);
  if(expEl) expEl.style.display = 'block';
  
  checkResultBtn();
}

function checkResultBtn(){
  const btn = document.getElementById('resultBtn');
  if(!btn) return;
  const answered = Object.keys(window._mcqAnswers||{}).length;
  const total = window._mcqTotal || 0;
  btn.style.display = total > 0 ? 'block' : 'none';
  if(answered < total){
    btn.style.opacity = '0.5';
    btn.innerHTML = `<i class="fas fa-chart-bar"></i> View Results (${answered}/${total} answered)`;
  } else {
    btn.style.opacity = '1';
    btn.innerHTML = `<i class="fas fa-chart-bar"></i> View Results ✅`;
  }
}

function showMCQResult(){
  const answers = window._mcqAnswers || {};
  const mcqs = window._mcqData || [];
  const total = mcqs.length;
  const answered = Object.keys(answers).length;
  
  // Unanswered questions pe scroll karo
  if(answered < total){
    for(let i=0; i<total; i++){
      if(answers[i] === undefined){
        const el = document.getElementById('mcq_'+i);
        if(el){ el.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'}); break; }
      }
    }
    toast('Pehle sab questions answer karo!');
    return;
  }
  
  // Score calculate
  let correct = 0;
  mcqs.forEach((q, idx) => {
    if(parseInt(answers[idx]) === parseInt(q.ans||0)) correct++;
  });
  const wrong = total - correct;
  const pct = Math.round((correct/total)*100);
  
  // Result popup
  const existing = document.getElementById('resultPopup');
  if(existing) existing.remove();
  
  const popup = document.createElement('div');
  popup.id = 'resultPopup';
  popup.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,.7);backdrop-filter:blur(6px);z-index:9999999;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;padding:20px;';
  popup.innerHTML = `
    <div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:24px;padding:28px 22px;width:100%;max-width:320px;text-align:center;animation:caAnim .25s ease;">
      <div style="width:70px;height:70px;border-radius:50%;background:${pct>=60?'rgba(16,185,129,.15)':'rgba(239,68,68,.12)'};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;margin:0 auto 14px;">
        <i class="fas fa-${pct>=60?'trophy':'redo'}" style="font-size:28px;color:${pct>=60?'var(--ok)':'var(--err)'};"></i>
      </div>
      <div style="font-family:var(--fdisp);font-size:22px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:4px;">${pct}%</div>
      <div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--txm);margin-bottom:18px;">${pct>=60?'Bahut Badhiya! 🎉':'Aur Practice Karo 💪'}</div>
      <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;margin-bottom:20px;">
        <div style="flex:1;background:rgba(16,185,129,.1);border-radius:12px;padding:12px;">
          <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:800;color:var(--ok);">${correct}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txm);">Correct ✅</div>
        </div>
        <div style="flex:1;background:rgba(239,68,68,.08);border-radius:12px;padding:12px;">
          <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:800;color:var(--err);">${wrong}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txm);">Wrong ❌</div>
        </div>
        <div style="flex:1;background:var(--plight);border-radius:12px;padding:12px;">
          <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:800;color:var(--p);">${total}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txm);">Total</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <button onclick="document.getElementById('resultPopup').remove()" style="width:100%;padding:12px;border:none;border-radius:12px;background:var(--g1);color:#fff;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:var(--font);">
        <i class="fas fa-check"></i> Done
      </button>
    </div>
  `;
  document.body.appendChild(popup);
  popup.addEventListener('click', e => { if(e.target===popup) popup.remove(); });
}

function renderPDFCards(pdfs, type){
  if(!pdfs || !Object.keys(pdfs).length) return '<div class="empty"><i class="fas fa-inbox"></i><p>PDF abhi available nahi</p></div>';
  return Object.values(pdfs).map(pdf => `
    <div onclick="openPDFViewer('${esc(pdf.title||'')}','${type}','${pdf.url||''}','${pdf.url||''}')"
      style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r2);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);padding:13px;margin-bottom:8px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .22s;"
      onmouseover="this.style.transform='translateY(-2px)';this.style.boxShadow='0 6px 20px rgba(79,70,229,.12)'"
      onmouseout="this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow=''">
      <div style="width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:11px;background:var(--g2);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px;color:#fff;flex-shrink:0;">
        <i class="fas fa-file-pdf"></i>
      </div>
      <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
        <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">${esc(pdf.title||'PDF')}</div>
        <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txm);margin-top:2px;">${pdf.total||''} Questions</div>
      </div>
      <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="color:var(--txm);font-size:12px;flex-shrink:0;"></i>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function toggleMcqView(){
  window._mcqListView = !window._mcqListView;
  const container = document.getElementById('mcqContainer');
  const ic = document.getElementById('mcqViewIc');
  if(!container) return;
  if(window._mcqListView){
    container.style.display = 'flex';
    container.style.flexDirection = 'column';
    if(ic) ic.className = 'fas fa-list';
  } else {
    container.style.display = 'block';
    if(ic) ic.className = 'fas fa-th-large';
  }
}
/* ══════════════════════════════════════
   SUBJECT DYNAMIC PAGE SYSTEM
   GUN realtime + localStorage cache
══════════════════════════════════════ */

const SUBJ_CACHE_PREFIX = 'esv07_subj_';

// Subject page open karo
function openSubjectDynamicPage(subjectId, subjectName, icon){
  $('customPageTitle').textContent = subjectName;
  openSP('customPageSP');
  const body = $('customPageBody');

  // Cache se turant dikha
  const cached = loadSubjCache(subjectId);
  if(cached && cached.items){
    renderSubjPage(body, cached.items, subjectId, subjectName, icon);
  } else {
    body.innerHTML = _subjLoader();
  }

  // GUN se live sync
  _watchSubjItems(subjectId, subjectName, icon, body);
}

// GUN watcher — realtime
let _subjWatchers = {};
function _watchSubjItems(subjectId, subjectName, icon, body){
  // Purana watcher band karo
  if(_subjWatchers[subjectId]){
    try{ _subjWatchers[subjectId](); }catch(e){}
  }

  const items = {};

  const off = gun.get('edu_sagar_v07')
    .get('subjPages')
    .get(activeStream)
    .get(subjectId)
    .get('items')
    .map()
    .on((data, key) => {
      if(!data || data._deleted){
        delete items[key];
      } else {
        items[key] = { id: key, ...data };
      }
      const list = Object.values(items)
        .filter(x => x && x.name)
        .sort((a,b) => (a.order||0) - (b.order||0));
      
      // Cache save
      saveSubjCache(subjectId, { items: list, ts: Date.now() });
      
      // Render
      renderSubjPage(body, list, subjectId, subjectName, icon);
    });

  _subjWatchers[subjectId] = off;
}

// Render subject page
function renderSubjPage(body, items, subjectId, subjectName, icon){
  GU && GU.membership === 'active';
  const chapters = items.filter(i => i.type === 'chapter');
  const setCards = items.filter(i => i.type === 'set');

  let html = `
  <div style="padding:12px 13px 40px;">

    <!-- HEADER -->
    <div style="background:var(--g1);border-radius:var(--r);padding:16px 18px;margin-bottom:16px;color:#fff;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:13px;position:relative;overflow:hidden;">
      <div style="position:absolute;top:-20px;right:-20px;width:80px;height:80px;border-radius:50%;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);"></div>
      <div style="width:46px;height:46px;border-radius:13px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.2);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:22px;flex-shrink:0;position:relative;z-index:1;">
        <i class="${icon||'fas fa-book'}"></i>
      </div>
      <div style="position:relative;z-index:1;">
        <div style="font-size:10px;opacity:.8;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:1px;text-transform:uppercase;">+2 Second Year Arts/Science/Commerce</div>
        <div style="font-family:'Baloo 2',cursive;font-size:18px;font-weight:800;margin-top:2px;">${esc(subjectName)}</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    ${!items.length ? `
      <div style="text-align:center;padding:50px 20px;color:var(--txm);">
        <i class="fas fa-inbox" style="font-size:36px;display:block;margin-bottom:12px;opacity:.3;"></i>
        <p style="font-size:13px;">Admin ne abhi content add nahi kiya</p>
      </div>
    ` : ''}

    ${chapters.length ? _renderChapters(chapters, hasMem, subjectId) : ''}
    ${setCards.length ? _renderSets(setCards, hasMem, subjectId) : ''}

    <!-- COPYRIGHT -->
    <div style="text-align:center;padding:24px 0 8px;color:var(--txl);font-size:10px;">
      <i class="fas fa-copyright" style="font-size:9px;margin-right:3px;"></i> 2026 EduSagar. All rights reserved.
    </div>

  </div>`;

  body.innerHTML = html;
}

// Chapters render
function _renderChapters(chapters, hasMem, subjectId){
  return `
  <div style="margin-bottom:18px;">
    <div style="font-family:'Baloo 2',cursive;font-size:16px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:12px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;">
      <i class="fas fa-book-open" style="color:var(--p);font-size:14px;"></i> Chapters
    </div>
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px;">
      ${chapters.map((ch, idx) => {
        const locked = ch.isPaid && !hasMem;
        const isOdd = chapters.length % 2 !== 0 && idx === chapters.length - 1;
        return `
        <div onclick="${locked ? 'openMem()' : `openChapterContentPage('${ch.id}','${esc(ch.name)}','${subjectId}')`}"
          style="
            background:var(--sur);
            border:1.5px solid ${locked ? 'var(--bd)' : 'var(--bds)'};
            border-radius:var(--r2);
            padding:14px 12px;
            cursor:pointer;
            transition:all .22s;
            position:relative;
            overflow:hidden;
            ${isOdd ? 'grid-column:1/-1;' : ''}
          "
          onmouseover="this.style.transform='translateY(-2px)';this.style.boxShadow='0 6px 20px rgba(79,70,229,.13)'"
          onmouseout="this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow=''">
          
          <!-- Lock badge -->
          <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:8px;">
            <span style="
              font-size:9px;font-weight:700;
              padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;
              background:${locked ? 'rgba(239,68,68,.1)' : 'rgba(16,185,129,.12)'};
              color:${locked ? 'var(--err)' : 'var(--ok)'};
              display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">
              <i class="fas fa-${locked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'}"></i>
              ${locked ? 'Premium' : 'Free'}
            </span>
            ${locked ? '' : `
              <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txl);"></i>
            `}
          </div>

          <!-- Chapter name -->
          <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:var(--tx);line-height:1.45;margin-bottom:10px;">
            ${esc(ch.name)}
          </div>

          <!-- Content tags -->
          <div style="display:flex;gap:4px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
            <span style="font-size:9px;background:var(--plight);color:var(--p);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">
              <i class="fas fa-pen" style="font-size:8px;"></i> MCQ
            </span>
            ${ch.has2mark ? `<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(249,115,22,.1);color:#f97316;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">2 Mark</span>` : ''}
            ${ch.has3mark ? `<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(245,158,11,.1);color:var(--warn);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">3 Mark</span>` : ''}
            ${ch.hasLong ? `<span style="font-size:9px;background:rgba(239,68,68,.1);color:var(--err);padding:2px 7px;border-radius:6px;font-weight:700;">Long Q</span>` : ''}
          </div>

          ${locked ? `
            <div style="position:absolute;inset:0;background:rgba(15,13,46,.04);border-radius:var(--r2);"></div>
          ` : ''}
        </div>`;
      }).join('')}
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

// Sets render
function _renderSets(setCards, hasMem, subjectId){
  return setCards.map(sc => {
    const locked = sc.isPaid && !hasMem;
    // Sets ke andar jo sets hain
    const sets = sc.sets ? Object.values(sc.sets).sort((a,b)=>(a.order||0)-(b.order||0)) : [];

    // Odd-even grid logic
    let setsHtml = '';
    sets.forEach((s, idx) => {
      const isLast = idx === sets.length - 1;
      const isOdd = sets.length % 2 !== 0 && isLast;
      const sLocked = (s.isPaid && !hasMem) || locked;
      setsHtml += `
        <div onclick="${sLocked ? 'openMem()' : `openChapterContentPage('${s.id}','${esc(s.name)}','${subjectId}')`}"
          style="
            background:${sLocked ? 'var(--sur2)' : 'var(--plight)'};
            border:1.5px solid ${sLocked ? 'var(--bd)' : 'var(--bds)'};
            border-radius:10px;padding:12px 8px;text-align:center;
            cursor:pointer;transition:all .2s;
            font-size:12px;font-weight:700;
            color:${sLocked ? 'var(--txm)' : 'var(--p)'};
            ${isOdd ? 'grid-column:1/-1;' : ''}
          "
          onmouseover="if(!${sLocked}){this.style.background='var(--p)';this.style.color='#fff';}"
          onmouseout="this.style.background='${sLocked ? 'var(--sur2)' : 'var(--plight)'}';this.style.color='${sLocked ? 'var(--txm)' : 'var(--p)'}';this.style.transform='';this.style.boxShadow='';">
          ${sLocked ? '<i class="fas fa-lock" style="display:block;margin-bottom:4px;font-size:13px;opacity:.5;"></i>' : ''}
          ${esc(s.name)}
        </div>`;
    });

    return `
    <div style="background:var(--sur);border-radius:var(--r);border:1.5px solid var(--bd);padding:16px;margin-bottom:14px;position:relative;overflow:hidden;">
      
      ${locked ? `
        <div style="position:absolute;inset:0;background:rgba(15,13,46,.55);border-radius:var(--r);display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:8px;z-index:5;backdrop-filter:blur(2px);">
          <i class="fas fa-lock" style="font-size:22px;color:#fff;"></i>
          <p style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);">Premium members only</p>
          <button onclick="openMem()" style="background:#fbbf24;color:#78350f;border:none;border-radius:20px;padding:7px 18px;font-size:11px;font-weight:800;cursor:pointer;">Unlock Now</button>
        </div>
      ` : ''}

      <div style="font-family:'Baloo 2',cursive;font-size:15px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:14px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;">
        <i class="fas fa-tasks" style="color:var(--ok);font-size:13px;"></i>
        ${esc(sc.name || 'Practice Sets')}
      </div>

      <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:8px;">
        ${setsHtml || `<div style="grid-column:1/-1;text-align:center;padding:16px;color:var(--txm);font-size:12px;">Koi set nahi abhi</div>`}
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

      <div style="background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;border-radius:var(--r2);height:100px;"></div>
      <div style="background:linear-gradient(90deg,var(--bd) 25%,var(--sur3) 50%,var(--bd) 75%);background-size:200% 100%;animation:skelA 1.6s infinite;border-radius:var(--r2);height:100px;"></div>

// LocalStorage cache
function saveSubjCache(subjId, data){
  try{ localStorage.setItem(SUBJ_CACHE_PREFIX + subjId, JSON.stringify(data)); }catch(e){}
}
function loadSubjCache(subjId){
  try{ return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(SUBJ_CACHE_PREFIX + subjId) || 'null'); }catch{ return null; }
}

// Chapter content page (MCQ + PDFs) — baad mein banayenge
function openChapterContentPage(chId, chName, subjId){
  toast(chName + ' — Content loading... 📖');
}
function _renderMembershipBadge(memData){
  if(!memData || memData.status !== 'active') return `<div class="mem-circle" style="border:2px solid var(--bd);background:var(--sur2);">👤</div>`;
  
  const plan = memData.plan || 'batch';
  const stream = memData.stream || '';
  const labels = { batch:'Batch', pro:'Pro', infinity:'Infinity ♾️' };
  
  return `
    <div class="mem-circle ${plan}">
      <span>${_streamIcon(stream)}</span>
      <span class="mem-badge-label">${labels[plan]}</span>
    </div>
    <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;margin-top:10px;">${stream} — ${labels[plan]}</div>`;
}
// ══ LOGIN PROMPT ══
let _loginPromptAction = null;

function showLoginPrompt(msg, afterLoginFn) {
  _loginPromptAction = afterLoginFn || null;
  document.getElementById('loginPromptMsg').textContent = msg || 'Yeh feature use karne ke liye pehle login karo.';
  document.getElementById('loginPromptOv').classList.add('open');
}

function closeLoginPrompt() {
  document.getElementById('loginPromptOv').classList.remove('open');
  _loginPromptAction = null;
}

function loginPromptGo() {
  closeLoginPrompt();
  const provider = new firebase.auth.GoogleAuthProvider();
  provider.addScope('email');
  provider.addScope('profile');
  auth.signInWithPopup(provider).then(() => {
    // Login ke baad original action chalao
    if (_loginPromptAction) {
      setTimeout(() => { _loginPromptAction(); }, 800);
    }
  }).catch(err => {
    if (err.code === 'auth/popup-blocked') toast('Popup block hai — Browser mein allow karo');
    else if (err.code === 'auth/popup-closed-by-user') toast('Login cancel ho gaya');
    else toast('Login fail: ' + (err.message || 'Try again'));
  });
}
function showLoginPopup() {
    const popup = document.getElementById('loginPopup');
    if(popup) {
        popup.style.display = 'flex';
    }
}

function redirectToLogin() {
    // Yahan apne login page ka sahi URL dalein
    window.location.href = 'login.html'; 
}


</script>
</body>
</html>
